--- FILE: Badger\Badger\Models\HEA.cs ---
namespace Badger.Models
{
    public class HEA
    {
        public string server = CommonInterfaces.Constants.Database.SQL_SERVER;

        #region Properties
        public string assetId { get; set; }
        public string maxId { get; set; }
        public int lienPosition { get; set; }
        public string assetStatus { get; set; }
        string name_simple { get; set; }
        string address_full { get; set; }
        public string bankruptcyInfo { get; set; }
        public string uw_issue { get; set; }
        public Boolean hasREO { get; set; }

        #endregion

        #region Constructors
        public HEA()
        {
            assetId = "";
            maxId = "";
        }

        #endregion

        #region Methods 
        public void SetAssetId(string assetId)
        {
            this.assetId = assetId;
        }
        public string GetAssetId()
        {
            return assetId;
        }

        public string GetAssetNiceName()
        {
            string statusDisplay = !string.IsNullOrEmpty(uw_issue) ? uw_issue : assetStatus;
            string title = $"{assetId} - {name_simple} | {address_full}    [{statusDisplay}]";
            
            if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(bankruptcyInfo))
            {
                title += $"  [{bankruptcyInfo}]";
            }

            if (hasREO)
            {
                title += "  [REO]";
            }

            return title;
        }

        public bool LoadAsset(string asset_id)
        {
            
            this.assetId = asset_id;
            var assetDetails = BadgerLib.Assets.GetAllAttributes<string>(this.server, asset_id);

            if (assetDetails == null || assetDetails.Count == 0)
            {
                return false;
            }

            
            this.maxId = assetDetails["max_id"];
            this.assetId = assetDetails["asset_id"];
            this.lienPosition = assetDetails["lien_position"].AsInt().Value;
            this.assetStatus = assetDetails["asset_status"];
            this.name_simple = assetDetails["name_simple"];
            this.address_full = assetDetails["address_full"];
            this.uw_issue = assetDetails["uw_issue"];

            this.bankruptcyInfo = BadgerLib.Defaults.GetBankruptcyInfo(this.server, asset_id);
            this.hasREO = BadgerLib.Defaults.GetREOInfo(this.server, asset_id);

            return true;
        }

        #endregion
    }
}

[assembly: log4net.Config.XmlConfigurator(ConfigFile = "log4net.config", Watch = true)]

namespace Badger
{
    static partial class Program
    {
        private static readonly ILog log = LogManager.GetLogger(typeof(Program));
        [STAThread]
        static void Main()
        {
            
            if (SquirrelAwareHandler.HandleSquirrelEvents())
                return;

#if (DEBUG == false)
            
            {
                AppDomain.CurrentDomain.UnhandledException += new UnhandledExceptionEventHandler(CurrentDomain_UnhandledException);
            }
#endif

            XmlConfigurator.Configure();
            log.Error("Error logging is now enabled.");
            
            WindowsFormsSettings.UseDXDialogs = DevExpress.Utils.DefaultBoolean.True;
            WindowsFormsSettings.AllowRoundedWindowCorners = DevExpress.Utils.DefaultBoolean.True; ;
            System.Reflection.Assembly asm = typeof(DevExpress.UserSkins.WinterJoy).Assembly;
            DevExpress.Skins.SkinManager.Default.RegisterAssembly(asm);
            SkinManager.EnableFormSkins();
            Application.EnableVisualStyles();
            BonusSkins.Register();
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            

            
            Application.Run(new mainForm());

        }



        private static void CurrentDomain_UnhandledException(Object sender, UnhandledExceptionEventArgs e)
         {

            try
            {
                Exception n = (Exception)e.ExceptionObject;
                XtraMessageBox.Show("Error Report Has Been Sent", "Uh oh...", MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Error);

                UtilsLib.Error.SendDefaultError(n);
            }
            catch (Exception n)
            {
                XtraMessageBox.Show("Error Report Has NOT Been Sent", "Uh oh...", MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Error);
            }
        }

  

        public static void NGEN()
        {
            if (ApplicationDeployment.IsNetworkDeployed && ApplicationDeployment.CurrentDeployment.IsFirstRun)
            {

                string appPath = Application.StartupPath;
                string winPath = Environment.GetEnvironmentVariable("WINDIR");

                Process proc = new Process();
                System.IO.Directory.SetCurrentDirectory(appPath);

                proc.EnableRaisingEvents = false;
                proc.StartInfo.CreateNoWindow = false;
                proc.StartInfo.WindowStyle = ProcessWindowStyle.Hidden;

                proc.StartInfo.FileName = winPath + @"\Microsoft.NET\Framework\v2.0.50727\ngen.exe";
                proc.StartInfo.Arguments = "uninstall " + Application.ProductName + " /nologo /silent";

                proc.Start();
                proc.WaitForExit();

                proc.StartInfo.FileName = winPath + @"\Microsoft.NET\Framework\v2.0.50727\ngen.exe";
                proc.StartInfo.Arguments = "install " + Application.ProductName + " /nologo /silent";

                proc.Start();
                proc.WaitForExit();

            }
        }
    }
}

        private void mainTabControl_SelectedPageChanged(object sender, DevExpress.XtraBars.Navigation.SelectedPageChangedEventArgs e)
        {
            RefreshActiveTab(null, false);
        }

        private void mainForm_KeyUp(object sender, KeyEventArgs e)
        {
            if (e.KeyCode == Keys.F5)
            {
                RefreshActiveTab(null, true);
            }
            else if (e.KeyCode == Keys.D && Control.ModifierKeys == Keys.Control)
            {
                Database.DBCache.GetInstance().Pool.Clear();
                Fields.GetInstance(this.server, Database.FieldHelper.GetFieldTableInternal).ClearCache();
                XtraMessageBox.Show("Database Cache Cleared");
            }
            else if (e.KeyCode == System.Windows.Forms.Keys.F && Control.ModifierKeys == Keys.Control)
            {
                
                barSearchTxt.Links[0].Focus();
                (barSearchTxt.Links[0] as DevExpress.XtraBars.BarEditItemLink).EditValue = null;
                (barSearchTxt.Links[0] as DevExpress.XtraBars.BarEditItemLink).ShowEditor();
            }
        }

        private void barSearchTxt_ShownEditor(object sender, DevExpress.XtraBars.ItemClickEventArgs e)
        {
            var item = (BarEditItem)sender;
            item.Manager.ActiveEditor.KeyDown -= ActiveEditor_KeyDown;
            item.Manager.ActiveEditor.KeyDown += ActiveEditor_KeyDown;
        }
        private void ActiveEditor_KeyDown(object sender, KeyEventArgs e)
        {
            var textEdit = sender as DevExpress.XtraEditors.TextEdit;
            if (e.KeyCode == System.Windows.Forms.Keys.Enter)
            {
                string search = textEdit.Text.Trim();
                textEdit.EditValue = null;
                DXHelper.QuickSearch qs = new DXHelper.QuickSearch();
                qs.SetExecuteDelegateOnSingleItemFilter(true);
                
                string csv_cols = "asset_id,loan_id,originator,servicer,original_balance,current_balance,property_address,property_city,property_state,original_term,remaining_term,lien,cutoff_date,borrower_id,loan_status_calc,dq_status_calc,primary_owner";
                DataTable tbl = PistonLib.Assets.GetAssetSummary(this.server,true);
                qs.SpawnQuickSearch(this.server, tbl, csv_cols, search, this.Owner, SetActiveAsset, true);
            }

        }

        public void HandleToolbarSearch()
        {
            barSearchTxt.ShownEditor += barSearchTxt_ShownEditor;
        }

        private void btnAccountKeys_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

        }
    }
}

using static DXHelper.LazyTable;
using static PistonLib.Trades;

namespace PistonControls
{
    public partial class ctrlAccountMaint : ITabBase
    {
        public ctrlAccountMaint()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }
        GridHelper _accounts;
        GridHelper _templates;
        public override void Init(string server, GridHelper.GridSetSearchGrid action, CommonInterfaces.Delegates.NewAssetSelected nas)
        {
            base.Init(server, action, nas);
            _accounts = new GridHelper(gridAccounts, server, true, action);
            _templates = new GridHelper(gridTemplates,server,true, action);
            
            _accounts.ShowFindPanel();
            Dictionary<string, string> acctMap = new Dictionary<string, string>();
            acctMap.Add("account_id", "id");
            _accounts.SetupGenericLazyTable("Accounts", "id", true, acctMap, null, null, null);
            CustomPopups.GetInstance(_accounts).RegisterEditGridPopup(null, "account_id,name,accounttype_id,name_short,is_saluda,legal_name,address_full,entity_state,servicingtype_id,entitytype_id,servicingtype_id,parent_id");
            _accounts.SetPostProcess(PostProcessRow);
            _templates.ShowFindPanel();
            Dictionary<string, string> colmap = new Dictionary<string, string>();
            colmap.Add("wiretemplate_id", "id");
            _templates.SetupGenericLazyTable("WireTemplates", "id", true, colmap, null, null, null);
            _templates.SetPostProcess(PostProcessRow);
            CustomPopups.GetInstance(_templates).RegisterEditGridPopup(null, "wiretemplate_id,account_id,name,nickname,bankacct_id,routing_number,account_number,ffc,bene_override_id,public_desc,wiretemplatetype_id,active");
        }

        public override void RefreshTab(string hei_id, bool force)
        {
            Task.Run(() => RefreshAccounts());
            Task.Run(() => RefreshTemplates());
        }
        private void PostProcessRow(DataRow row)
        {
            Database.DBCache.GetInstance().Pool.Clear();
        }

        public void RefreshTemplates()
        {
            int? account_id = _accounts.GetActiveRowValueNullable<int>("account_id");
            DataTable templates = PistonLib.Wires.GetWireTemplates(server, account_id, chkShowAll.Checked);
            DataTable accounts = PistonLib.Accounts.GetAccountList(server, false);

            DataTable types = PistonLib.Wires.GetWireTemplateTypes(server);

            _templates.SetGrid(templates, "account_id,nickname,bankacct_id,routing_number,account_number,ffc,bene_override_id,public_desc,wiretemplatetype_id,active");
            _templates.SetUpDropdown(accounts, "account_id", "name", "account_id");

            _templates.SetUpDropdown(types, "wiretemplatetype_id", "type", "wiretemplatetype_id");  

            DataTable bankaccts = PistonLib.Accounts.GetAccountList(server, false,8);
            _templates.SetUpDropdown(bankaccts, "bankacct_id", "name", "account_id");

            DataTable benne = PistonLib.Accounts.GetAccountList(server, false, null);
            _templates.SetUpDropdown(benne, "bene_override_id", "name", "account_id",new string[] { "legal_name" });


        }
        public void RefreshAccounts()
        {
            DataTable accounts = PistonLib.Accounts.GetAccountList(server, false);
            string cols = "name,accounttype_id,name_short,is_saluda,legal_name,entitytype_id,address_full,entity_state,entitytype_id,servicingtype_id,parent_id";
            _accounts.SetGrid(accounts, cols);


            DataTable account_types = PistonLib.Accounts.GetAccountTypes(server);
            _accounts.SetUpDropdown(account_types, "accounttype_id", "type", "accounttype_id");

            DataTable servicing_types = PistonLib.Servicing.GetServicingList(server);
            _accounts.SetUpDropdown(servicing_types, "servicingtype_id", "type", "servicingtype_id");

            DataTable entittype_id = PistonLib.Accounts.GetEntityTypes(server);
            _accounts.SetUpDropdown(entittype_id, "entitytype_id", "type", "entitytype_id");

            DataTable states = PistonLib.States.GetStateDropdown(server);
            _accounts.SetUpDropdown(states, "entity_state", "state_full", "state",new string[] { "state", "state_full" },null);

            DataTable parents = PistonLib.Accounts.GetAccountList(server,true,null);
            _accounts.SetUpDropdown(parents, "parent_id", "name", "account_id",null, null); 

            _accounts.BestFitVisible();
        }

            ((System.ComponentModel.ISupportInitialize)(this.checkEdit1.Properties)).EndInit();

        private void btnNewAccount_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            DataTable accounts = PistonLib.Accounts.GetAccountList(this.server, false);
            DXHelper.Forms.LazyTableEditor le = new DXHelper.Forms.LazyTableEditor();
            le.Init(server, accounts, "account_id,name,name_short,accounttype_id", "Accounts", "id", "accounttype_id,name,name_short", true, new Dictionary<string, string> { { "account_id", "id" } }, null);
            le.SetupDropDown(accounts, "account_id", "name", "account_id");
            DataTable account_types = PistonLib.Accounts.GetAccountTypes(this.server);
            le.SetupDropDown(account_types, "accounttype_id", "type", "accounttype_id");
            le.SetDimentions(500, 700);
            le.Show();
            
        }

        private void chkShowAll_CheckedChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            RefreshTemplates();
        }

        private void viewAccounts_FocusedRowChanged(object sender, DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Base.FocusedRowChangedEventArgs e)
        {
            RefreshTemplates();
        }

        private void btnAccountKeys_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            DataTable account_keys = PistonLib.Accounts.GetAccountKeys(server, null);
            DXHelper.Forms.LazyTableEditor le = new DXHelper.Forms.LazyTableEditor();
            le.Init(server, account_keys, "account_id,key,value","AccountKeys","id","account_id,key,value",true,new Dictionary<string,string> { { "accountkey_id", "id" } },null); 
            
            DataTable accounts = PistonLib.Accounts.GetAccountList(this.server, false);
            le.SetupDropDown(accounts, "account_id", "name", "account_id");

            DataTable keys = PistonLib.Keys.GetKeys(this.server);
            
            le.SetupDropDown(keys, "key","key","key");
            le.ShowFindPanel();
            le.SetDimentions(500, 750);
            le.Show();
        }
    }
}

using static System.Windows.Forms.VisualStyles.VisualStyleElement.ListView;
using static DevExpress.XtraEditors.RoundedSkinPanel;
namespace PistonControls
{
    public partial class ctrlDataIntegrity : ITabBase
    {
        public ctrlDataIntegrity()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        PistonGrid _summary;
        PistonGrid _offenders;
        public override void Init(string server, GridHelper.GridSetSearchGrid action, CommonInterfaces.Delegates.NewAssetSelected nas)
        {
            base.Init(server, action, nas);
            _summary = new PistonGrid(gridChecks, server, true, action);
            _summary.ToggleSearchPanel(true);
            PistonControls.PistonCustomPopups.GetPistonInstance(_summary).RegisterPopupsInternal(nas, null, null);
            
            _offenders = new PistonGrid(gridOffenders, server, true, action);
            _offenders.ToggleSearchPanel(true);
            _offenders.ShowGroupPanel(true);
            _offenders.AddRowCountsToGroup();

            PistonControls.PistonCustomPopups.GetPistonInstance(_offenders).RegisterPopupsInternal(nas, null, null);
        }




        public override void RefreshTab(string asset, bool force)
        {
            Task.Run(() => { RefreshChecks(); });
        }

        public void RefreshChecks()
        {
            DataTable summary = PistonLib.IntegrityChecks.GetIntegrityChecks(server);
            string cols = "priority,name_long,priority,check_type,scope";
            _summary.SetGrid(summary,cols);
            
   
        }

        private void btnAllTerm_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            RunChecks(new List<int> { 2 });
        }

        private void btnAllRTL_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            RunChecks(new List<int> { 1 });
        }

        private void RunChecks(List<int> product_type)
        {
            _offenders.ShowLoadingPanel();
            DataTable checks = PistonLib.IntegrityChecks.RunIntegrityChecks(this.server, new List<int>(), true, product_type,chkActiveAssets.Checked,chkOnlyTradedAssets.Checked);
            _offenders.SetGrid(checks);
            _offenders.ShowGridCalcs("loan_id", "Total Check Failures: {0:0,###}", DevExpress.Data.SummaryItemType.Count);
            _offenders.HideLoadingPanel();
        }
    }
}

--- FILE: Saluda\PistonControls\ctrlDocs.cs ---
using static System.Windows.Forms.VisualStyles.VisualStyleElement.ListView;
using static DevExpress.XtraEditors.RoundedSkinPanel;

namespace PistonControls
{
    public partial class ctrlDocs : ITabBase
    {
        public ctrlDocs()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        PistonGrid _summary;
        public override void Init(string server, GridHelper.GridSetSearchGrid action, CommonInterfaces.Delegates.NewAssetSelected nas)
        {
            base.Init(server, action, nas);
            _summary = new PistonGrid(gridDocs, server, true, action);
            _summary.ToggleSearchPanel(true);
            PistonControls.PistonCustomPopups.GetPistonInstance(_summary).RegisterPopupsInternal(nas, null, null);
        }


        public override void RefreshTab(string asset, bool force)
        {
            Task.Run(() => { RefreshDocs(); });
        }

        public void RefreshDocs()
        {
            DataTable summary = PistonLib.Docs.DocConfigSummary(server);
            DataTable docs = PistonLib.Docs.DocSummaryFromPackages(server);
            docs = docs.TrimColumms("account_name,effective_date,rev,docconfig_id,doc_id");
            DataSet s = new DataSet();
            s.Tables.Add(summary.Copy());
            s.Tables.Add(docs.Copy());
            s.Relations.Add(s.Tables[0].Columns["docconfig_id"], s.Tables[1].Columns["docconfig_id"]);

            string cols = "docconfig_id,name,base_folder,file_format,docoutputtype";
            _summary.SetGrid(s, cols);

        }
    }
}

--- FILE: Saluda\PistonControls\ctrlDraws.cs ---
using static DXHelper.LazyTable;
namespace PistonControls
{
    public partial class ctrlDraws : ITabBase
    {
        public ctrlDraws()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        GridHelper _draws;
        GridHelper _summary;
        GridHelper _summary_by_day;
        public override void Init(string server, GridHelper.GridSetSearchGrid action, CommonInterfaces.Delegates.NewAssetSelected nas)
        {
            base.Init(server, action, nas);
            _draws = new GridHelper(gridDraws,server, true, action);
            _summary = new GridHelper(gridSummary, server, true, action);
            _summary_by_day = new GridHelper(gridSummaryByDay,server, true, action);

            PistonControls.PistonCustomPopups.GetPistonInstance(_draws).RegisterPopupsInternal(nas, null, null);
            
            _draws.ShowFindPanel();

            this.viewDraws.Appearance.GroupRow.Font = new System.Drawing.Font("Tahoma", 11.5F, System.Drawing.FontStyle.Bold);
            this.viewDraws.Appearance.GroupRow.ForeColor = System.Drawing.Color.Firebrick;
            this.viewDraws.Appearance.GroupRow.Options.UseFont = true;
            this.viewDraws.Appearance.GroupRow.Options.UseForeColor = true;

            _draws.ToggleAutoFilter(true);
            _draws.ToggleSearchPanel(true);
            _draws.ShowFooter(true);


            
            
            
        }
        bool initial_refresh = true;
        public override void RefreshTab(string hei_id, bool force)
        {
            if (initial_refresh || force)
            {
                Task.Run(() => { PopulateDraws(); });
                initial_refresh = false;
            }
            Task.Run(() => { PopulateSummary(); });
            Task.Run(() => { LastUpdate(); });

        }

        public void PopulateSummary()
        {
            DataTable summary = PistonLib.Draws.DrawStatusSummary(server);
            _summary.SetGrid(summary);
            _summary.ShowSums("pending_approval_upb,approved_not_disbursed_upb");

            DataTable summary_by_day = PistonLib.Draws.DrawStatusSummaryByDeal(server);
            _summary_by_day.SetGrid(summary_by_day);
            _summary_by_day.ShowSums("draw_amount");


        }

        public void LastUpdate()
        {
            DateTime? last_update = PistonLib.Draws.LastUpdate(server);
            lblLastUpdate.SetTextSafe($"Last Update: {last_update}");
        }
        
        public void PopulateDraws()
        {

            DataTable draws = PistonLib.Draws.DrawHistoryWithTrades(server);
            string cols = "asset_id,loan_id,address,status,draw_num,request_type,draw_amount,request_date,fund_date,requestor_email,sg_approver,sg_approval_date,reimbursement_date,sg_deal,trade_id";
            _draws.SetGrid(draws,cols);
            
            _draws.GroupBySingle("status");
            _draws.SetCustomSort("request_date", "request_date", DevExpress.Data.ColumnSortOrder.Ascending);
            _draws.ExpandAllGroupBy();
            _draws.ShowSums("draw_amount");
        }

        private void btnTodaysDraws_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            
            string filter = "[reimbursement_date] = Today()";
            _draws.SetActiveFilterStringSafe(filter);
        }
    }
}

namespace PistonControls
{
    public partial class ctrlHome : ITabBase
    {
        public ctrlHome()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        PistonGrid _main;

        public override void Init(string server, GridHelper.GridSetSearchGrid action, CommonInterfaces.Delegates.NewAssetSelected nas)
        {
            base.Init(server, action, nas);
            _main = new PistonGrid(mainGrid, server, true, action);
            _main.ToggleSearchPanel(true);
            _main.ToggleAutoFilter(true);
            PistonControls.PistonCustomPopups.GetPistonInstance(_main).RegisterPopupsInternal(nas, null, null);
            ctrlLegend.Init(server);
        }

        private bool loaded_once = false;

        public override async void RefreshTab(string asset,bool force)
        {
            if (loaded_once && !force)
                return;


            Task.Run(() => { PopulateMainGrid(null);});
            Task.Run(() => { ctrlLegend.RefreshLegend(_main); });
            _main._view.GridControl.Invoke(new MethodInvoker(() => { gridView1.OptionsView.ColumnAutoWidth = false; }));
            

            
            
            
            gridView1.HorzScrollVisibility = DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Base.ScrollVisibility.Always;
            

            
            
            
            
            loaded_once = true;
        }

        public void PopulateMainGrid(List<int> asset_ids)
        {
            
            ShowLoadingPanelSafe();
            var asset_summary = PistonLib.Assets.GetAssetSummarySet(this.server,asset_ids);
            bool dupe = false;
            if(null != asset_ids)
            {
                if (asset_ids.Count != asset_summary.Tables[0].Rows.Count)
                    XtraMessageBox.Show("Happens when a loan ID also matches an asset id - you'll have extra records in the grid","Warning: Multiple Loan ID / Asset ID Match");
            }

            
            asset_summary.Tables[0].ReOrder("asset_id", asset_ids, false);
            FormatMainGridWithColor(asset_summary);
            if (null == asset_ids)
                _main.SetColorPostProcessing(ProcessedColor);
            else
                _main.SetColorPostProcessing(null);

            bool do_long_queries = true;
#if (DEBUG == true)
            do_long_queries = true;
#endif
            if(do_long_queries)
                _main.AddColorAsync(asset_ids);

           
     

            





        }

        DataSet full_search_cache;
        public void ProcessedColor(DataSet set)
        {
            this.full_search_cache = set;
            btnQuickPopulate.EnabledSafe(true);
        }

        public void FormatMainGridWithColor(DataSet asset_summary)
        {
            
            
            string cols = "asset_id,loan_id,originator,owner_name_calc,address_full,dq_status_calc,total_committed_amount,current_balance_calc,LTC,LTARV,FICO,borrower,property_type_calc,Units,loan_purpose_calc,product_type_calc,loan_type_calc,next_due_date,origination_date,current_maturity_date,gross_rate,pass_thru_rate"; 
            _main.SetGrid(asset_summary, cols,null,null,true,null,false);
            
        }

        public void ShowLoadingPanelSafe()
        {
            if (_main._view.GridControl.InvokeRequired)
            {
                _main._view.GridControl.Invoke(new MethodInvoker(() => { ShowLoadingPanelSafe(); }));
            }
            else
            {
                _main._view.ShowLoadingPanel();
            }
        }
        private void btnRemitSummary_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            string sql = "select deal,asOf,sum(beginning_upb) [beginning_upb], sum(ending_upb) [ending_upb] from Remits group by deal,asOf";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            DataTable tbl = q.ExecuteTable();
            _main.SetGrid(tbl);
        }

        private void simpleButton1_Click_1(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            SearchBoxExecute();
            
        }

        private void txtSearch_EditValueChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            btnSearch.Enabled = txtSearch.Text.Length > 0;
        }

        private void txtSearch_PreviewKeyDown(object sender, PreviewKeyDownEventArgs e)
        {
            if(e.KeyCode == System.Windows.Forms.Keys.Enter)
            {
                SearchBoxExecute();
            }
        }

        public void SearchBoxExecute()
        {
            List<string> raw = txtSearch.Text.Replace("\r", "").Split('\n').Where(n => !String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(n)).ToList();
            List<int> asset_ids = new List<int>();
            bool multiple = false;

            _main.ClearFindFilter();
            List<string> missing = new List<string>();
            foreach (string asset in raw)
            {
                if (PistonLib.Assets.IsAssetID(asset))
                    asset_ids.Add(Convert.ToInt32(asset));
                else
                {
                    int? asset_id = PistonLib.Assets.GetAssetId(server, asset,null,null, false);
                    if (null == asset_id)
                    {
                        
                        missing.Add(asset);
                        
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        if (!asset_ids.Contains(asset_id.Value))
                            asset_ids.Add(asset_id.Value);
                        else
                            multiple = true;
                    }
                }
            }
            if(multiple)
            {
                XtraMessageBox.Show("Duplicate asset id's found - removed duplicates.");
            }
            if(missing.Count > 0)
            {
                string msg = String.Join(Environment.NewLine, missing);
                System.Windows.Forms.Clipboard.SetText(msg);
                XtraMessageBox.Show(msg,"Missing Loans - Copied to Clipboard");
            }
            PistonLib.Usage.RecordUsage(server, PistonLib.Usage.UsageTypes.SEARCH, asset_ids.Count, null, txtSearch.Text, null, null, null);
            PopulateMainGrid(asset_ids);
        }

        private void btnQuickPopulate_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            if(null != this.full_search_cache)
            {
                FormatMainGridWithColor(this.full_search_cache);
            }
        }

        private void ctrlHome_KeyUp(object sender, KeyEventArgs e)
        {

        }

        private void ctrlHome_PreviewKeyDown(object sender, PreviewKeyDownEventArgs e)
        {
            if (e.KeyCode == System.Windows.Forms.Keys.F && Control.ModifierKeys == System.Windows.Forms.Keys.Control)
            {
                
                txtSearch.Focus();
                
                
            }
        }

        private void btnReinstall_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            string install_location = Database.Common.GetGlobal<string>(server, "INSTALL_LOCATION", true, true);
            string[] setup = System.IO.Directory.GetFiles(install_location, "Setup.exe");
            if(setup.Length == 1)
            {
                UtilsLib.FileLib.SpawnProcess(setup[0], true);
                
                Application.Exit();
            }
        }
    }
}

namespace PistonControls
{
    public partial class ctrlIssues : ITabBase
    {
        public ctrlIssues()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        PistonGrid _issues;
        public override void Init(string server, GridHelper.GridSetSearchGrid action, CommonInterfaces.Delegates.NewAssetSelected nas)
        {
            base.Init(server, action, nas);
            _issues = new PistonGrid(gridIssues, server, true, action);

            Dictionary<string, string> colmap = new Dictionary<string, string>();
            colmap.Add("issue_id", "id");
            PistonControls.PistonCustomPopups.GetPistonInstance(_issues).RegisterPopupsInternal(nas, null, null);
            _issues.SetupGenericLazyTable("Issues", "id", true, colmap, null, null, null);
            CustomPopups.GetInstance(_issues).RegisterEditGridPopup(EnableEligibilityEditing);
        }


        public override void RefreshTab(string asset, bool force)
        {
            DataTable issues = PistonLib.Issues.GetIssues(server);
            _issues.SetGrid(issues, "asset_id,loan_id,property_address,issuetype_id,note,issueresolutiontype_id,update_time,update_by");

            DataTable types = PistonLib.Issues.GetIssueTypes(server);
            DataTable resolutions = PistonLib.Issues.GetIssueResolutions(server);

            _issues.SetUpDropdown(types, "issuetype_id", "type", "issuetype_id");
            _issues.SetUpDropdown(resolutions, "issueresolutiontype_id", "type", "issueresolutiontype_id");

        }
        public void EnableEligibilityEditing()
        {
            _issues.SetEditable("asset_id,issuetype_id,note,issueresolutiontype_id", CommonInterfaces.Constants.BADGER.EDIT_COLOR);

        }
    }
}

namespace BatCave.Controls
{
    public partial class ctrlLegend : DevExpress.XtraEditors.XtraUserControl
    {
        public ctrlLegend()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        private string _server;
        public void Init(string server)
        {
            _server = server;
        }

        DataTable _colors;
        GridHelper _gh;
        public void RefreshLegend(GridHelper gh)
        {
            _gh = gh;
            Populate("type");
        }


        public void Populate(string column)
        {
            _colors = PistonLib.Color.GetColorLegend(_server);
            _val_col = "type";
            listBox1.Items.ClearSafe(_gh.GridControl);
            foreach (DataRow row in _colors.Rows)
            {
                listBox1.Items.AddSafe(_gh.GridControl,row[column]);
            }
        }

        public void MultiColumn(bool multi)
        {
            listBox1.MultiColumn = multi;
        }
        public void ToggleLabelVisibility(bool visible)
        {
            labelControl1.Visible = visible;
        }
        private string _val_col;


        public void SetBold()
        {
            this.listBox1.Appearance.Font = new System.Drawing.Font(listBox1.Font.Name, listBox1.Font.Size, System.Drawing.FontStyle.Bold);
        }
        public void PopulateEasy(string item,string color)
        {
            if(null == _colors)
            {
                _colors = new DataTable();
                _val_col = "type";
                _colors.Columns.Add("value");
                _colors.Columns.Add("row_color");
            }
            _colors.Rows.Add(new object[] { item, color });
            listBox1.Items.Add(item);
        }

        public void Resize(Nullable<int> width, Nullable<int> height)
        {
            int _width = listBox1.Width;
            int _height = listBox1.Height;
            if (null != width)
                _width = width.Value;
            if (null != height)
                _height = height.Value;

            listBox1.Size = new Size(_width, _height);
        }


         private void listBox1_DrawItem(object sender, ListBoxDrawItemEventArgs e)
        {
            string item = listBox1.Items[e.Index].ToString();
            string color = _colors.Select("["+_val_col+"] = '" + item + "'")[0]["row_color"].ToString();
            e.AllowDrawSkinBackground = false;
            e.Appearance.BackColor = System.Drawing.Color.FromName(color);
        }
    }
}

using static DXHelper.LazyTable;
namespace PistonControls
{
    public partial class ctrlLoader :  ITabBase
    {
        public ctrlLoader()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        GridHelper _summary;
        GridHelper _tapeNotes;
        GridHelper _integrityChecks;


        public override void Init(string server, GridHelper.GridSetSearchGrid action, CommonInterfaces.Delegates.NewAssetSelected nas)
        {
            base.Init(server, action, nas);
            _summary = new GridHelper(gridTapeDetail, server, true, action);
            _tapeNotes = new GridHelper(gridTapeNotes,server, true, action);
            _integrityChecks = new GridHelper(gridIntegrityChecks,server, true, action);
            _integrityChecks.AddRowCountsToGroup();
            _summary.ToggleSearchPanel(true);
            _summary.ToggleAutoFilter(true);
            
            _tapeNotes.ToggleGroupBy(false);
            PistonControls.PistonCustomPopups.GetPistonInstance(_summary).RegisterPopupsInternal(nas, null, null);
            PistonControls.PistonCustomPopups.GetPistonInstance(_integrityChecks).RegisterPopupsInternal(nas, null, null);


        }


        public override void RefreshTab(string asset,bool force)
        {
            PopulateLoaderDropdown();
            Task.Run(() => PopulateRemitSummary());
            PopulateTapeTypeDropdown();
            PopulateTapeMaps(null);
            PopulateBatch();

            dtAsOf.EditValue = DateTime.Today;
            drpCutoff.EditValue = null;
            if (Environment.UserName.Contains("nite") || Environment.UserName.ContainsIns("dan"))
            {
                drpDeals.EditValue = 18;
                
                
                drpTapeTypes.EditValue = 2;
                drpMapping.EditValue = 32;
            }
            if (force)
            {
                
            }
        }

        public void PopulateIntegrityChecks(int tape_id)
        {
            _integrityChecks.ShowLoadingPanel();
            DataTable checks = PistonLib.IntegrityChecks.RunIntegrityChecks(this.server, new List<int> { tape_id },true,new List<int>(),false,false);
            _integrityChecks.SetGrid(checks);
            _integrityChecks.HideLoadingPanel();
        }

        public void PopulateTapeMaps(int? selected_map)
        {
            DataTable tapemaps = PistonLib.Tapes.GetTapeMaps(server);
            drpMapping.PopulateLookup(tapemaps, "name", "tapemap_id", true);
            if (null != selected_map)
                drpMapping.EditValue = selected_map.Value;
        }

        public void PopulateBatch()
        {
            DataTable batches = new DataTable();
            batches.Columns.Add("batch_id", typeof(int));
            batches.Columns.Add("name", typeof(string));
            batches.Rows.Add(1, "Remit");
            batches.Rows.Add(2, "Batch Trade File");
            drpBatch.PopulateLookup(batches, "name", "batch_id", false);
        }
        public void PopulateTapeTypeDropdown()
        {
            DataTable tapetypes = PistonLib.Tapes.GetTapeTypes(this.server);
            drpTapeTypes.PopulateLookup(tapetypes, "type", "tapetype_id", false);
        }

        public void PopulateRemitSummary()
        {
            _summary.ShowLoadingPanel();
            DataSet summary = PistonLib.Tapes.GetRemitSummary(this.server);
            string cols = "tape_id,tape_type,account,cutoff_date,loans,balance,gwac,margin,asof,load_time,loaded_by";
            _summary.SetGrid(summary,cols);
        }
        public void PopulateLoaderDropdown()
        {
            DataTable deals = PistonLib.Accounts.GetAccountList(this.server, true);
            drpDeals.PopulateLookup(deals, "name", "account_id", false);
        }

        private void btnGo_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            int? tape_id = null;
            bool exception = false;
            bool aborted = false;
            try
            {

                int account_id = drpDeals.EditValue.AsInt().Value;
                int tapetype_id = drpTapeTypes.EditValue.AsInt().Value;
                int? tapemap_id = drpMapping.EditValue.AsInt();
                DateTime? cutoff_date = drpCutoff.EditValue.AsDate();
                DateTime? asOf = dtAsOf.EditValue.AsDate();

                var file_load = XL.FileReaderSimple.PickAndRead("Pick Tape", "xlsx", false, true);
                DataTable tbl = file_load.Table;
                aborted = file_load.aborted;
                if (null == tbl || file_load.aborted)
                    return;
                lblFilename.Text = $"Loading: {System.IO.Path.GetFileName(file_load.filename)}";
                if (tbl.Columns.Contains("asof"))
                    tbl.Columns["asOf"].ChangeDataType(typeof(DateTime));

                if (null != drpBatch.EditValue)
                {
                    int batch_id = drpBatch.EditValue.AsInt().Value;
                    string first_group = null;
                    string asof_lookup_filed = null;
                    string account_lookup_field = null;
   
                    if (batch_id == 1)
                    {
                        first_group = "DEAL";
                        asof_lookup_filed = "ASOF";
                        account_lookup_field = "deal";
        
                    }
                    if (batch_id == 2)
                    {
                        first_group = "tape_break";
                        asof_lookup_filed = "asOf";
                        account_lookup_field = "account_id";
                    }
                    if(batch_id == 2 || batch_id == 1)
                    {
                        GC.Collect();
                        List<DataTable> deals = tbl.AsEnumerable().GroupBy(row => row.Field<string>(first_group)).Select(g => g.CopyToDataTable()).ToList();
                        DXETA eta = new DXETA(tbl.Rows.Count, null, this.ParentForm);
                        int blank_loan_ids = 0;
                        foreach (DataTable deal in deals)
                        {
                            if (batch_id == 2)
                            {
                                cutoff_date = asOf;
                            }
                            GC.Collect();
                            string deal_name = deal.Rows[0][account_lookup_field].ToString();
                            List<DataTable> result = deal.AsEnumerable().GroupBy(row => row.Field<DateTime>(asof_lookup_filed)).Select(g => g.CopyToDataTable()).ToList();
                            foreach (DataTable remit in result)
                            {

                                if(!int.TryParse(deal_name, out account_id))
                                    account_id = PistonLib.Accounts.GetAccountId(server, deal_name).Value;
                                DateTime asOf_remit = System.Convert.ToDateTime(remit.Rows[0][asof_lookup_filed]);
                                
                                asOf = asOf_remit;
                                if (null == cutoff_date || (null != cutoff_date && cutoff_date.Value.Year == 1900))
                                    cutoff_date = asOf;

                                
                                bool tape_exists = PistonLib.Tapes.TapeExists(server, account_id, asOf.Value, cutoff_date.Value);
                                
               
                                if(tape_exists) 
                                {
                                        string account_name = PistonLib.Accounts.GetSingleAttribute<string>(server, account_id, "name");
                                        var dr = XtraMessageBox.Show($"Tape for {account_name} already exists for {asOf:M/d/yyyy}{Environment.NewLine}{Environment.NewLine}Creating a new tape...", "FYI");
                                }
                                
                                {
                                    tape_id = PistonLib.Tapes.CreateTape(server, drpTapeTypes.EditValue.AsInt().Value, account_id, cutoff_date.Value, asOf.Value,txtNotes.Text,tapemap_id, System.IO.Path.GetFileName(file_load.filename));
                                }
                                
                                
                                
                                
                                
                                
                                
                                
                                
                                
                                
                                
                                
                                

                                
                                
                                
                                
                                
                                


                                var results = PistonLib.Tapes.TransformTape(server, tapemap_id, remit, true,true,true);
                                
                                
                                
                                
                                
                                
                                
                                
                                

                                
                                if (remit.Rows.Count == 0)
                                {
                                    continue;
                                }

                                results.clean_tape.Columns.AddColumnWithDefaultIgnoreIfAlreadyExists<int>("tape_id", tape_id.Value);



                                
                                List<string> sqls = Database.QueryBuilder.SQLInsertValidate(results.clean_tape, server, "TapeDetail", true).lines;
                                lblProcessing.Text = $"Processing: {deal_name} - {asOf:M/d/yyyy}";
                                Application.DoEvents();
                                
                                Query q = new Query(null, server);
                                q.SetETA(eta);
                                q.ExecuteBatch(sqls, 25, null);
                                PistonLib.Tapes.ProcessTapes(server, tape_id.Value,null);
                                

                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                else
                {
                    aborted = true;
                    var results = PistonLib.Tapes.TransformTape(server, tapemap_id, tbl, true,true, true);

                    
                    


                    QuickView clean = new QuickView();
                    clean.InitAndShowLazy(this.server, results.clean_tape, "Mapped Data", _summary.DoubleClickAction);
                    clean.ToggleColumnAutoWidth(false);

                    if(results.removed_data.Columns.Count > 0)
                    {
                        string unmapped = results.removed_data.Columns.ToCSVCols(Environment.NewLine);
                        var dr = XtraMessageBox.Show(unmapped, "Bro....You're not loading columns.  You sure?", MessageBoxButtons.YesNoCancel);
                        if(dr != DialogResult.Yes)
                        {
                            return;
                        }
                    }
                    
                    
                    

                    



                    if (!chkValidate.Checked)
                    {
                        if (results.removed_data.Columns.Count > 0)
                        {
                            var confirm = XtraMessageBox.Show($"You have {results.removed_data.Columns.Count} unmapped columns - Load anyway?", "Hi", MessageBoxButtons.YesNoCancel);
                            if (confirm != DialogResult.Yes)
                            {
                                return;
                            }
                        }
                        
                        DXETA eta = new DXETA(results.clean_tape.Rows.Count, null, this.ParentForm);

                        var result = PistonLib.Tapes.CreateAndLoadTape(server, true, tapetype_id, account_id, cutoff_date.Value, asOf.Value, txtNotes.Text, tapemap_id.Value, file_load.filename,eta,results,false);
                        tape_id = result.tape_id;
                        if(!String.IsNullOrEmpty(result.error))
                        {
                            XtraMessageBox.Show(result.error, "Errors");
                        }
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        aborted = false;
                    }

                }

            }
            catch (Exception n)
            {
                UtilsLib.Error.SendDefaultError(n);
                XtraMessageBox.Show(n.Message + Environment.NewLine + Environment.NewLine + n.StackTrace);
                return;
            }
            finally
            {
                if (null != tape_id)
                    XtraMessageBox.Show("Tape Load ID: " + tape_id);
                if(!chkValidate.Checked && !aborted && !exception)
                    PistonLib.Tapes.ProcessTapes(server,tape_id,null);
                lblFilename.Text = null;
            }
            if (!chkValidate.Checked)
            {
                
                RefreshTab(_active_hei);
            }
            if(exception)
            {
                
            }
            lblProcessing.Text = null;
            
        }

        private void dtAsOf_TextChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            dtAsOf.Enabled = null == drpBatch.EditValue;
            drpDeals.Enabled = null == drpBatch.EditValue;
            drpTapeTypes.Enabled = null == drpBatch.EditValue;
            drpCutoff.Enabled = null == drpBatch.EditValue;

            btnGo.Enabled = (null != dtAsOf.EditValue && null != drpDeals.EditValue && null != drpTapeTypes.EditValue && null != drpCutoff.EditValue) || (null != drpBatch.EditValue);
            
        }

        private void btnResetAll_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            var dr = XtraMessageBox.Show("You sure bro?", "Quick q", MessageBoxButtons.YesNoCancel);
            if (dr == DialogResult.Yes)
            {
                PistonLib.Tapes.ResetAccountRemits(server, null);
                XtraMessageBox.Show("DONE!");
                this.RefreshTab(_active_hei);
            }
        }

        }

        private void viewTapeDetail_FocusedRowChanged(object sender, DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Base.FocusedRowChangedEventArgs e)

                return;
            int tape_id = _summary.GetRowValue<int>(e.FocusedRowHandle, "tape_id");

            Task.Run(() => PopulateIntegrityChecks(tape_id));
        }

--- FILE: Saluda\PistonControls\ctrlPositions.cs ---
namespace PistonControls
{
    public partial class ctrlPositions : ITabBase
    {
        public ctrlPositions()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }
        GridHelper _summary;
        GridHelper _detail;
        public override void Init(string server, GridHelper.GridSetSearchGrid action, CommonInterfaces.Delegates.NewAssetSelected nas)
        {
            base.Init(server, action, nas);
            _summary = new GridHelper(gridPositions, server, true, action);
            _summary.ToggleSearchPanel(true);

            _detail = new GridHelper(gridDetail, server, true, action);
            _detail.ToggleSearchPanel(true);
            PistonControls.PistonCustomPopups.GetPistonInstance(_summary).RegisterPopupsInternal(nas, null, null);
            PistonControls.PistonCustomPopups.GetPistonInstance(_detail).RegisterPopupsInternal(nas, null, null);
        }
        public override void RefreshTab(string asset, bool force)
        {
            
            Task.Run(() => { PopulatePositionSummary(); });
        }

        public void PopulatePositionSummary()
        {
            
            _summary.ShowLoadingPanel();
            DataTable summary = PistonLib.Positions.GetPositionSummaryTable(this.server);
            string cols = "account,ln_cnt,beginning_upb,purchased_upb,total_drawn_amount,scheduled_principal,unscheduled_principal,princ_sold,ending_upb,last_remit,reinvestable_cash_live";

            DateTime? cash_load_time = summary.AsEnumerable().Select(x => x.Field<DateTime?>("cash_asOf")).Min();
            
            
            lblCashAsOf.SetTextSafe($"<href=https:

            _summary.SetGrid(summary,cols);
            _summary.ShowSums("ln_cnt,beginning_upb,purchased_upb,total_drawn_amount,scheduled_principal,unscheduled_principal,princ_sold,ending_upb", "{0:n0}");
            _summary.ShowGridCalcs("account", "Totals: {0}", DevExpress.Data.SummaryItemType.Count);
            _summary.ShowGridCalcs("reinvestable_cash_live", "Total: {0:n0}", DevExpress.Data.SummaryItemType.Sum);
            _summary.HideLoadingPanel();
        }

        private void viewDetail_FocusedRowChanged(object sender, DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Base.FocusedRowChangedEventArgs e)
        {

        }

        private void viewPositions_FocusedRowChanged(object sender, DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Base.FocusedRowChangedEventArgs e)
        {
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            

        }

        private void lblCashAsOf_HyperlinkClick(object sender, DevExpress.Utils.HyperlinkClickEventArgs e)
        {
            lblCashAsOf.LinkVisited = true;
            System.Diagnostics.Process.Start(e.Link);
        }

        private void viewDetail_SelectionChanged(object sender, DevExpress.Data.SelectionChangedEventArgs e)
        {
           
        }

        public void RefreshDetail(List<int> tapes)
        {
            _detail.ShowLoadingPanel();
            DataTable detail = PistonLib.TapeDetail.GetTapeDetailAllStatic(server, tapes);
            string cols = "account_name,asset_id,loan_id,originator,dq_status_calc,total_committed_amount,ending_upb,LTC_calc,LTARV,FICO_calc,borrower,Units,property_type_calc,loan_purpose_calc,product_type_calc,next_due_date,origination_date,current_maturity_date,gross_rate,pass_thru_rate";
            _detail.SetGrid(detail, cols);
        }
        private void viewPositions_SelectionChanged(object sender, DevExpress.Data.SelectionChangedEventArgs e)
        {
            List<int> tapes = _summary.GetSelectedRowList<int>("tape_id", true);
            Task.Run(() => { RefreshDetail(tapes); });

        }
    }

namespace PistonControls
{
    public partial class ctrlReports : ITabBase
    {
        public ctrlReports()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        PistonGrid _results;
        public override void Init(string server, GridHelper.GridSetSearchGrid action, CommonInterfaces.Delegates.NewAssetSelected nas)
        {
            base.Init(server, action, nas);
            _results = new PistonGrid(gridResults, server, true, action);

            _results.ToggleSearchPanel(true);
            PistonControls.PistonCustomPopups.GetPistonInstance(_results).RegisterPopupsInternal(nas, null, null);
        }

        private void btnExecute_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

        }

        private void btnGo_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            DataTable remits = PistonLib.TapeDetail.GetAllRemitTapes(server);
            _results.SetGrid(remits);
        }

        private void btnNeedMapping_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            Query q = new Query("select count(*),loan_type from vAssetsEx a where a.product_1 is null group by loan_type", this.server);
            var p = q.ExecuteTable();
            _results.SetGrid(p);
        }

        private void btnLoanStatus_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            Query q = new Query("select count(*),td.loan_status,loan_status_calc,lt.map_to from TapeDetail td left join vMaps lt on lt.db_field = 'loan_status' and td.loan_status = lt.map_from where map_to is null group by lt.map_to,td.loan_status,loan_status_calc", this.server);
            var p = q.ExecuteTable();
            _results.SetGrid(p);
        }

        private void btnMissingDQStatus_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            Query q = new Query("select count(*),td.dq_status,dq_status_calc,lt.map_to from TapeDetail td left join vMaps lt on lt.db_field = 'dq_status' and td.dq_status = lt.map_from where map_to is null group by lt.map_to,td.dq_status,dq_status_calc", this.server);
            var p = q.ExecuteTable();
            _results.SetGrid(p);
        }
    }

}

--- FILE: Saluda\PistonControls\ctrlTrades.cs ---
using static DXHelper.LazyTable;
namespace PistonControls
{
    public partial class ctrlTrades : ITabBase
    {
        public ctrlTrades()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        GridHelper _trades;
        GridHelper _detail;
        public override void Init(string server, GridHelper.GridSetSearchGrid action, CommonInterfaces.Delegates.NewAssetSelected nas)
        {
            base.Init(server, action, nas);
            _trades = new GridHelper(gridTrades, server, true, action);
            _detail = new GridHelper(gridDetail,server, true, action);

            PistonControls.PistonCustomPopups.GetPistonInstance(_trades).RegisterPopupsInternal(nas, null, null);
            CustomPopups.GetInstance(_trades).RegisterEditGridPopup(SetMappingEditable);

            PistonControls.PistonCustomPopups.GetPistonInstance(_detail).RegisterPopupsInternal(nas, null, null);
            CustomPopups.GetInstance(_detail).RegisterEditGridPopup(SetTradesDetailEditable);

            _trades.ShowFindPanel();

            
            _trades.SetupGenericLazyTable("Trades", "trade_id", true,null, null, null, null);
            _trades.SetPreProcess(PreProcessRow);
            _trades.SetPostProcess(PostProcessRow);

            _detail.ShowFooter(true);
            
            
            
            
        }

        private void PreProcessRow(DataRow row)
        {
            if (row.RowState == DataRowState.Added)
            {
                row["tape_id"] = selected_tape_id;
            }
        }
        private void PostProcessRow(DataRow row)
        {

            int focused_row_handle = _trades._view.FocusedRowHandle;

            if (focused_row_handle != -1 && row.RowState != DataRowState.Deleted)
            {
                
                
                _trades.SetRowValue(focused_row_handle, "trade_id", row["trade_id"]);
                current_trade_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["trade_id"]);
                _trades._DataTable.AcceptChanges();

            }
        }
        public void SetMappingEditable()
        {
            _trades.SetEditable("trade_id,account_id,buy_sell,counterparty_id,trade_date,settle_date,notes,tape_id", null);
            _trades.ToggleEmbeddedNavigator(true);
        }

        public void SetTradesDetailEditable()
        {
            _detail.SetEditable("PRICE,ACCRUED_INTEREST", null);
            _detail.ToggleEmbeddedNavigator(true);
        }

        public override void RefreshTab(string hei_id, bool force)
        {
            
            PopulateTrades(current_trade_id);

        }
        public void RefreshTab(int? trade_id)
        {
            PopulateTrades(trade_id);
        }

        bool new_trade = false;
        public void EnableNewTrade()
        {
            
            
            
            btnInsertTrades.Visible = true;
            new_trade = true;
        }

        
        public void PopulateTrades(int? trade_id)
        {

            DataTable trades = null;
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            {
                trades = PistonLib.Trades.GetTrades(this.server);
                grpTrades.Text = "Trade Summary";
            }

            string cols = "trade_id,ln_count,account_id,buy_sell,counterparty_id,cface,trade_date,settle_date,notes,update_time,update_by,ticket_type";

            _trades.SetGrid(trades,cols);

            DataTable accounts = PistonLib.Accounts.GetAccountList(this.server,true);
            _trades.SetUpDropdown(accounts, "account_id","name","account_id");
            _trades.SetUpDropdown(accounts, "counterparty_id", "name", "account_id");

            DataTable buy_sell = PistonLib.Trades.BuySellTable();
            _trades.SetUpDropdown(buy_sell, "buy_sell", "BUY/SELL", "id");
        }

        public int? current_trade_id;
        private void viewTrades_SelectionChanged(object sender, DevExpress.Data.SelectionChangedEventArgs e)
        {


        }

        public void PopulateTapeFromTradeId(int? trade_id)
        {
            
            DataTable trade_details = PistonLib.Trades.GetTradeDetail(server, trade_id);
            string col = "asset_id,loan_id,cface,coupon,price,market_value,accrued_interest,total_proceeds";
            SetTradeDetail(trade_details,col);
            
            
            
            
        }

        private int? selected_tape_id;
        public void PopulateTape(int tape_id)
        {
            selected_tape_id = tape_id;
            DataTable tape = PistonLib.Tapes.GetTape(this.server, tape_id);
            if(!tape.Columns.Contains("price"))
                tape.Columns.Add("price", typeof(double));
            
            if (tape.Columns.Contains("market_value"))
                tape.Columns.Remove("market_value");
                tape.Columns.Add("market_value", typeof(double), "[price] * [balance]");
            if (!tape.Columns.Contains("accrued_interest"))
                tape.Columns.Add("accrued_interest", typeof(double));


            if (tape.Columns.Contains("total_proceeds"))
                tape.Columns.Remove("total_proceeds");
            if (tape.Columns.Contains("gross_rate"))
                tape.Columns["gross_rate"].ColumnName = "coupon";
            if (tape.Columns.Contains("balance"))
                tape.Columns["balance"].ColumnName = "cface";
            

            tape.Columns.Add("total_proceeds", typeof(double), "[market_value] + [accrued_interest]");
            string col = "asset_id,loan_id,cface,coupon,price,market_value,accrued_interest,total_proceeds";
            SetTradeDetail(tape,col);

        }

        public void SetTradeDetail(DataTable tape,string col)
        {
            
            
            _detail.SetGrid(tape, col);
            _detail.ShowSums("market_value,accrued_interest,total_proceeds,cface");
        }

        private void checkEdit1_CheckedChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            int? trade_id = null;
            
            
            
            
            PopulateTrades(trade_id);
        }
  
        private void viewTrades_FocusedRowChanged(object sender, DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Base.FocusedRowChangedEventArgs e)
        {
            int? new_trade_id = _trades.GetRowValueNullable<int>(e.FocusedRowHandle,"trade_id");
            if (null != new_trade_id && new_trade_id != current_trade_id && new_trade == false)
            {
                PopulateTapeFromTradeId(new_trade_id.Value);
            }
            current_trade_id = new_trade_id;
        }

        private void btnInsertTrades_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            DataTable tbl = _detail._DataTable;
            
            bool populated = tbl.RowsAllHaveValue("asset_id,cface,price,accrued_interest,coupon,days_accrued,trade_date,settle_date,buy_sell,account_id,counterparty_id");
            if (!populated)
            {
                XtraMessageBox.Show("You have blank columns that are required...", "Oops...");
                return;
            }


            DXETA eta = new DXETA(tbl.Rows.Count, null, this.ParentForm);

            foreach (DataRow row in tbl.Rows)
            {
                
                PistonLib.Trades.InsertTradeDetail(server, current_trade_id.Value, row["asset_id"].AsInt().Value, row["cface"].AsDouble().Value, row["cface"].AsDouble().Value, row["price"].AsDouble().Value, row["accrued_interest"].AsDouble().Value, row["trade_date"].AsDate().Value, row["settle_date"].AsDate().Value, row["buy_sell"].ToString(), row["account_id"].AsInt().Value, row["counterparty_id"].AsInt().Value, row["tape_id"].AsInt(),null,"TT");

                eta.IncrementAndReport();
            }
            PistonLib.Trades.ProcessTrades(server);
            XtraMessageBox.Show("Trade ID: " + current_trade_id,"Done!");
        }

        private void btnValidateTrades_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

        }

        private void btnViewAllTrades_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            DataTable all_trades = PistonLib.Trades.GetTradeDetail(server, null);
            QuickView qv = new QuickView();
            qv.InitAndShowLazy(server, all_trades, "All Trade Detail", null);
        }
    }
}

namespace PistonControls
{
    public partial class ctrlTrash : ITabBase
    {
        public ctrlTrash()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        PistonGrid _issues;
        public override void Init(string server, GridHelper.GridSetSearchGrid action, CommonInterfaces.Delegates.NewAssetSelected nas)
        {
            base.Init(server, action, nas);

        }


        public override void RefreshTab(string asset, bool force)
        {


        }

        private void btnLoadBuilders_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            string base_location = "C:\\Users\\DanFoster\\Saluda Grade Advisory LLC\\Asset Management - GRADE 2023-RTL3\\Reinvestment Loan Trades\\Purchases\\";
            string[] draw_directories = System.IO.Directory.GetDirectories(base_location, "*- DRAWS - BC*",System.IO.SearchOption.AllDirectories);
            int loaded = 0;
            DXETA eta = new DXETA(draw_directories.Length, null, this.ParentForm);
            foreach (string draw_folder in draw_directories)
            {
                string[] files = System.IO.Directory.GetFiles(draw_folder, "*Budget*Request*", System.IO.SearchOption.AllDirectories);
                eta.IncrementAndReport();
                foreach (string file in files)
                {
                    if (file.ContainsIns("internal"))
                        continue;
                    int? loaded_num = PistonLib.Transactions.LoadBuilderTransactions(server, file);
                    if (null == loaded_num)
                        continue;
                    
                    else
                        loaded += loaded_num.Value;
                }
            }
             XtraMessageBox.Show("Loaded: " + loaded);
        }
    }
}

        GridHelper _users;
        GridHelper _userroles;
        public override void Init(string server, GridHelper.GridSetSearchGrid action, CommonInterfaces.Delegates.NewAssetSelected nas)
        {
            base.Init(server, action, nas);
            _users = new GridHelper(gridUsers, server, true, action);
            _userroles = new GridHelper(gridUserRole,server, true, action);
            _users.ShowFindPanel();
            PistonControls.PistonCustomPopups.GetPistonInstance(_users).RegisterPopupsInternal(nas, null, null);

            Dictionary<string, string> colmap = new Dictionary<string, string>{ { "user_id", "id" }};

            _users.SetupGenericLazyTable("Users", "id", true, colmap, null, null, null);
            CustomPopups.GetInstance(_users).RegisterEditGridPopup(SetUserEditable);

            Dictionary<string, string> userMap = new Dictionary<string, string> { { "useraccountrolemap_id", "id" } };

           _userroles.SetupGenericLazyTable("UserAccountRoleMap", "id", true, userMap, null, null, null);
            CustomPopups.GetInstance(_userroles).RegisterEditGridPopup(SetUserAccountRoleEditable);
            _users.SetPostProcess(PostProcessRow);

        }

        private void PostProcessRow(DataRow row)
        {
            Database.DBCache.GetInstance().Pool.Clear();
        }
        public void SetUserAccountRoleEditable()
    {
        _userroles.SetEditable("userrole_id,user_id,account_id,title_override", null);
        _userroles.ToggleEmbeddedNavigator(true);
    }
    public void SetUserEditable()
    {
        _users.SetEditable("user_id,first_name,last_name,email,title,account_id", null);
        _users.ToggleEmbeddedNavigator(true);
    }

    public override void RefreshTab(string hei_id, bool force)
        {
            Task.Run(() => RefreshUsers());
            Task.Run(() => RefreshUserRole());
        }

        public void RefreshUserRole()
        {
            int? user_id = _users.GetActiveRowValueNullable<int>("user_id");
            DataTable uar = PistonLib.Users.UserAccountRoles(server,user_id,chkShowAllRoles.Checked);
            DataTable roles = PistonLib.Users.GetAllRoles(server);
            DataTable accounts = PistonLib.Accounts.GetAccountList(server, false);
            DataTable users = PistonLib.Users.GetUsers(server, false);

            _userroles.SetGrid(uar, "userrole_id,user_id,account_id,title_override,account_id");

            _userroles.SetUpDropdown(roles, "userrole_id", "role", "userrole_id");
            _userroles.SetUpDropdown(accounts, "account_id", "name", "account_id");
            _userroles.SetUpDropdown(users, "user_id", "full_name", "user_id");

        }
        public void RefreshUsers()
        {
            DataTable users = PistonLib.Users.GetUsers(server, false);
            string cols = "first_name,last_name,email,title,account_id";
            _users.SetGrid(users, cols);

            DataTable accounts = PistonLib.Accounts.GetAccountList(server, false);
            _users.SetUpDropdown(accounts, "account_id", "name", "account_id");
        }

        private void chkShowAllRoles_CheckedChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            RefreshUserRole();
        }

        private void viewUsers_SelectionChanged(object sender, DevExpress.Data.SelectionChangedEventArgs e)
        {
            RefreshUserRole();
        }
    }
}

        GridHelper _pending;
        GridHelper _wire;
        public override void Init(string server, GridHelper.GridSetSearchGrid action, CommonInterfaces.Delegates.NewAssetSelected nas)
        {
            base.Init(server, action, nas);
            _wire = new GridHelper(gridWireSetup, server, true, action);
            _pending = new GridHelper(gridPending,server, true, action);

            _pending.ShowFindPanel();

            PistonControls.PistonCustomPopups.GetPistonInstance(_wire).RegisterPopupsInternal(nas, null, null);
            PistonControls.PistonCustomPopups.GetPistonInstance(_pending).RegisterPopupsInternal(nas, null, null);
            _wire.SetupGenericLazyTable("Wires", "id", true, new Dictionary<string, string>{ { "wire_id","id"} }, null, null, null);
            CustomPopups.GetInstance(_wire).RegisterEditGridPopup(null, "wiretemplate_id,wire_amount,reference,linker_id,value_date,wiretype_id");
            _wire.SetPreProcess(PreProcessRow);
        }

        int? selected_linker_id;
        private void PreProcessRow(DataRow row)
        {
            if (row.RowState == DataRowState.Added)
            {
                row["linker_id"] = selected_linker_id;
                row["value_date"] = _pending.GetFocusedRowValue<DateTime>("value_date");
                row["wiretype_id"] = _pending.GetFocusedRowValue<int>("wiretype_id");   
            }
        }
        public override void RefreshTab(string hei_id, bool force)
        {
            Task.Run(() => RefreshPending());
            
        }

        public void RefreshPending()
        {
            
            var tbl = PistonLib.Wires.GetWireSetupSummary(server);
            string cols = "id,type,wire_desc,value_date,due,allocated,remaining_to_allocate";
            _pending.SetGrid(tbl, cols);

        }
        public void RefreshWireDetail()
        {
            int? linker_id = _pending.GetFocusedRowValueNullable<int>("linker_id");
            DataTable tbl = null;
            if(null != linker_id)
            {
                tbl = PistonLib.Wires.GetWireDetail(server, linker_id.Value);
                
                
                
                string cols = $"wire_id,account,wiretemplate_id,beneficiary_name,bank_routing_number,account_number,ffc,wire_amount,account_id,reference";
                
                
                _wire.SetGrid(tbl, cols);

                DataTable templates = PistonLib.Wires.GetWireTemplates(server, null, true);
                _wire.SetUpDropdown(templates, "wiretemplate_id", "nickname", "wiretemplate_id", new string[] { "account", "nickname","public_desc" }, 600);

                DataTable accounts = PistonLib.Accounts.GetAccountList(server,true,null);
                _wire.SetUpDropdown(accounts,"account_id", "name", "account_id", new string[] { "name", "nickname" }, null);

                _wire.ShowSums("wire_amount", "{0:C}");

            }
            
        }

        private void chkShowAllRoles_CheckedChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            
        }

        private void viewUsers_SelectionChanged(object sender, DevExpress.Data.SelectionChangedEventArgs e)
        {
            selected_linker_id = _pending.GetFocusedRowValueNullable<int>("linker_id");
            RefreshWireDetail();
        }
    }

--- FILE: Saluda\PistonControls\CustomDoubleClicks.cs ---
namespace PistonControls
{
    public class CustomDoubleClicks
    {
        
        string server;

        
        
        
        
        
        
        public CustomDoubleClicks(string server)
        {
            this.server = server;
        }


       
        public void DoubleClickAsset(GridView view, GridHitInfo info)
        {
            if (null == info.Column)
                return;
            string clicked = info.Column.FieldName.ToLower();

            if (null != clicked && view.Columns.ContainsColumn("address_full"))
            {
                ViewInGoogleInternal(this.server, view, GOOGLE_MAP.EARTH);
            }
            else if (null != clicked && view.Columns.ContainsColumn("asset_id"))
            {
                List<int> asset_ids = view.GetActiveRowList<int>("asset_id", true);
                NewColor nc = new NewColor();
                nc.Init(server, null);
                nc.PopulateAssets(asset_ids); 
                nc.SetDefaultColorType(1);
                nc.ShowDialog();
            }
        }

        
        

        

        public enum GOOGLE_MAP { EARTH, MAPS }
        public static void ViewInGoogleInternal(string server, GridView view, GOOGLE_MAP GM)
        {
            List<string> addresses = new List<string>();

            if (view.Columns.ContainsColumn("asset_id") && !view.Columns.ContainsColumn("address_full"))
            {
                List<int> asset_ids = view.GetActiveRowList<int>("asset_id", true);

                foreach (int asset_id in asset_ids)
                {
                    string address_full = PistonLib.Assets.GetSingleAttribute<string>(server, asset_id.ToString(), "address_full", true, PistonLib.Assets.ASSET_ID_SEARCH.ASSET_ID);
                    if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(address_full))
                    {
                        XtraMessageBox.Show("No Address in Piston", asset_id.ToString());
                        return;
                    }
                    addresses.Add(address_full);
                }
            }
            if (view.Columns.ContainsColumn("address_full"))
                addresses = view.GetActiveRowList<string>("address_full", true);
     

            foreach (string address in addresses)
            {
                string url = null;
                if (GM == GOOGLE_MAP.MAPS)
                    url = $"https:
                else if (GM == GOOGLE_MAP.EARTH)
                {
                    url = $"https:
                }
                UtilsLib.FileLib.SpawnProcess(url, true, true);
            }
        }
    }
}

        public static PistonCustomPopups GetPistonInstance(GridHelper gh)
        {
            if (!_instance.ContainsKey(gh))
            {
                _instance.Add(gh, new PistonCustomPopups(gh, gh._server));
            }
            return _instance[gh];
        }

        public PistonCustomPopups(GridHelper gh,string server) : base(gh,server)

        {

            base.RegisterPopupsInternal(nas, writer, c);
            _gc.AppendPopup(this._view, DefaultPistonPopups);
            
            _gc.GridControl.ViewRegistered += SetupPistonPopups;
        }

            _gc.GridControl.ViewRegistered += SetupPistonPopups;

        {

            
            
            GridView view = e.HitInfo.View;
            _popup_view = view;

                        docconfigs.Items.Add(viewFolder);

                {
