        public void _genStrats(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {


            GridView v = _popup_view;
            int tape_id = v.GetActiveRowValue<int>("tape_id", true, true);
            string account_name = PistonLib.Tapes.GetSingleAttribute<string>(server, tape_id, "account_name", true);
            string template = Database.Common.GetGlobal(server, "STRATS_TEMPLATE", true, true);
            string xll_location = XLUtils.GetXLLLocation(server);
            string strat_name = $"{account_name} - Tape #{tape_id}";
            var vars = new Dictionary<string, object> { { "tape_id", tape_id }, { "strat_name", strat_name } };
            string s = XL.Macro.RunMacroAndDepart(xll_location, template, "GenerateStrats", vars, null,true);
            
        }

        void _deleteColor(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            GridView v = _popup_view;
            List<int> color_ids = v.GetActiveRowList<int>("color_id", true);
            foreach (int color_id in color_ids)
            {
                PistonLib.Color.DeleteColor(server, color_id);
            }

            XtraMessageBox.Show($"Deleted {color_ids.Count} pieces of color");
        }




        void _tradeTicket(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            GridView v = _popup_view;
            int tape_id = v.GetActiveRowList<int>("tape_id", true)[0];
            TradeTicket tt = new TradeTicket();
            tt.Init(server);
            tt.EnableNewTrade();
            tt.PopulateTradeFromTicket(tape_id,null);
            tt.ShowDialog();
        }

        void _editTape(object sender,EventArgs e)
        {
            GridView v = base._gc._view;
            int tape_id = v.GetActiveRowList<int>("tape_id", true)[0];
            DataTable tape = PistonLib.Tapes.GetTapeConfig(this.server, tape_id);
            DXHelper.Forms.LazyTableEditor le = new DXHelper.Forms.LazyTableEditor();
            le.Init(server, tape, "account_id,asOf,cutoff_date,tapetype_id,note", "Tapes","id", "cutoff_date,note,tapetype_id,account_id,asOf",false,new Dictionary<string, string> { { "tape_id", "id" } },null);
            DataTable accounts = PistonLib.Accounts.GetAccountList(server, true);
            le.SetupDropDown(accounts, "account_id", "name", "account_id");
            DataTable tape_types = PistonLib.Tapes.GetTapeTypes(server);
            le.SetupDropDown(tape_types, "tapetype_id", "type", "tapetype_id");

            le.Show();
        }


        void _batchSell(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            GridView v = base._gc._view;
            List<int> tape_ids = v.GetActiveRowList<int>("tape_id", true);

            DXETA eta = new DXETA(tape_ids.Count, null, this._parent_form);
            foreach (int tape_id in tape_ids)
            {
                DataTable tape = PistonLib.Tapes.GetTape(server,tape_id);
                
                
                
                
                
                string account_id_str = tape.Columns["deal"].FirstNonNullValue<string>();
                
                int? account_id = PistonLib.Accounts.GetAccountId(server, ((DXMenuItem)sender).Tag.ToString());
                int counterparty_id = PistonLib.Tapes.GetGeneric<int>(server, tape_id,"account_id");
                if (null == account_id)
                    XtraMessageBox.Show($"Couldn't match account: {account_id_str}");
                
                
                if (null == counterparty_id || null == account_id)
                    return;
                DateTime trade_date = PistonLib.Tapes.GetSingleAttribute<DateTime>(server, tape_id, "asOf", false);
                int trade_id = Database.Common.GetNextId(server, "TRADE_ID");
                
                eta.IncrementAndReport();
                if (!tape.Columns.Contains("trade_date"))
                    tape.Columns.Add("trade_date", typeof(DateTime));
                foreach (DataRow l in tape.Rows)
                {
                    if(l["asset_id"] == DBNull.Value || l["purchased_upb"] == DBNull.Value || l["price"] == DBNull.Value || l["accrued_interest"] == DBNull.Value || l["loan_id"] == DBNull.Value)
                    {
                        string msg = $"LOAN ID: {l["loan_id"]}\nPURCHASED UPB: {l["purchased_upb"]}\nPRICE: {l["price"]}\nACCRUED INTEREST: {l["accrued_interest"]}";
                        XtraMessageBox.Show(msg, $"Required Field Blank - Tape ID: {tape_id}  (Loan ID copied to clipboard)");
                        System.Windows.Forms.Clipboard.SetText(l["loan_id"] as string);
                        return;
                    }
                    if (DBNull.Value == l["trade_date"] && DBNull.Value != l["settlement_date"])
                        l["trade_date"] = l["settlement_date"];

                    List<string> missing_required = l.BlankColsFromCSV("asset_id,purchased_upb,price,accrued_interest,trade_date,settlement_date");
                    if(missing_required.Count > 0)
                    {
                        string msg = $"Missing required fields:\n{string.Join("\n", missing_required)}";
                        XtraMessageBox.Show(msg, $"Required Field Blank - Tape ID: {tape_id}  (Loan ID copied to clipboard)");
                        System.Windows.Forms.Clipboard.SetText(l["loan_id"] as string);
                        return;
                    }   
                    PistonLib.Trades.InsertTradeDetail(server, trade_id, l["asset_id"].AsInt().Value, l["purchased_upb"].AsDouble().Value, l["purchased_upb"].AsDouble().Value, l["price"].AsDouble().Value, l["accrued_interest"].AsDouble().Value, l["trade_date"].AsDate().Value, l["settlement_date"].AsDate().Value, "B", account_id.Value,counterparty_id,tape_id,null,"TT");
                   
                }
                
                
            }
            PistonLib.Trades.ProcessTrades(server);
            XtraMessageBox.Show("Done!");
        }

        void _reloadTape(object send, EventArgs e)
        {
            GridView v = base._gc._view;
            List<int> tape_ids = v.GetActiveRowList<int>("tape_id", true);
            
            string directory_hack = @"C:\Users\DanFoster\Saluda Grade Advisory LLC\Saluda Grade Corp - DanApps\03 - Deals\GRADE 2023-RTL3\";
             var sure = XtraMessageBox.Show("Are you absolutely sure?", "Hi", MessageBoxButtons.YesNo);
            if (sure == DialogResult.Yes)
            {
                var output = new PistonLib.Tapes.TapeLoaderHelper();
                foreach (int tape_id in tape_ids)
                {
                    int tapetype_id = PistonLib.Tapes.GetGeneric<int>(server, tape_id, "tapetype_id");
                    int account_id = PistonLib.Tapes.GetGeneric<int>(server, tape_id, "account_id");
                    DateTime cutoff_date = PistonLib.Tapes.GetGeneric<DateTime>(server, tape_id, "cutoff_date");
                    DateTime asOf = PistonLib.Tapes.GetGeneric<DateTime>(server, tape_id, "asOf");
                    int tapemap_id = PistonLib.Tapes.GetGeneric<int>(server, tape_id, "tapemap_id");
                    string filename = PistonLib.Tapes.GetGeneric<string>(server, tape_id, "filename");
                    string full_filename = System.IO.Directory.GetFiles(directory_hack, $"*{filename}")[0];

                    output = PistonLib.Tapes.CreateAndLoadTape(server, true, tapetype_id, account_id, cutoff_date, asOf, $"Reload of Tape {tape_id}", tapemap_id, full_filename, null, null,true);
                    XtraMessageBox.Show($"Tape ID: {output.tape_id}", "DONE!");
                  }
                
            }
        }


        public void SetupWireInternal(int trade_id)
        {

            List<int> tradedetail_ids = PistonLib.Trades.GetTradeDetailIds(server, trade_id);
            if (tradedetail_ids.Count > 1)
            {
                 var dr = XtraMessageBox.Show("You're about to setup wires for ALL counterparties for this trade id", "Cool?", MessageBoxButtons.YesNo);
                if (dr != DialogResult.Yes)
                    return;
            }
            List<int> wires = new List<int>();

            var trades = PistonLib.Trades.GetTrades(server, trade_id);
            int? wiretemplatetype_id = trades.FirstOrDefault().wiretemplatetype_id;

            var wire_grouped = from trade in trades group trade by trade.counterparty_id into t select new { amount = t.Sum(n => n.net_proceeds), counterparty_id = t.First().counterparty_id, settle_date = t.First().settle_date, wire_reference = t.Distinct().Aggregate("",(current,s) => current.Trim() + (s.loan_id+ ", "))};

            foreach (var wire in wire_grouped)
            {

                int linker_id = PistonLib.Linker.GetLinkOrAddIfNot(server, 1, trade_id);
                var wire_template_ids = PistonLib.Wires.GetWireTemplates(server, wire.counterparty_id, wiretemplatetype_id);
                if(null == wire_template_ids || wire_template_ids.Count == 0)
                {
                    wire_template_ids = PistonLib.Wires.GetWireTemplates(server, wire.counterparty_id, null);
                }
                double? wire_amt = wire.amount;
      
                
                if (wire_template_ids.Count > 1)
                    wire_amt = null;
                string wire_ref = wire.wire_reference;
                if(null != wire_ref && wire_ref.Length > 1)
                {
                    wire_ref = wire_ref.Substring(0, wire_ref.Length - 2);
                    if(wire_ref.Contains(','))
                        wire_ref = String.Join(", ", wire_ref.Split(',').Distinct().ToArray()).Trim();
                 }   

                if(wire.wire_reference?.Length > 200)
                {
                    wire_ref = $"Total Loans: {tradedetail_ids.Count}";
                }
                foreach (int wire_template_id in wire_template_ids)
                {
                    int wire_id = PistonLib.Wires.SetupWire(server, wire_template_id, wire_amt, wire.settle_date, linker_id, wire.counterparty_id, wire_ref);
                }
                XtraMessageBox.Show("Done - go to Wire Maint to complete...");
            }
            
            
            

            
            

            
            
            
            
            
            
            
        }
        void _setupWire(object sender, EventArgs a)
        {
            
            int trade_id = base._gc._view.GetActiveRowValue<int>("trade_id", true, true);
            SetupWireInternal(trade_id);
        }



        void _linkTrades(object sender, EventArgs a)
        {
            List<long> draw_list = _view.GetFocusedRowList<long>("draw_id", true);
            List<int> tradedetail_ids = PistonLib.Trades.GetDetailIdsFromDrawIds(server, draw_list, true);
            if(draw_list.Count != tradedetail_ids.Count)
            {
                XtraMessageBox.Show("Couldn't match some of the trades OR draws already associated with a trade - tell Dan");
                return;
            }
            int new_trade_id = Trades.LinkTrades(server, tradedetail_ids);

            SetupWireInternal(new_trade_id);

            XtraMessageBox.Show("Trade: #" + new_trade_id);
        }


        void _resetWire(object sender, EventArgs a)
        {
            int? linker_id = null;
            if (base._gc.ContainsColumn("linker_id"))
            {
                linker_id = base._gc._view.GetActiveRowValueNullable<int>("linker_id", true);
            }
            else if (base._gc.ContainsColumn("trade_id"))
            {
                int? trade_id = base._gc._view.GetActiveRowValueNullable<int>("trade_id", true);
                if (null != trade_id)
                    linker_id = PistonLib.Linker.GetLinkerIdFromTrade(server, trade_id.Value);
            }
            if (null == linker_id)
            {
                XtraMessageBox.Show("No Linker ID found - tell Dan");
            }
            else
            {
                PistonLib.Linker.ResetWire(server, linker_id.Value);
                XtraMessageBox.Show("Wire Deported.");
            }
        }

        }

            _docGenInternal(3,null);
        }

        void _docGenCustody(object sender, EventArgs a)
        {
            _docGenInternal(4, 13);
        }
        void _docGenInternal(int docpackagetype_id,int? docconfig_ids_only)
        {
            int? relevant_id = null;
            int? account_id = null;
            List<int> assets = null;

            if (docpackagetype_id == 2 || docpackagetype_id == 3)
            {
                relevant_id = base._gc._view.GetActiveRowValueNullable<int>("trade_id", true).Value;
                if (null == relevant_id)
                {
                    XtraMessageBox.Show("Blank Trade ID - Tell Dan");
                    return;
                }
                account_id = PistonLib.Trades.GetSingleAttributeFromTrade<int>(server, relevant_id.Value, "account_id", true);
            }

            if (docpackagetype_id == 4)
            {
                assets = base._gc._view.GetActiveRowList<int>("asset_id", true, true);
                List<int> owners = PistonLib.Assets.GetOwnerCalc(server, assets);
                if (owners.Count == 1)
                {
                    relevant_id = owners[0];
                }
                else
                {
                    XtraMessageBox.Show("Doesn't work with multiple account owners");
                }
            }

            
            int? docpackage_id = PistonLib.Docs.GetDocPackage(server, account_id, docpackagetype_id);
            List<string> files = new List<string>();
            DXETA eta = new DXETA(0, null, this._parent_form);
            string final_path = UtilsLib.PathLib.CreateNewTempDir();
            if(null == docpackage_id)
            {
                XtraMessageBox.Show("No Doc Package ID Associated");
                return;
            }
            if (null != docpackage_id || (null == docpackage_id && null != docconfig_ids_only))
            {
                UtilsLib.ProcessHelper.SpawnAsync(final_path);
                try
                {
                    files = PistonLib.Docs.GenerateDocPackage(server, docpackage_id, relevant_id, final_path, eta, true, assets, new List<int?> { docconfig_ids_only });
                    XtraMessageBox.Show("Done!");
                }
                catch(Exception e)
                {
                    XtraMessageBox.Show(e.Message);
                    return;
                }
            }
            else
            {
                XtraMessageBox.Show("Somepin Jacked");
            }
            
        }

        }

            string cols = "asset_id,loan_id,property_address,property_city,property_state,property_zip,original_term,remaining_term,lien,original_loan_amt,purchased_upb,cutoff_date,servicer,originator,dq_status,loan_status,gross_rate,address_full,last_account,product_1,product_2,product_3,total_committed_amount,ltc,ltarv,fico,units,next_due_date,origination_date,current_maturity_date,pass_thru_rate,loan_purpose,property_type,cltv,borrower_experience,original_maturity_date,most_recent_primary_borrower_fico,cltv_orig,originator_dti,property_state_full,loan_age,loan_type\r\n";
            asset_history.CopyAndTrimColumns(cols);
            DXHelper.Forms.QuickView f = new DXHelper.Forms.QuickView();

        void _CreateTape(object sender, EventArgs a)
        {
            GridView v = base._gc._view;
            List<int> assets = v.GetActiveRowList<int>("asset_id",true);
            DataTable tapedetail = PistonLib.TapeDetail.GetCustomTape(server,assets);
            var results = PistonLib.Tapes.TransformTape(server, null, tapedetail, false, false, true);
            
            int tape_id = PistonLib.Tapes.CreateTape(server,5,null, DateTime.Now, DateTime.Now,"Custom Tape - Piston",null,null);

            results.clean_tape.Columns.AddColumnWithDefaultIgnoreIfAlreadyExists<int>("tape_id", tape_id);
            if(results.clean_tape.Rows.Count != assets.Count)
            {
                XtraMessageBox.Show("Error - not all assets made it into the tape.  Canceled.");
                return;
            }
            List<string> sqls = Database.QueryBuilder.SQLInsertValidate(results.clean_tape, server, "TapeDetail", true).lines;

            Query q = new Query(null, server);
            q.ExecuteBatch(sqls, 25, null);
            PistonLib.Tapes.ProcessTapes(server, tape_id, assets);
            
            XtraMessageBox.Show("Done!", $"Tape ID: {tape_id}");
        }
        void _viewDeleteRemit(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            GridView v = base._gc._view;
            if (null != v.Columns["tape_id"])
            {
                List<int> tape_ids = v.GetActiveRowList<int>("tape_id", true);
                
                foreach (int tape_id in tape_ids)
                {
                    List<int> trade_ids = PistonLib.Trades.GetTradesFromTapeId(server, tape_id);
                    if(trade_ids.Count == 1)
                    {
                        var dr = XtraMessageBox.Show($"Trade ID: {String.Join(Environment.NewLine, trade_ids)}", "Delete trades too?",MessageBoxButtons.YesNoCancel);
                        if(dr == DialogResult.Yes)
                        {
                            foreach (int trade_id in trade_ids)
                            {
                                PistonLib.Trades.DeleteTrade(server, trade_id);
                                PistonLib.Trades.ProcessTrades(server);
                            }
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            XtraMessageBox.Show("Suit your self - we're done here.");
                            return;
                        }
                    }
                    List<int> assets = PistonLib.TapeDetail.GetAllAssets(server, tape_id);
                    PistonLib.Tapes.DeleteTape(this.server, tape_id);
                    
                }
                 XtraMessageBox.Show("Done - Refresh Tab (F5)");
            }

        }
    }

namespace PistonControls.Forms
{
    public partial class NewColor : DevExpress.XtraEditors.XtraForm
    {
        public NewColor()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        GridHelper _detail;
        string server;
        public void Init(string server,int? color_id)
        {
            _detail = new GridHelper(gridNotes, server, true,null);
            this.server = server;
            this._color_id = color_id;
            assets = new DataTable();
            assets.Columns.Add("asset_id", typeof(int));
            assets.Columns.Add("note", typeof(string));
        }

        public void RefreshTab()
        {
            Task.Run(() => PopulateAccounts());
            Task.Run(() => PopulateTypes());
        }

        DataTable assets = new DataTable();
        public void PopulateAssets(List<int> asset_ids)
        {
            
            assets.Rows.Clear();
            if (null != asset_ids)
            {
                foreach (int s in asset_ids)
                {
                    assets.Rows.Add(s);
                }
            }
            _detail.SetGrid(assets);
            _detail.SetEditable("note",null);
        }

        private int? _color_id;
        public void PopulateColor(int color_id)
        {
            PistonLib.Color c = new PistonLib.Color(this.server);
            c.Populate(color_id);
            drpAccounts.EditValue = c.account_id;
            drpColorTypes.EditValue = c.colortype_id;
            memoEdit1.EditValue = c.note;
            _color_id = color_id;
            PopulateAssets(new List<int> { c.asset_id.Value });
            this.Text = "***EDITING EXISTING COLOR***";
        }
        public void SetDefaultColorType(int colortype_id)
        {
            drpColorTypes.EditValue = colortype_id;
        }
        private void PopulateTypes()
        {
            DataTable types = PistonLib.Color.GetColorTypes(server);
            drpColorTypes.PopulateLookup(types, "type", "colortype_id");
        }
        private void PopulateAccounts()
        {
            DataTable accounts = PistonLib.Accounts.GetAccountList(server, true);
            drpAccounts.PopulateLookup(accounts, "name", "account_id", false);
        }
        private void drpMapping_Properties_EditValueChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

        }

        private void simpleButton1_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

            foreach (DataRow row in assets.Rows)
            {
                int? asset_id = row["asset_id"].AsInt();
                PistonLib.Color.InsertUpdateColor(server, _color_id, drpColorTypes.EditValue.AsInt().Value, asset_id, memoEdit1.Text, drpAccounts.EditValue.AsInt());
            }
            this.Close();
            XtraMessageBox.Show($"Added {assets.Rows.Count} Color!");
        }

        private void NewColor_Load(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            RefreshTab();
        }

        private void memoEdit1_EditValueChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            btnSave.Enabled = memoEdit1.Text.Length > 0 && null != drpColorTypes.EditValue;
            assets.Columns["note"].Expression = $"'{memoEdit1.Text.Replace("'","''")}'";
            assets.AcceptChanges();
        }
    }
}

--- FILE: Saluda\PistonControls\Forms\NewMapping.cs ---
namespace PistonControls.Forms
{
    public partial class NewMapping : DevExpress.XtraEditors.XtraForm
    {
        public NewMapping()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }
        string server;
        GridHelper _mapping;
        GridHelper _maps;
        CommonInterfaces.Delegates.NewAssetSelected _nas;
        public void Init(string server, GridHelper.GridSetSearchGrid action, CommonInterfaces.Delegates.NewAssetSelected nas)
        {
            this.server = server;
            _mapping = new GridHelper(gridMapDetail, server, true, action);
            _maps = new GridHelper(gridMaps, server, true, action);
            _mapping.ToggleSearchPanel(true);
            _nas = nas; ;
            PistonControls.PistonCustomPopups.GetPistonInstance(_mapping).RegisterPopupsInternal(nas, null, null);
            PistonControls.PistonCustomPopups.GetPistonInstance(_maps).RegisterPopupsInternal(nas, null, null);

            _maps.ShowFindPanel();
            CustomPopups.GetInstance(_mapping).RegisterEditGridPopup(SetMappingDetailEditable);
            _mapping.SetupGenericLazyTable("TapeMapDetail", "id", true, new Dictionary<string, string> { { "tapemapdetail_id", "id" } }, null, new List<string> { "row_color", "sample_data", "bounds","id"}, null);
            _mapping.SetPreProcess(PreProcessRow);

            CustomPopups.GetInstance(_maps).RegisterEditGridPopup(SetTapeMapEditable);
            _maps.SetupGenericLazyTable("TapeMaps", "id", true, new Dictionary<string, string> { { "tapemap_id", "id" } }, null, null , new List<string> { "id" });
            _maps.SetPreProcess(PreProcessRow);
            _maps.SetPostProcess(PostProcessRow);
            viewMaps.InitNewRow += ViewMaps_InitNewRow;


        }

        private void ViewMaps_InitNewRow(object sender, DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Grid.InitNewRowEventArgs e)
        {
            DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Grid.GridView view = sender as GridView;
            view.SetRowCellValue(e.RowHandle, "hide", false);
        }

        public void RefreshControl()
        {
            

            PopulateTapeMaps();
        }

        private void PostProcessRow(DataRow row)
        {
            if (row.RowState != DataRowState.Deleted)
                _tapemap_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["id"]);
            else
                _tapemap_id = null;
            RefreshControl();
        }
        private void PreProcessRow(DataRow row)
        {
           if (row.RowState == DataRowState.Added && DBNull.Value == row["id"])
            {
                
                
                _maps.SetFocusedRowValue("tapemap_id", row["id"]);
                if (row.Table.Columns.Contains("tapemap_id"))
                    row["tapemap_id"] = _tapemap_id;
                
            }
        }

        public void PopulateTapeMaps()
        {
            DataTable maps = PistonLib.Maps.GetMapTable(server, chkShowAll.Checked);
            string cols = "name,account_id,note,hide";
            _maps.SetGrid(maps,cols);
            DataTable accounts = PistonLib.Accounts.GetAccountList(server, false);
            _maps.SetUpDropdown(accounts,"account_id", "name", "account_id", new string[] { "name" });
            
        }
        public void SetTapeMap(int tapemap_id)
        {
            bool success = _maps.FindAndFocusOnId("tapemap_id", tapemap_id);
        }
        int? __tapemapd_id;
        public int? _tapemap_id
        {
            get { return __tapemapd_id; }
            set
            {
                if (value != _tapemap_id)
                {
                    __tapemapd_id = value;
                    if(null != value)
                        RefreshDetail(__tapemapd_id.Value);
                }
                
            }
        }

        
        
        



        


        public void SetTapeMapEditable()
        {
            _maps.SetEditable("account_id,name,note,hide", null);
            _maps.ToggleEmbeddedNavigator(true);
        }

        public void SetMappingDetailEditable()
        {
            SetMappingDetailEditable(true);
        }
        public void SetMappingDetailEditable(bool enable)
        {
            _mapping.SetEditable("field,db_field,correction_mult,tapemap_id".Split(','), null,enable);
            _mapping.ToggleEmbeddedNavigator(enable);
        }


        private void ctrlTableMapping_Load(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            
        }

        private void drpMapping_EditValueChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            
            
        }

        public void RefreshDetail(int tapemap_id)
        {
            DataTable mappings = PistonLib.Tapes.GetTapeMapDetail(server, tapemap_id);
            mappings.Columns.Add("sample_data", typeof(object));
            _mapping.SetGrid(mappings, "field,db_field,correction_mult,sample_data,bounds");

            btnAutoMap.Enabled = mappings.Rows.Count > 0;

            DataTable db_fields = Database.DBUtils.GetTableColumnsTable(server, "TapeDetail",true);
            _mapping.SetUpDropdown(db_fields, "db_field", "column_name", "column_name", new string[] { "column_name" });
            
            btnLoadFromFile.Enabled = mappings.Rows.Count == 0;
            
        }

        private void drpMapping_TextChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
        }



        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        Dictionary<string, object> sample_values = new Dictionary<string, object>();
        private void btnLoadFromFile_Click_1(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            _mapping.DisableEditing();
            var tbl = XL.FileReaderSimple.PickAndRead("Pick Tape", "xlsx", false, true);
            sample_values.Clear();
            if (null == tbl.Table)
                return;
            foreach (DataColumn col in tbl.Table.Columns)
            {
                object o = col.FirstNonNullValue<object>();
                sample_values.Add(col.ColumnName, o);
                PistonLib.Maps.InsertUpdateTapeMap(server, _tapemap_id.Value, col.ColumnName);
            }
        }

        public void PopulateSampleValuesFromExcel()
        {
            var tbl = XL.FileReaderSimple.PickAndRead("Pick Tape", "xlsx", false, true);
            sample_values.Clear();
            if (null == tbl.Table)
                return;
            foreach (DataColumn col in tbl.Table.Columns)
            {
                object o = col.FirstNonNullValue<object>();
                sample_values.Add(col.ColumnName, o);
                
            }
        }


        public void PopulateSampleValuesInGrid()
        {
            DataTable underlying = _mapping.GetUnderlyingTable(null);
            foreach (DataRow row in underlying.Rows)
            {
                string field = row["field"].ToString();
                if (sample_values.ContainsKeyIns(field))
                {
                    
                    row["sample_data"] = sample_values[field];
                }
            }
        }
        private void btnAutoMap_Click_1(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            DataTable tbl = _mapping.GetUnderlyingTable(null);
            
            

            
            List<string> mapped_already = new List<string>();
            
            foreach (DataRow row in tbl.Rows)
            {
                bool changed = false;
                string field = row["field"].ToString();
                string db_field = row["db_field"]?.ToString();
                

                if (sample_values.ContainsKeyIns(field))
                {
                    row["sample_data"] = sample_values[field];
                    row.AcceptChanges();
                }
                
                

                
                {
                    string auto_map = PistonLib.Maps.TryAutoMap(server, field);
                    bool exists_already = PistonLib.Maps.DatabaseMapExists(server, _tapemap_id.Value, auto_map);
                    if (exists_already)
                        continue;
                    if (null != auto_map && !mapped_already.Contains(auto_map))
                    {
                        changed = true;
                        
                        if(!String.IsNullOrEmpty(auto_map))
                            row["db_field"] = auto_map;
                        else if(!String.IsNullOrEmpty(db_field))
                            row["db_field"] = db_field;
                        mapped_already.Add(db_field);
                        _mapping._lt.ForceLazyUpdate(true);
                        _mapping._view.UpdateCurrentRow();
                    }
                }
                if (changed)
                {
                    
                    

                    
                }
            }
            tbl.AcceptChanges();
        }

        
        
        
        
        
        


        private void viewMaps_FocusedRowChanged(object sender, DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Base.FocusedRowChangedEventArgs e)
        {
            
            _tapemap_id = _maps.GetRowValueNullable<int>(e.FocusedRowHandle, "tapemap_id");

        }

        private void btnViewList_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            DataTable fields = Database.DBUtils.GetTableColumnsTable(server, "TapeDetail", true);
            foreach (DataRow row in fields.Rows)
            {
                row["column_name"] = row["column_name"].ToString().ToUpper();
            }
            QuickView qv = new QuickView();
            qv.InitAndShowLazy(server, fields, "Data Field Mapping", null);
            qv.Width = 500;
            
        }

        private void chkShowAll_CheckedChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            PopulateTapeMaps();
        }

        private void btnPopulateSampleData_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            PopulateSampleValuesFromExcel();
            PopulateSampleValuesInGrid();
        }

   
    }
}

namespace PistonControls.Forms
{
    public partial class TradeTicket : DevExpress.XtraEditors.XtraForm
    {
        public TradeTicket()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        public void Init(string server)
        {
            ctrlTrades.Init(server, null, null);
        }

        public void PopulateTradeFromTicket(int tape_id,int? trade_id)
        {
            ctrlTrades.PopulateTape(tape_id);
            ctrlTrades.RefreshTab(trade_id);
        }

        public void PopulateUnallocatedTrades(int tape_id)
        {
            ctrlTrades.PopulateTape(tape_id);
            ctrlTrades.RefreshTab(null);
        }

        public void EnableNewTrade()
        {
            ctrlTrades.EnableNewTrade();
        }
    }
}

--- FILE: Saluda\PistonControls\PistonGrid.cs ---
namespace PistonControls
{
    public class PistonGrid : GridHelper
    {
        public PistonGrid(GridControl gc, string server, bool add_events, GridHelper.GridSetSearchGrid gssg) : base(gc, server, add_events, gssg)
        {

        }

        List<string> color_tables = new List<string>(new string[] { "Color", "Trade History", "Performance History", "Paid Off Assets", "Draws" }); 
        List<string> color_tables_no_link = new List<string>(new string[] { "Paid Off Assets" });

        public bool IsExecuting = false;
        public void AddColorAsync(List<int> asset_ids)
        {

            
            
            IsExecuting = true;
            if (IsExecuting && executingqueries.Count != 0)
            {
                executingqueries.ForEach(n => n.CancelQuery());
            }

            
            
            

            if(true)
            { 
                Query c = PistonLib.Color.GetColorQuery(base._server, asset_ids);
                c.SetTableNames(new List<string> { "Color" });
                c.ExecuteAsync(AddColorSafe);

                Query t = PistonLib.Trades.GetTradesQuery(base._server, asset_ids);
                t.SetTableNames(new List<string> { "Trade History" });
                t.ExecuteAsync(AddColorSafe);

                Query r = PistonLib.TapeDetail.GetTapeDetailSimpleQuery(base._server, asset_ids);
                r.SetTableNames(new List<string> { "Performance History" });
                r.ExecuteAsync(AddColorSafe);

                Query po = PistonLib.Assets.GetPaidOffAssets(base._server, asset_ids);
                po.SetTableNames(new List<string> { "Paid Off Assets" });
                po.ExecuteAsync(AddColorSafe);

                Query dq = PistonLib.Draws.GetDrawQuery(base._server, asset_ids);
                dq.SetTableNames(new List<string> { "Draws" });
                dq.ExecuteAsync(AddColorSafe);

                executingqueries.AddRange(new List<Query> { r, t, c, po, dq });
            }
        }


        List<Query> executingqueries = new List<Query>();


        private string PickColorTable(DataSet incoming_color)
        {
            foreach (string s in color_tables)
            {
                if (incoming_color.Tables.Contains(s))
                    return s;
            }
            return null;
        }

        private bool AllColorReady(DataSet set)
        {
            int tables_included = 0;
            foreach(string s in color_tables)
            {
                if (set.Tables.Contains(s))
                    tables_included++;
            }
            return tables_included == color_tables.Count;
        }

        public Dictionary<int,double> SetupColorPriority(DataSet set)
        {

            List<KeyValuePair<int, double>> priorities = new List<KeyValuePair<int, double>>();

            foreach(string color_table in color_tables)
            {
                var tbl_priorities = set.Tables[color_table].ToDictionaryListUnique<int, double>("asset_id", "color_priority");
                
                

                
                
                foreach (var tp in tbl_priorities)
                {
                    foreach(var val in tp.Value)
                    {
                        priorities.Add(new KeyValuePair<int,double>(tp.Key, val));
                    }    
                }


                
            }
            
            var pair = priorities.GroupBy(n => n.Key).Select(grp => new { asset_id = grp.Key, highest_priority = grp.Min(e => e.Value) }).ToDictionary(n => n.asset_id, n => n.highest_priority);
            return pair;
        }

        

        public void AddColorSafe(DataSet set)
        {
            if (base._view.GridControl.InvokeRequired)
            {
                base._view.GridControl.Invoke(new MethodInvoker(() => { this.AddColor(set); }));
            }
            else
            {
                AddColor(set);
            }
        }

        
        public delegate void FinishDelegate(DataSet finished_set);

        public FinishDelegate finish = null;

        public void SetColorPostProcessing(FinishDelegate finish)
        {
            this.finish = finish;
        }
        public void AddColor(DataSet set)
        {
            bool added_column = false;
            string color_table = PickColorTable(set);
            _DataSet.Tables.Add(set.Tables[color_table].Copy());

            if (!_DataSet.Tables[0].Columns.Contains("row_color"))
            { 
                _DataSet.Tables[0].Columns.Add("row_color", typeof(string));
                added_column = true;
            }
            set.Tables[color_table].TrimBlankColumns();
            bool all_color_ready = AllColorReady(_DataSet);     
            
            if (!all_color_ready)
                return;
            foreach (var order in color_tables)
            {
                if (!color_tables_no_link.Contains(order))
                {
                    var s = base.AddRelationSafe(order, _DataSet.Tables[0].Columns["asset_id"], _DataSet.Tables[order].Columns["asset_id"]);
                }
            }

            
            IsExecuting = false;
            executingqueries.Clear();
            Debug.WriteLine("Processing Color: " + _DataSet.Tables[0].Rows.Count);
            bool any_changed = false;
            var priorities = SetupColorPriority(_DataSet);

            foreach (var col in priorities)
            {

                string row_color = PistonLib.ColorTypes.GetRowColorFromColorPrioirty(_server, col.Value);
                DataRow[] asset_row = _DataSet.Tables[0].Select($"[asset_id] = {col.Key}");
                foreach (var row in asset_row)
                {
                    row["row_color"] = row_color;
                    any_changed = true;
                }
            }
            if (any_changed)
            {
                
                

                _view.LayoutChanged();
            }
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            if (null != this.finish)
                finish(_DataSet);
        }

        public override void _gc_ViewRegistered(object sender, ViewOperationEventArgs e)
        {
            GridView v = e.View as GridView;
            
            
            v.OptionsBehavior.ReadOnly = true;
            SetUpView(v);
            Fields f = Fields.GetInstance(this._server, Database.FieldHelper.GetFieldTableInternal);
            string cols = "";
            if (v.LevelName == "Trade History")
            {
                cols = PistonLib.ColorTypes.GetSingleAttribute<string>(this._server, 3,"csv_cols");
            }
            if (v.LevelName == "Color")
            {
                cols = PistonLib.ColorTypes.GetSingleAttribute<string>(this._server, 1,"csv_cols");
                
            }
            if (v.LevelName == "Performance History")
            {
                cols = PistonLib.ColorTypes.GetSingleAttribute<string>(this._server, 4, "csv_cols");
            }
            if (v.LevelName == "Draws")
            {
                cols = PistonLib.ColorTypes.GetSingleAttribute<string>(this._server, 6, "csv_cols");
            }


            v.CleanColumns(f,cols,false,false,false);

            if (null != v.Columns["note"])
            {
                RepositoryItemMemoEdit color = new RepositoryItemMemoEdit();
                color.WordWrap = true;
                v.Columns["note"].ColumnEdit = color;
                v.AutoFillColumn = v.Columns["note"];
            }
        }
    }
}

            string sql = "select * from vAccounts a where (a.name = @name or a.name_short=@name)";

            q.AddParameter("@name", name);
            q.UseCache = true;
            int? account_id = q.ExecuteSingleNullable<int>("account_id");

            return account_id;

--- FILE: Saluda\PistonLib\Assets.cs ---
namespace PistonLib
{
    public class Assets
    {
        public static DataTable GetAssetSummary(string server,bool use_cache = false)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vAssetsEx a order by update_time desc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.UseCache = use_cache;
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static bool IsAssetID(string asset_id)
        {
            if(String.IsNullOrEmpty(asset_id)) return false;

            if (asset_id.Length == 10 && asset_id.IsInt())
                return true;
            
            return false;
        }


        public static DataSet GetAssetSummarySet(string server, List<int> assets)
        {
            string sql = "select a.*,convert(varchar(30),null) [row_color] from vAssetsEx a order by update_time desc";
            if(null != assets)
                sql = "select a.*,convert(varchar(30),null) [row_color] from vAssetsEx a join @assets ass on (ass.item = a.asset_id or ass.item = try_convert(float,a.loan_id)) order by update_time desc";

            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@assets", assets);
            var tbl = q.Execute();
            tbl.Tables[0].TableName = "loan_schedule";
            return tbl;
        }
        public static DataTable GetAssetSummary(string server, List<int> assets)
        {
            return GetAssetSummarySet(server, assets).Tables[0];
        }
        public static Query GetPaidOffAssets(string server, List<int> asset_ids)
        {
            string sql = "select c.asset_id,ct.row_color,ct.priority [color_priority] from vAssets c join vColorTypes ct on ct.colortype_id = 5 join @assets a on a.item = c.asset_id and c.current_balance = 0";
            if (null == asset_ids)
                sql = "select c.asset_id,ct.row_color,ct.priority [color_priority] from vAssets c join vColorTypes ct on ct.colortype_id = 5 and c.current_balance = 0";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@assets", asset_ids);
            return q;
        }

        public static DataTable GetAssetHistory(string server,int asset_id)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vTapeDetail td where td.asset_id = @asset_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            var tbl = q.ExecuteTable();
            tbl.TrimBlankColumns();
            return tbl;
        }

        private static readonly Lazy<Dictionary<string,int>> lazy = new Lazy<Dictionary<string, int>>(() => new Dictionary<string, int>());

        public static Dictionary<string,int> GetAssetIds(string server,bool use_cache)
        {
            if (use_cache && lazy.Value.Count != 0)
                return lazy.Value;

            string sql = "select upper(loan_id) [loan_id],id [asset_id] from Assets";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.UseCache = false;
            var s = q.ExecuteDictRows<string, int>("loan_id", "asset_id");
            lazy.Value.Clear();
            lazy.Value.AddRange<string, int>(s);
            return lazy.Value;
        }

        public static Dictionary<string, long> GetAssetIdsBatch(string server, bool use_cache,List<string> loan_ids)
        {
            Dictionary<string, long> results = new Dictionary<string, long>();
            foreach(string loan in loan_ids)
            {
                long asset_id = GetAssetId(server, loan,null,null,false).Value;
                if(!results.ContainsKey(loan))
                    results.Add(loan, asset_id);
            }
            return results;
        }

        public static int? GetAssetId(string server,string loan_id,string originator,string property_address,bool insert_if_needed)
        {
            if ((null != loan_id && loan_id.ToUpper() == "TBD") || String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(loan_id))
            {
                loan_id = null;
            }

            Dictionary<string, int> ids = GetAssetIds(server, true);
            if(null != loan_id && ids.ContainsKeyIns(loan_id.Trim()))
            {
                return ids.GetKeyIns<string, int>(loan_id);
            }
            if (insert_if_needed)
            {
                int? asset_id = FindAssetIdFromAddressOriginator(server, originator, property_address);
                if(null == asset_id)
                    asset_id = InsertAssetID(server, loan_id);
                if(null != loan_id)
                    lazy.Value.Add(loan_id, asset_id.Value);
                return asset_id;
            }
            return null;
        }

        public static int? FindAssetIdFromAddressOriginator(string server,string originator,string property_address)
        {
            string sql = "select top 1 asset_id from TapeDetail td where td.property_address = @property_address and td.originator = @originator";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@originator", originator);
            q.AddParameter("@property_address", property_address);
            return q.ExecuteSingleNullable<int>("asset_id");
        }
        public static int InsertAssetID(string  server,string loan_id)
        {
            
            
            if (null != loan_id)
                loan_id = loan_id.ToUpper();
            string sql = "insert into Assets (loan_id) output inserted.id values (@loan_id)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@loan_id", loan_id);
            int asset_id = q.ExecuteSingle<int>();
            return asset_id;
        }

        public static List<int> GetOwnerCalc(string server,List<int> asset_ids)
        {
            return GetListFromAssets(server, asset_ids, "owner_account_id_calc");
        }

        public static List<int> GetListFromAssets(string server, List<int> asset_ids,string db_field)
        {
            string sql = $"select distinct {db_field} from vAssetsEx a join @asset_ids ass on ass.item = a.asset_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_ids", asset_ids);
            return q.ExecuteList<int>(db_field);
        }
        public static T GetSingleAttribute<T>(string server, string asset_id, string db_field, bool use_cache, Nullable<ASSET_ID_SEARCH> search_type)
        {
            CommonLib.ColumnCacher.EnsureColumnsCached(server, "select * from vAssets a where 1=2", "select * from vAssetsEx a where 1=2");
            if (ColumnCacher.Instance.simple.Contains(db_field))
                return GetSingleAttributeSimple<T>(server, asset_id, db_field, use_cache,search_type);
            else
                return GetSingleAttributeComplex<T>(server, asset_id, db_field, use_cache, search_type);
        }
        public static int? FindAssetID<T>(string server, string search_field)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vAssetsEx a where a.property_address = @search_field or a.loan_id = @search_field or convert(varchar(30),a.asset_id) = @search_field";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@search_field", search_field);
            return q.ExecuteSingleNullable<int>("asset_id");
        }

        public static T GetSingleAttributeComplex<T>(string server, string asset_id, string db_field, bool use_cache, Nullable<ASSET_ID_SEARCH> search_type)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vAssetsEx a where (a.asset_id = try_convert(float,@asset_id) or a.loan_id = @asset_id)";
            string parm_name = "@asset_id<varchar>";
            if (null != search_type) {
                if (search_type.Value == ASSET_ID_SEARCH.LOAN_NUM) {
                    sql = "select * from vAssets a where a.loan_id = @asset_id";
                }
                if (search_type.Value == ASSET_ID_SEARCH.ASSET_ID) {
                    sql = "select * from vAssets a where a.asset_id = @asset_id";
                    parm_name = "@asset_id";
                }
            }
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter(parm_name, asset_id);
            q.UseCache = use_cache;
            T t = q.ExecuteSingle<T>(db_field);
            if (ColumnCacher.Instance.es_listo)
            {
                ColumnCacher.Instance.complex.AddRange(q.ColumnListFromTable);
            }
            return t;
        }

        public enum ASSET_ID_SEARCH { ANY, LOAN_NUM, ASSET_ID }
        public static T GetSingleAttributeSimple<T>(string server, string asset_id, string db_field, bool use_cache,Nullable<ASSET_ID_SEARCH> search_type = null)
        {
            
            string sql = "select * from vAssets a where (a.asset_id = try_convert(float,@asset_id) or a.loan_id = @asset_id)";
            string parm_name = "@asset_id<varchar>";
            if(null != search_type)
            {
                if(search_type.Value == ASSET_ID_SEARCH.LOAN_NUM)
                {
                    sql = "select * from vAssets a where a.loan_id = @asset_id";
                }
                if (search_type.Value == ASSET_ID_SEARCH.ASSET_ID)
                {
                    sql = "select * from vAssets a where a.asset_id = @asset_id";
                    parm_name = "@asset_id";
                }
            }
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter(parm_name, asset_id);
            q.UseCache = use_cache;
            T t = q.ExecuteSingle<T>(db_field);
            if (ColumnCacher.Instance.es_listo)
            {
                ColumnCacher.Instance.complex.AddRange(q.ColumnListFromTable);
            }
            return t;
        }

    }
}

            DataTable tbl = q.ExecuteTable();
            if(tbl.Rows.Count == 1)

        public static int? InsertUpdateColor(string server,int? existing_color_id, int colortype_id, int? asset_id, string note,int? account_id)
        {
            string sql = null;
            if (null == existing_color_id)
            {
                sql = "insert into Color (colortype_id,asset_id,note,account_id) output inserted.id values (@colortype_id,@asset_id,@note,@account_id)";
            }
            else
            {
                sql = "update Color set colortype_id = @colortype_id, asset_id = @asset_id, note = @note, account_id = @account_id where id = @existing_color_id";

            }
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.AddParameter("@existing_color_id", existing_color_id);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            q.AddParameter("@note", note);
            q.AddParameter("@colortype_id", colortype_id);
            return q.ExecuteSingleNullable<int>("id");
        }

            return tbl;

        {

            if(null == asset_ids)
                sql = "select * from vColorEx c order by update_time_ny desc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@assets", asset_ids);
   
            return q;
        }

            q.AddParameter("@color_id", color_id);
            q.Execute();

namespace PistonLib
{
    public class ColorTypes
    {
        public static string GetRowColorFromColor(string server, int colortype_id)
        {
            string sql = "select row_color from vColorTypes ct where ct.colortype_id = @colortype_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@colortype_id", colortype_id);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteSingle<string>("row_color");
        }

        public static string GetRowColorFromColorPrioirty(string server, double color_priority)
        {
            string sql = "select row_color from vColorTypes ct where ct.priority = @color_priority";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@color_priority", color_priority);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteSingle<string>("row_color");
        }

        public static T GetSingleAttribute<T>(string server, int colortype_id,string db_field)
        {
            string sql = "select csv_cols from vColorTypes ct where colortype_id = @colortype_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@colortype_id", colortype_id);
            q.UseCache = true;
            T t = q.ExecuteSingle<T>(db_field);
            return t;
        }

    }

--- FILE: Saluda\PistonLib\DocGen.cs ---
namespace PistonLib
{
    public static class DocGen
    {
        public static Dictionary<string, T> GetCommonAttributes<T>(string server, Dictionary<string,T> r, bool do_missing, string surround_variable_with)
        {
            if (null != surround_variable_with)
            {
                Dictionary<string, T> new_list = new Dictionary<string, T>();
                foreach (var s in r)
                {
                    string new_key = $"{surround_variable_with}{s.Key}{surround_variable_with}";
                    new_list.Add(new_key, s.Value);
                }
                r = new_list;

            }
            if (do_missing)
            {
                List<string> blank_keys = new List<string>();
                foreach (KeyValuePair<string, T> kvp in r)
                {
                    if (typeof(T) == typeof(string))
                    {
                        if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(kvp.Value as String))
                            blank_keys.Add(kvp.Key);
                    }
                }
                foreach (string missing in blank_keys)
                {
                    
                    r.Remove(missing);
                }
            }
            return r;
        }
    }
}

        public class FileNameHelper

        public static FileNameHelper GenerateFilename(string server, int doc_id, Dictionary<string, object> all_vars,string path_destination,bool copy_template_to_dest)
        {
            int docconfig_id = GetDocAttribute<int>(server, doc_id, "docconfig_id");
            string file_format = GetFileNameFormat(server, docconfig_id);
            string ext = GetDocConfigAttribute<string>(server, docconfig_id, "docoutputtype_extension");
            
            DateTime? created = null;

            Dictionary<string, object> final_vars = new Dictionary<string, object>();
            foreach (KeyValuePair<string, object> kvp in all_vars)
            {
                final_vars.Add($"@{kvp.Key}@", $"{kvp.Value}");
            }
            
            string template_file = GetTemplateFile(server, doc_id,true);

            string filename = UtilsLib.Clean.CommonVariables(file_format, null, final_vars);

            string filename_fixed = Clean.CleanFilename(filename, false);
            
            string final_filename = Path.Combine(path_destination, filename_fixed + ext);
            if(copy_template_to_dest)
                FileLib.CopyFileReallySmartly(template_file, final_filename,true);

            return new FileNameHelper { final_name_full = final_filename, file_name_only_with_no_ext = Path.GetFileNameWithoutExtension(final_filename), file_name_only_with_ext = Path.GetFileName(final_filename) , working_file = template_file};
            
        }

        public static string GenerateExcelFile(string server,int doc_id,Dictionary<string,object> vars,int trade_id,FileNameHelper fnh)
        {
            string csv_cols = PistonLib.Docs.GetDocAttribute<string>(server, doc_id, "csv_cols");
            int docconfig_id = PistonLib.Docs.GetDocAttribute<int>(server, doc_id, "docconfig_id");
            string sql = PistonLib.Docs.GetDocConfigAttribute<string>(server, docconfig_id, "sql");
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@trade_id", trade_id);
            DataTable tbl = q.ExecuteTable();
            tbl = tbl.TrimColumms(csv_cols);
            FieldLib.Fields f = new FieldLib.Fields(server, Database.FieldHelper.GetFieldTableInternal);
            
            string temp_filename = UtilsLib.Excel.CreateQuickExcel(fnh.file_name_only_with_no_ext, new DataTable[] { tbl }, true, Excel.EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE.XLSB, false, f);
            FileLib.CopySmart(temp_filename, fnh.final_name_full);
            return fnh.final_name_full;
        }

        public static List<string> GenerateDocPackage(string server, int? docpackage_id,int? relevant_id_input,string path_dest,IETA eta,bool spawn_when_done,List<int> asset_ids,List<int?> docconfig_ids_only)
        {
            int relevant_id = -1;
            if (null != relevant_id_input)
                relevant_id = relevant_id_input.Value;


            List<int> docs = new List<int>();
            int? packagetype = null;
            if (null != docpackage_id)
            {
                docs = GetDocsForPackage(server, docpackage_id.Value);
                packagetype = GetPackageAttribute<int>(server, docpackage_id.Value, "docpackagetype_id");
            }
            else
            {
                if (null != docconfig_ids_only)
                {
                    foreach(int? docconfig in docconfig_ids_only)
                    {
                        if (null != docconfig)
                        {
                            int? doc_id = PistonLib.Docs.GetLatestDocFromConfig(server, docconfig.Value, relevant_id).Value;
                            if (null == doc_id)
                                throw new Exception($"No doc found for docconfig {docconfig.Value} and relevant_id {relevant_id}");
                            docs.Add(doc_id.Value);
                        }
                    }
                    
                    
                    
                }
            }
           
            if (null != eta)
                eta.SetTotal(docs.Count);
            
            Dictionary<string, object> vars = new Dictionary<string, object>();
            Dictionary<string, object> fields = new Dictionary<string, object>();
            List<string> files = new List<string>();

            if (packagetype == 2 || packagetype == 3)
            {
                fields = PistonLib.Trades.GetTradeDocGenFields<object>(server, relevant_id);
                
                DataTable loans = PistonLib.Trades.GetTradeAssetDocGen(server, relevant_id);
                vars.Add(loans.TableName, loans);

                int? linker_id = PistonLib.Linker.GetLink(server, 1, relevant_id);
                if(null == linker_id)
                {
                    throw new Exception("Need to setup a wire first....");
                }
                Fields.GetInstance(server,Database.FieldHelper.GetFieldTableInternal).FormatColumnNames(loans,true);
                 

                DataSet wires = PistonLib.Wires.GetWireSet(server, "html_wire", linker_id.Value);
                ProcessWires(server,relevant_id,wires, vars, docpackage_id);
            }
            if(packagetype == 4 || null == packagetype)
            {
                DataTable loans = PistonLib.Assets.GetAssetSummary(server, asset_ids);
                loans = loans.TrimColumms("loan_id,address_full,borrower");
                Fields f = Fields.GetInstance(server, Database.FieldHelper.GetFieldTableInternal);
                f.FormatColumnNames(loans, true);
                vars.Add("table_" + loans.TableName, loans);
            }


            PistonLib.Usage.RecordUsage(server, PistonLib.Usage.UsageTypes.DOCS_GENERATED, docs.Count, null, null, null, null, null);

            vars.AddRange(PistonLib.DocGen.GetCommonAttributes<object>(server, fields, true, null));
            string filename = null;
            bool async = true;
            List<Task> tasks = new List<Task>();
            
            
            foreach (int doc_id in docs)
            {
                var vars_local = vars.Clone();
                CleanTables(server, doc_id, vars_local);
                if (!async)
                    GenerateDocSingle(server, doc_id, vars_local, path_dest, eta, spawn_when_done, relevant_id);
                else
                {
                    tasks.Add(Task.Run(() =>
                    {
                        GenerateDocSingle(server, doc_id, vars_local, path_dest, eta, spawn_when_done, relevant_id);
                    }));
                }
            }
 
            Task.WaitAll(tasks.ToArray());

                
                
                
                

                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                return files;
        }

        public static void CleanTables(string server,int doc_id, Dictionary<string,object> vars)
        {
            
            {
                Dictionary<string, string> maps = GetDocColumnMaps(server, doc_id);
                foreach(var m in maps)
                {
                    if(vars.ContainsKey(m.Key))
                    {
                        if(!String.IsNullOrEmpty(m.Value))
                        {
                            DataTable tbl = ((DataTable)vars[m.Key]).TrimColumms(m.Value);

                            string total_cols = GetTotalsColumn(server,doc_id);
                            if(!String.IsNullOrEmpty(total_cols))
                            {
                                DataRow row = tbl.Rows.Add();
                                row[0] = "TOTALS:";
                                
                                foreach(string total in total_cols.Split(','))
                                {
                                    double? col_total = tbl.AsEnumerable().Sum(r => r.Field<double?>(total));
                                    
                                    
                                    row[total] = col_total;
                                }
                            }
                            vars[m.Key] = tbl;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }

        }

        public static string GetTotalsColumn(string server,int doc_id)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vDocColumnConfig dc where dc.doc_id = @doc_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@doc_id", doc_id);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteSingle<string>("total_columns");
        }
        public static Dictionary<string, string> GetDocColumnMaps(string server,int doc_id)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vDocColumnConfig dc where dc.doc_id = @doc_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@doc_id", doc_id);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteDictRows<string,string>("table_name", "csv_config");
        }
        public static List<string> GenerateDocSingle(string server,int doc_id, Dictionary<string, object> vars, string path_dest, IETA eta,bool spawn_when_done,int relevant_id)
        {
            List<string> files = new List<string>();

            string filename = null;
            
            

            var doc_output = Docs.GetOutputType(server, doc_id);
            int docconfig_id = Docs.GetDocAttribute<int>(server, doc_id, "docconfig_id");
            var file_helper = GenerateFilename(server, doc_id, vars, path_dest, false);
            if (doc_output == REPORT_OUTPUT_TYPE.PDF)
            {
                filename = GenerateWordDoc(server, doc_id, vars, file_helper, UtilsLib.WordLib.ChopOffPagesAfterLastVariable);
            }
            if (doc_output == REPORT_OUTPUT_TYPE.EXCEL)
            {
                filename = GenerateExcelFile(server, doc_id, vars, relevant_id, file_helper);
            }
            if (doc_output == REPORT_OUTPUT_TYPE.MACRO_TEMPLATE)
            {
                filename = GenerateMacroTemplate(server, doc_id, vars, file_helper);
            }
            if (doc_output == REPORT_OUTPUT_TYPE.WORD_DOC)
            {
                filename = GenerateWordDoc(server, doc_id, vars, file_helper, null);
            }
            if (spawn_when_done)
                UtilsLib.ProcessHelper.SpawnAsync(filename);
            files.Add(filename);
            
            return files;
        }

        

        public static void ProcessWires(string server, int trade_id,DataSet wires,Dictionary<string,object> vars,int? docpackage_id)
        {
            double total_wire_amt = 0;
            int wire_num = 0;
            foreach (DataTable tbl in wires.Tables)
            {
                DataRow[] delete = tbl.Select("wire_amount is null");
                if(delete.Length > 0)
                {
                    throw new Exception("Bro - allocate your wires...");
                }
                total_wire_amt += System.Convert.ToDouble(tbl.Compute("sum(wire_amount)", null));
             }
            vars.Add("total_wire_amt_formatted", $"${total_wire_amt:#,##0.00}");
            vars.Add("total_wires", wires.Tables.Count);

            DataTable wire_summary = new DataTable();
            wire_summary.Columns.Add("benefciary_name");
            wire_summary.Columns.Add("wire_amount_formatted");
           
            foreach (DataTable tbl in wires.Tables)
            {
                string html = TableToVars(tbl, "wire");
                vars.Add(tbl.TableName, html);

                List<int> accounts = tbl.GetUniqueList<int>("account_id");
                if (accounts.Count != 1)
                    throw new Exception("Can't have multiple (or zero) accounts on same wire?");
                if(null == accounts)
                    throw new Exception("Can't have null accounts on same wire?");
                DataTable tape = PistonLib.Trades.GetTapeMaster(server, trade_id, accounts[0]);
                string tbl_format = "loan_id,address_full,borrower_name";
                if (null != docpackage_id)
                    tbl_format = GetPackageAttribute<string>(server, docpackage_id.Value, "wire_table_format");
                if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(tbl_format) && tbl_format == "-1")
                {

                    
                    
                    tape.Columns.Clear();
                    tape.Rows.Clear();
                }

                foreach (DataRow row in tbl.Rows)
                {
                    if (tbl.Columns.Contains("beneficiary_name") && tbl.Columns.Contains("wire_amount_formatted"))
                    {
                        wire_summary.Rows.Add(row["beneficiary_name"], row["wire_amount_formatted"]);
                    }
                }
                
                if (tape.Columns.Contains("draw_amount_formatted"))
                {
                    decimal wire_total = tbl.AsEnumerable().Sum(row => row.Field<decimal>("wire_amount"));
   
                        tape = tape.TrimColumms(tbl_format);

                    if (tape.Columns.Contains("draw_amount_formatted"))
                    {
                        DataRow total_row = tape.Rows.Add();
                        total_row[0] = "TOTAL:";
                        
                        total_row["draw_amount_formatted"] = $"{wire_total:#,##0.00}";
                    }
                    
                }

                
                
                {
                    Fields.GetInstance(server, Database.FieldHelper.GetFieldTableInternal).FormatColumnNames(tape, true);
                    vars.Add($"table_loan_list_{wire_num}", tape.Copy());
                }
                wire_num++;
            }
            Fields.GetInstance(server, Database.FieldHelper.GetFieldTableInternal).FormatColumnNames(wire_summary, true);
            wire_summary.Sort(wire_summary.Columns[0].ColumnName, true);
            wire_summary.Rows.Add($"{wire_summary.Rows.Count} WIRES", $"TOTAL: ${total_wire_amt:#,##0.00}");
            
            vars.Add("table_wire_summary", wire_summary);
        }

        public static string TableToVars(DataTable tbl, string template)
        {
            string html_base = File.ReadAllText($"templates\\{template}.html");
            var vars = tbl.SingleRowToDict<object>();
            foreach (var var in vars)
            {
                string search = "{{" + var.Key + "}}";
                html_base = html_base.Replace(search, var.Value as string);
            }
            return html_base;
        }
        public static string GetTemplateFile(string server, int document_id,bool copy_2_temp_folder)
        {
            string base_consumer_doc_location = Database.Common.GetGlobal(server, "BASE_PISTON_DIR", true,true);

            string doc_name = GetDocName(server, document_id);
            string rev_name = GetRev(server, document_id);
            int docconfig_id = GetDocAttribute<int>(server, document_id, "docconfig_id");
            
            string doc_name_final = $"{doc_name} - {rev_name}";
            string base_folder = GetDocConfigAttribute<string>(server, docconfig_id, "base_folder");
            if (null == base_folder)
                return null;
            string base_doc_location = Path.Combine(base_consumer_doc_location, base_folder);

            
            

            
            string doc_name_no_ext = $"{doc_name_final} - {DateTime.Now:M.d.yyyy}";
            string ext = "docx";

            
            string[] files_tmp = Directory.GetFiles(base_doc_location, $"*{rev_name}*", SearchOption.AllDirectories);
            string[] files = files_tmp.Where(n => !n.Contains("~")).ToArray();
            string full_location = null;
            if (null != files && files.Length == 1)
            {
                if (copy_2_temp_folder)
                {
                    string new_name = Path.Combine(Path.GetTempPath(), Path.GetRandomFileName() + $"{Path.GetExtension(files[0])}");
                    File.Copy(files[0], new_name);
                    full_location = new_name;
                }
                else
                {
                    full_location = files[0];
                }
            }
            else
            {
                throw new Exception("Files not matched: " + doc_name_final);
            }

            
            
            


            return full_location;
        }

        }

        }

namespace PistonLib

    public static class Draws
    {

        public static DataTable DrawHistory(string server)

            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DateTime? LastUpdate(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select max(update_time) [last_update] from Draws";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteSingleNullable<DateTime>("last_update");
        }

        public static DataTable DrawHistoryWithTrades(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select d.*,t.trade_id from vDrawsEx d left join vLinker l on l.foreign_id = d.draw_id AND l.linkertype_id = 2 left join vTrades t on l.linker_id = t.trade_id and t.ticket_type = 'D' order by request_date desc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static Query GetDrawQuery(string server, List<int> asset_ids)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vDrawsEx c join @assets a on a.item = c.asset_id order by request_date desc";
            if (null == asset_ids)
                sql = "select * from vDrawsEx c order by request_date desc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@assets", asset_ids);

            return q;
        }

        public static DataTable DrawStatusSummary(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select status, sum(case when d.sg_approval_date is null then d.draw_amount else 0 end) [pending_approval_upb], sum(case when d.sg_approval_date is not null and d.reimbursement_date is null then d.draw_amount else 0 end) [approved_not_disbursed_upb] from vDrawsEx d where status is not null and reimbursable = 1 group by status,request_type having (sum(case when d.sg_approval_date is null then d.draw_amount else 0 end) != 0 or sum(case when d.sg_approval_date is not null and d.reimbursement_date is null then d.draw_amount else 0 end) != 0) order by sum(case when d.reimbursement_date is null then d.draw_amount else 0 end) desc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DataTable DrawStatusSummaryByDeal(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select count(*) [#], sg_deal, sum(d.draw_amount) [draw_amount] from vDrawsEx d where reimbursement_date is null and d.sg_approval_date is not null and sg_deal not in ('AFLOW') and d.reimbursable = 1 group by sg_deal order by sum(d.draw_amount) desc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }
    }
}

namespace PistonLib
{
    public static class FieldsHelper
    {
        public static T GetSingleAttribute<T>(string server, string db_field, string col_2_return)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vFields f where f.field = @db_field";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@db_field", db_field);
            q.UseCache = true;
            T t = q.ExecuteSingle<T>(col_2_return);
            return t;
        }

    }
