--- FILE: Saluda\PistonLib\Linker.cs ---
namespace PistonLib
{
    public static class Linker
    {
        public static int AddLink(string server,int linkertype_id, int foreign_id)
        {
            string sql = "insert into Linker (linkertype_id,foreign_id) output inserted.id values (@linkertype_id,@foreign_id)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@linkertype_id", linkertype_id);
            q.AddParameter("@foreign_id", foreign_id);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<int>();
        }


        public static int? GetLinkerIdFromTrade(string server,int trade_id)
        {
            string sql = "select top 1 linker_id from vLinker l where linkertype_id = 1 and foreign_id = @trade_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@trade_id", trade_id);
            return q.ExecuteSingleNullable<int>("linker_id");
        }

        public static void ResetWire(string server,int linker_id)
        {
             string sql = "exec dbo.ResetWire @linker_id=@linker_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);   
            q.AddParameter("@linker_id", linker_id);
            q.Execute();
        }
        public static int GetLinkOrAddIfNot(string server, int linkertype_id,int foreign_id)
        {
            int? linker_id = GetLink(server,linkertype_id,foreign_id);
            if (null == linker_id)
                return AddLink(server, linkertype_id, foreign_id);
            else
            {
                return linker_id.Value;
            }
        }
        public static int? GetLink(string server,int linkertype_id,int foreign_id)
        {
            string sql = "select linker_id from vLinker l where linkertype_id = @linkertype_id and foreign_id = @foreign_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@linkertype_id", linkertype_id);
            q.AddParameter("@foreign_id", foreign_id);
            return q.ExecuteSingleNullable<int>("linker_id");
        }

    }
}


--- FILE: Saluda\PistonLib\Maps.cs ---
namespace PistonLib
{
    public static class Maps
    {
        public static void AddMapDetail(string server,int tapemap_id, string field)
        {
            string sql = "insert into TapeMapDetail (tapemap_id,field) values (@tapemap_id,@field)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@tapemap_id", tapemap_id);
            q.AddParameter("@field", field);
            q.Execute();
        }

        public static DataTable GetAvailableMaps(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select distinct db_field from vMaps order by db_field";
            Query q = new Query(sql,server);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static void DeleteMap(string server,int tapemap_id)
        {
            string sql = "delete from TapeMapDetail where tapemap_id = @tapemap_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@tapemap_id", tapemap_id);
            q.Execute();
            q.SetSQL("delete from TapeMaps where id = @tapemap_id");
            q.Execute();
        }

        public static void InsertUpdateTapeMap(string server, int tapemap_id, string field)
        {
            bool exists = MapeExists(server, tapemap_id, field);
            if (!exists)
                AddMapDetail(server, tapemap_id, field);
        }
        public static bool MapeExists(string server, int tapemap_id, string field)
        {
            string sql = "select * from TapeMapDetail where tapemap_id = @tapemap_id and field = @field";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@tapemap_id", tapemap_id);
            q.AddParameter("@field", field);
            return q.ExecuteTable().Rows.Count > 0;
        }


        public static bool DatabaseMapExists(string server, int tapemap_id, string db_field)
        {
            string sql = "select * from TapeMapDetail where tapemap_id = @tapemap_id and db_field = @db_field";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@tapemap_id", tapemap_id);
            q.AddParameter("@db_field", db_field);
            return q.ExecuteTable().Rows.Count > 0;
        }
        
        
        
        
        
        

        public static string TryAutoMap(string server,string field)
        {
            string sql = "select distinct db_field from vTapeMapDetail tmd where upper(tmd.field) = upper(@field) and db_field is not null";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@field", field);
            q.UseCache = true;
            var results = q.ExecuteSingle<string>();
            if(null == results)
            {
                var fields = DBUtils.GetTableColumns(server, "TapeDetail",true);
                if (fields.ContainsKeyIns(field))
                    return field.ToLower();
                if (fields.ContainsKeyIns(field.Replace(" ","_")))
                    return field.Replace(" ", "_").ToLower();
            }
            return results;
        }

        public static void UpdateMap(string server, int tapemap_id, int? account_id, string name)
        {
            string sql = "update Tapemaps set name = @name,  account_id = @account_id where id = @tapemap_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@name", name);
            q.AddParameter("@tapemap_id", tapemap_id);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            q.Execute();

        }


        public static string GetMapName(string server, int tapemap_id)
        {
            string sql = "select name from vTapeMaps t where t.tapemap_id = @tapemap_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@tapemap_id", tapemap_id);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<string>("name");
        }

        public static DataTable GetMapTable(string server,bool show_all)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vTapeMaps t where (@show_all = 1 or hide=0)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@show_all", show_all);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DataTable GetFieldMapTable(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vMaps";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }
    }
}

namespace PistonLib
{
    public static class Positions
    {
        public static DataTable GetPositionSummaryTable(string server)
        {
            
            Query q = new Query("RemitSummary.sql", server);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DataTable GetTradeDetail(string server, int account_id)
        {
            string sql = "select p.*,a.address_full,a.loan_id from vPositions p join vAssets a on a.asset_id = p.asset_id where p.account_id = @account_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DataTable GetPositionDetail(string server, int account_id)
        {
            string sql = "select a.*,p.* from vPositions p join vAssets a on a.asset_id = p.asset_id where p.account_id = @account_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static int? HistoricalOwner(string server,int asset_id,DateTime? asOf,string return_value)
        {
            string sql = "SELECT account,account_id from vTradesEx t where t.ticket_type = 'TT' and asset_id = @asset_id and settle_date <= @asOf and buy_sell = 'B' order by t.trade_date desc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.AddParameter("@asOf", null == asOf ? DateTime.Today : asOf.Value);
            return q.ExecuteSingleNullable<int>(return_value);
        }

    }
}

--- FILE: Saluda\PistonLib\SQL\RemitSummary.sql ---
drop table if exists #tmp

SELECT 
      t.account_id
      , a.name [account]
      , sum(case when td.ending_upb != 0 then 1 else 0 end) [ln_cnt]
      , sum (td.beginning_upb) [beginning_upb]
      , sum(td.purchased_upb) [purchased_upb]
      , sum(isnull(td.draws_from_collections,0)+isnull(td.draws,0)) [total_drawn_amount]
      , sum(td.total_capitalized_amount) [capitalized_amount]
      , -sum(td.scheduled_principal) [scheduled_principal]
      , -sum(td.prepayment) [unscheduled_principal]
      
      , -sum(isnull(td.scheduled_principal,0)+isnull(td.prepayment,0)) [total_principal_remit]
      , sum(td.total_int_remit) [total_interest]
      , -sum(isnull(td.asset_principal_sold_in_period,0)+isnull(td.loan_sale,0)) [princ_sold]
      , null [undrawn_hold_back]
      , null [recoverable_fees_and_advances]
      , sum(td.non_cash_principal_adj) [non_cash_adj]
      , null [realized_loss]
      , sum (td.ending_upb) [ending_upb]
      , max (t.cutoff_date) [last_remit]
      , sum(b.balance) [cash_balance_live]
      , max(b.asOf) [cash_balance_asOf]
      , t.tape_id
      into #tmp
     from vTapes t
     join vTapeDetail td ON td.tape_id = t.tape_id
     join vAccounts a on a.account_id = t.account_id
     left join vBalancesEx b on b.account_id = a.account_id and b.latest = 1 and b.reinvestable =1
     WHERE 
      t.latest_tapetype = 1
      and accounttype_id = 1
      and t.tapetype_id = 2
      
     GROUP BY 
      t.account_id
      , a.name
      , t.tape_id
     order by a.name
     
     


select * from #tmp order by account


drop table if exists #tmp


--- FILE: Saluda\PistonLib\SQL\RemitSummary2.sql ---
select
t.tape_id
, t.account_id
, t.tape_type
, t.account
, t.asof
, t.cutoff_date
, sum(case when td.LOAN_ID is not null then 1 else 0 end) [loans]
, sum(td.balance) [balance]
, sum(td.gwac*td.balance)/sum(td.balance) [gwac]
, sum(td.margin*td.balance)/sum(td.balance) [margin]
, t.update_time [load_time]
  from 
    vTapesEx t
    left join vTapeDetail td on td.tape_id = t.tape_id
group by
t.tape_id
, t.account_id
, t.tape_type
, t.account
, t.cutoff_date
, t.update_time 
, t.asof
  order by t.tape_id desc


--- FILE: Saluda\PistonLib\SQL\RemitSummaryHistorical.sql ---
drop table if exists #tmp

SELECT 
      DATEADD(month, DATEDIFF(month, 0, t.cutoff_date), 0) [cutoff_collection_month]
      , a.name [account]
      , sum(case when td.ending_upb != 0 then 1 else 0 end) [ln_cnt]
      , sum (td.beginning_upb) [beginning_upb]
      , sum(td.purchased_upb) [purchased_upb]
      , sum(isnull(td.draws_from_collections,0)+isnull(td.draws,0)) [total_drawn_amount]
      , sum(td.total_capitalized_amount) [capitalized_amount]
      , -sum(td.scheduled_principal) [scheduled_principal]
      , -sum(td.prepayment) [unscheduled_principal]
      , -sum(isnull(td.scheduled_principal,0)+isnull(td.prepayment,0)) [total_principal]
      , sum(td.total_int_remit) [total_interest]
      , -sum(isnull(td.asset_principal_sold_in_period,0)+isnull(td.loan_sale,0)) [princ_sold]
      , null [undrawn_hold_back]
      , null [recoverable_fees_and_advances]
      , sum(td.non_cash_principal_adj) [non_cash_adj]
      , null [realized_loss]
      , sum (td.ending_upb) [ending_upb]
      , t.tape_id
      into #tmp
     from vTapes t
     join vTapeDetail td ON td.tape_id = t.tape_id
     join vAccounts a on a.account_id = t.account_id
     left join vBalancesEx b on b.account_id = a.account_id and b.latest = 1 and b.reinvestable =1
     WHERE 
      
      accounttype_id = 1
      and t.latest_tapetype_month = 1
      and t.tapetype_id = 2
      
     GROUP BY 
      t.account_id
      , a.name
      , t.tape_id
      , DATEADD(month, DATEDIFF(month, 0, t.cutoff_date), 0)
     order by a.name, DATEADD(month, DATEDIFF(month, 0, t.cutoff_date), 0)
     
     


select * from #tmp order by cutoff_collection_month desc,account


drop table if exists #tmp

select @tape_id = tape_id from vTrades t where t.trade_id = @trade_id

 select
 
   'L' [Rec Type]

--- FILE: Saluda\PistonLib\SQL\TradeDocGenFields.sql ---
declare @depositor_id int = 116

drop table if exists #tmp

select
  a.legal_name [buyer_legal_name]
  
  , max(coalesce(a.name_short,a.name)) [buyer_name_simple]
  , max(a.name) [buyer_name]
  
  , case when count(distinct t.counterparty_id) != 1 then 'MULTIPLE SELLERS' else max(c.legal_name) end [seller_legal_name]
  , d.legal_name [depositor_legal_name]
  , t.settle_date
  , format(t.settle_date,'MMMM d, yyyy') [settle_date_spelled]
  , max(format(t.trade_date,'MMMM d, yyyy')) [trade_date_spelled]
  , format(a.indenture_date,'MMMM d, yyyy') [indenture_date_spelled]
  , d_u.full_name [depositor_signer]
  , isnull(uam.title_override,d_u.title) [depositor_title]
  
  , case when count(distinct t.counterparty_id) != 1 then 'MULTIPLE SELLERS' else max(d_u_sell.full_name) end [seller_signer]
  , case when count(distinct t.counterparty_id) != 1 then 'MULTIPLE SELLERS' else max(d_u_sell.email) end [seller_email]
  
  , case when count(distinct t.counterparty_id) != 1 then 'MULTIPLE SELLERS' else max(COALESCE(srm.title_override,d_u_sell.title)) end [seller_title]
  , d_u.full_name [buyer_signer]
  , isnull(uam.title_override,d_u.title) [buyer_title]
  
  , STRING_AGG(isnull(c.name_short,c.name),'+') WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY isnull(c.name_short,c.name)) [seller_name_simple_alt]
  , convert(varchar(150),case when count(distinct t.counterparty_id) != 1 then 'MULTIPLE SELLERS' else max(isnull(c.name_short,c.name)) end) [seller_name_simple]
  , convert(varchar(150),case when count(distinct t.counterparty_id) != 1 then 'MULTIPLE SELLERS' else max(c.name) end) [seller_name]
  , convert(varchar(150),case when count(distinct t.counterparty_id) != 1 then 'MULTIPLE SELLERS' else max(isnull(c.name_short,c.name)) end) [seller_name_simple_all] 
  , max(t.trade_date) [trade_date]
  , t.trade_id
  , count(*) [loan_count]
  , sum(cface) [trade_upb]
  
  , sum(cface*t.price)/sum(cface)*100.0 [trade_price_100]
  
  , sum(t.market_value-cface) [total_premium]
  
  , sum(t.market_value) [market_value]
  
  , sum(t.accrued_interest) [accrued_interest]
 
  , sum(t.total_proceeds) [total_proceeds]
  , sum(isnull(td.prepaid_interest_reserve,0)) [prepaid_interest_reserve]
  , sum(td.gross_margin*t.oface)/sum(t.oface) [gross_margin]
  , sum(td.gross_rate*t.oface)/sum(t.oface) [gwac]
  , sum(td.net_int_rate*t.oface)/sum(t.oface) [nwac]
  , sum((td.net_int_rate-(td.gross_rate-td.gross_margin))*t.oface)/sum(t.oface) [pass_thru_margin]
  , sum(t.total_proceeds-isnull(td.prepaid_interest_reserve,0)) [net_proceeds]
  
  
  
  
  
  
  
  , t.tape_id
  

  
  , a.indenture_date
  , a.draw_account
  , ake.forward_flow_agreement_date_spelled
  , ake.loan_sale_agreement_date_spelled
  , sum(case when (td.gross_margin is null or td.gross_margin = 0) then td.gross_rate else td.gross_margin end*t.oface)/sum(t.oface) [coupon_1]
  , sum(case when (td.gross_margin is null or td.gross_margin = 0) then td.net_int_rate else td.pass_thru_rate end*t.oface)/sum(t.oface) [coupon_2]
  , max(case when (td.gross_margin is null or td.gross_margin = 0) then 'GWAC' else 'Gross Weighted Margin' end)  [coupon_1_name]
  , max(case when (td.gross_margin is null or td.gross_margin = 0) then 'NWAC' else 'Weighted Pass Thru Margin' end)  [coupon_2_name]
  
  , max(seller_state.state_full) [seller_entity_state_full]
  , max(sell_entity.type) [seller_entity_type]
  , max(seller_servicing.type) [released_retained]
  
  , max(buyer_state.state_full) [buyer_entity_state_full]
  , max(buy_entity.type) [buyer_entity_type]
  
  , max(ake.purchase_agreement_type) [purchase_agreement_type_seller]
  , MAX(ake.purchase_agreement_date_spelled) [purchase_agreement_date_seller_spelled]
  , MAX(AKE.depositor_sale_agreement_date_spelled) [depositor_sale_agreement_date_seller_spelled]
  , max(a.custody_acct_num) [custody_acct_num_buyer]
  into #tmp
  from 
    vTrades t 
    join vAccountsEx a on a.account_id = t.account_id
    
    
    join vAccounts c on c.account_id = t.counterparty_id
    left join vStates seller_state on seller_state.state = c.entity_state
    left join vStates buyer_state on buyer_state.state = a.entity_state
    left join vEntityTypes sell_entity on sell_entity.entitytype_id = c.entitytype_id
    left join vEntityTypes buy_entity on buy_entity.entitytype_id = a.entitytype_id
    left join vServicingTypes seller_servicing on seller_servicing.servicingtype_id = c.servicingtype_id
    
    join vAccounts d on d.account_id = @depositor_id
    join UserAccountRoleMap uam on uam.account_id = d.account_id and uam.userrole_id = 1
    left join UserAccountRoleMap uam_sell on uam_sell.account_id = c.account_id and uam_sell.userrole_id = 1
    join vUsers d_u on uam.[user_id] = d_u.[user_id]
    left join vUsers d_u_sell on uam_sell.user_id = d_u_sell.user_id
    left join UserAccountRoleMap srm on srm.account_id = c.account_id and srm.userrole_id = 1
    
    left join vTapeDetail td on td.tape_id = t.tape_id and td.asset_id = t.asset_id
    join vAssets ass on ass.asset_id = t.asset_id
    left join vAccountKeysEx ake on ake.account_id = c.account_id
    
  where 
    trade_id = @trade_id
    
  group by
   a.legal_name
  , a.name_short
  
  , d.legal_name
  , t.settle_date
  , format(t.settle_date,'MMMM d, yyyy')
  
  , d_u.full_name
  , uam.title_override
  
  
  
  , t.trade_id
  , d_u.full_name
  , d_u.title
  , t.tape_id
  , a.indenture_date
  , a.draw_account
  , ake.loan_sale_agreement_date_spelled
  , ake.forward_flow_agreement_date_spelled
  , ake.purchase_agreement_type
  , ake.purchase_agreement_date_spelled
  , AKE.depositor_sale_agreement_date_spelled



update #tmp set seller_name_simple = replace(dbo.Trim(dbo.DistinctWords(seller_name_simple_alt,'+')),'+',', ')
update #tmp set seller_name_simple_all = replace(dbo.Trim(dbo.DistinctWords(seller_name_simple_alt,'+')),'+',', ')

select * from #tmp

drop table if exists #tmp


--- FILE: Saluda\PistonLib\SQL\WireSetup.sql ---
drop table if exists #pending
drop table if exists #alloc

create table #pending
(
  id int
  , wire_desc varchar(250)
  , due decimal(18,2)
  , allocated decimal(18,2)
  , linkertype_id int
  , linker_id int
  , ticket_type varchar(3)
  , cnt int
  , account varchar(50)
  , settle_date date
  , draw_id int
  , trade_id int
  , update_time datetime
  , wiretype_id int
)
insert into #pending (id,due,linkertype_id,wire_desc,ticket_type,cnt,account,settle_date,trade_id,update_time,wiretype_id)
select 
  t.trade_id
  , sum(t.total_proceeds)
  , 1
  , case when ticket_type = 'D' then 'DRAW' ELSE t.trade_desc_simple END
  , ticket_type
  , count(distinct counterparty_id)
  , max(account) [account]
  , settle_date
  , trade_id
  , max(update_time)
  , max(wtt.wiretype_id)
  from 
    vTradesEx t
    
    join vWireTemplateTypes wtt on wtt.wiretemplatetype_id = t.wiretemplatetype_id
        
  
  
  group by 
    t.trade_id
    
    , case when ticket_type = 'D' then 'DRAW' ELSE t.trade_desc_simple END
    , ticket_type
    , settle_date
  
  
 
  update p set wire_desc = account + ' - DRAW - (' + convert(varchar(3),CNT) + ' counterparties)' from #pending p where ticket_type = 'D'
 
  update p set p.linker_id = l.linker_id from #pending p join vLinkerEx l on p.linkertype_id = l.linkertype_id and p.id = l.foreign_id
  
  
  
  select 
    sum(w.wire_amount) [allocated]
    , w.linker_id
    , l.foreign_id
    , l.draw_id
    , l.trade_id
    into #alloc
    from
      vWires w
      join vLinkerEx l on l.linker_id = w.linker_id
    group by
      w.linker_id
      , l.foreign_id
      , l.draw_id
      , l.trade_id
     
 update p set allocated = a.allocated from #pending p join #alloc a on p.linker_id = a.linker_id
 delete from #pending where linker_id is null
 
 select 
  [id]
  , settle_date [value_date]
  , tt.note [type]
  , wire_desc
  , p.due
  , allocated
  , due-isnull(allocated,0) [remaining_to_allocate] 
  , linker_id
  , trade_id
  , p.ticket_type
  , wiretype_id
  from 
    #pending p 
    
    join TicketTypes tt on tt.ticket_type = p.ticket_type
    order by settle_date desc,p.update_time desc,p.due desc
 





drop table if exists #pending
drop table if exists #alloc

--- FILE: Saluda\PistonLib\TapeDetail.cs ---
namespace PistonLib
{
    public static class TapeDetail
    {

        public static Query GetTapeDetailQuery(string server, List<int> asset_ids)
        {
            string cols = PistonLib.ColorTypes.GetSingleAttribute<string>(server, 4, "csv_cols");
            string sql = $"select asset_id,color_priority,{cols} from vTapeDetailEx c join @assets a on a.item = c.asset_id order by c.tape_cutoff desc";
            if (null == asset_ids)
                sql = $"select asset_id,color_priority,{cols} from vTapeDetailEx c";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@assets", asset_ids);
            return q;
        }

        public static DataTable GetTapeDetailAllStatic(string server,List<int> tape_ids)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vTapeDetailStatic tds join @tape_ids t on t.item = tds.tape_id order by account_name,account_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@tape_ids", tape_ids);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static void InsertAudit(string server,int tape_id,long asset_id,string field,object new_value)
        {
            var old_value = GetCurrentValue(server, tape_id, asset_id, field);
            string sql = "insert into TapeDetailAudit (tape_id,asset_id, [field], old_value, new_value) values (@tape_id,@asset_id,@field, @old_value, @new_value)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@tape_id", tape_id);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.AddParameter("@field", field);
            q.AddParameter("@new_value", new_value);
            q.AddParameter("@old_value", old_value);
            q.Execute();
        }

        public static object GetCurrentValue(string server,int tape_id, long asset_id,string field)
        {
            string sql = $"select {field} from TapeDetail where tape_id = @tape_id and asset_id = @asset_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@tape_id", tape_id);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<object>();
        }
        public static void UpdateField(string server,int tape_id,long asset_id, string field,object new_value)
        {
            InsertAudit(server,tape_id,asset_id,field,new_value);

            string sql = $"update TapeDetail set {field} = @new_value where tape_id = @tape_id and asset_id = @asset_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@tape_id", tape_id);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.AddParameter("@new_value", new_value);
            q.Execute();
        }

        public static DataTable GetCustomTape(string server, List<int> asset_ids)
        {
            string sql = "select * from TapeDetail td join @asset_ids a on a.item = td.asset_id and td.asset_latest = 1";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_ids", asset_ids);
            DataTable tape = q.ExecuteTable();
            tape.Columns.Remove("id");
            tape.Columns.Remove("asset_earliest");
            tape.Columns.Remove("asset_latest");
            tape.Columns.Remove("latest_prior");
            tape.Columns.Remove("dq_status_calc");
            tape.Columns.Remove("loan_status_calc");
            tape.Columns.Remove("loan_type_calc");
            tape.Columns.Remove("balance");
            tape.Columns.Remove("update_time");
            tape.Columns.Remove("update_time_ny");
            tape.Columns.Remove("update_by");
            tape.Columns.Remove("tape_id");
            return tape;
        }

        public static Query GetTapeDetailSimpleQuery(string server, List<int> asset_ids)
        {
            string cols = PistonLib.ColorTypes.GetSingleAttribute<string>(server, 4, "csv_cols");
            string sql = $"select asset_id,color_priority,tape_id,{cols} from vTapeDetailExSimple c join @assets a on a.item = c.asset_id order by c.asset_id, c.tape_cutoff desc";
            if (null == asset_ids)
                sql = $"select asset_id,color_priority,tape_id,{cols} from vTapeDetailExSimple c order by c.asset_id, c.tape_cutoff desc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@assets", asset_ids);
            return q;
        }

        public static List<int> GetAllAssets(string server,int tape_id)
        {
            string sql = "select asset_id from vTapeDetail t where tape_id = @tape_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@tape_id", tape_id);
            return q.ExecuteList<int>("asset_id");
        }

        public static DataTable GetAllRemitTapes(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vTapeDetailEx t where tapetype_id = 2";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

    }
}


--- FILE: Saluda\PistonLib\Tapes.cs ---
using static UtilsLib.Dates;
namespace PistonLib
{
    using Fields = FieldLib.Fields;
    public static class Tapes
    {

        
        public static string GetConstraintString(string server, string db_field)
        {
            string sql = "select convert(varchar(5),min_value) + ' to ' + convert(varchar(5),max_value) from Fields f where f.field = @db_field";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@db_field", db_field);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteSingle<string>();
        }
        public static string GetMappedColumn(string server,int? tapemap_id,string field)
        {

            string ret_val = null;
            if (null != tapemap_id)
            {
                string sql = "select * from vTapeMapDetailEx tmd where tmd.tapemap_id = @tapemap_id and tmd.field = @field";
                Query q = new Query(sql, server);
                q.AddParameter("@field", field);
                q.AddParameter("@tapemap_id", tapemap_id);
                q.UseCache = true;
                ret_val = q.ExecuteSingle<string>("db_field");
            }
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(ret_val))
            {
                bool exists = Database.DBUtils.ColumnExistsInServer(server, "TapeDetail", field);
                if (exists)
                    return field;
                else
                    return null;
            }
            return ret_val;
        }

        public static int CreateNewMap(string server, int? account_id, string name)
        {
            string sql = "insert into TapeMaps (name,account_id)  output inserted.id values (@name,@account_id)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@name", name);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<int>("id");
        }

        public static T GetSingleAttribute<T>(string server, int tape_id,string db_field,bool use_cache)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vTapesEx t where t.tape_id = @tape_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@tape_id", tape_id);
            q.UseCache = use_cache;
            T t = q.ExecuteSingle<T>(db_field);

            return t;
        }

        public static DataTable GetRemitList(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vAccounts a where a.accounttype_id=1 order by name";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DataTable GetTapeMapDetail(string server,int tapemap_id)
        {
            string sql = "select tmd.*  , case when f.min_value is not null or f.max_value is not null then 'GreenYellow' else null end [row_color],case when min_value is not null then convert(varchar(4),min_value) + ' to ' + convert(varchar(4),max_value) end [bounds] from     vTapeMapDetail tmd    left join Fields f on f.field = tmd.db_field  where  tmd.tapemap_id = @tapemap_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@tapemap_id", tapemap_id);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static int CreateTape(string server, int tapetype_id, int? account_id, DateTime? cutoff_date,DateTime? asOf, string note, int? tapemap_id,string filename)
        {
            PistonLib.Usage.RecordUsage(server, PistonLib.Usage.UsageTypes.TAPE_LOADED, account_id, tapetype_id, filename, null, null, null);
            string sql = "insert into Tapes (cutoff_date,account_id,tapetype_id,note,asOf,tapemap_id,filename) OUTPUT inserted.id  values (@cutoff_date,@account_id,@tapetype_id,@note,@asOf,@tapemap_id,@filename)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@cutoff_date", cutoff_date);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            q.AddParameter("@note", note);
            q.AddParameter("@tapetype_id", tapetype_id);
            q.AddParameter("@cutoff", cutoff_date);
            q.AddParameter("@asOf", asOf);
            q.AddParameter("@tapemap_id", tapemap_id);
            q.AddParameter("@filename", filename);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<int>("id");
        }

        public static T GetGeneric<T>(string server, int tape_id,string column)

        }

        public class LoadOutput
        {
            public DataTable removed_data;
            public DataTable clean_tape;
        }

        public static int LoadTape(string server,int tape_id,DataTable clean_tape,IETA eta)
        {
            clean_tape.Columns.AddColumnWithDefault<int>("tape_id", tape_id);
            if(!clean_tape.Columns.ContainsIns("asset_id"))
            {
                List<string> loan_ids = clean_tape.ToList<string>("loan_id");
                Dictionary<string, long> id_list = PistonLib.Assets.GetAssetIdsBatch(server, false, loan_ids);
                DataColumn col = clean_tape.Columns.Add("asset_id", typeof(int));
                foreach(DataRow row in clean_tape.Rows)
                {
                    string loan_id = row["loan_id"].ToString().ToUpper();

                    row[col] = id_list.GetKeyIns<string,long>(loan_id);
                }
            }
            
            
            var sqls = Database.QueryBuilder.SQLInsertValidate(clean_tape, server, "TapeDetail", true);
            Query q = new Query(null, server);
            q.SetETA(eta);
            q.ExecuteBatch(sqls.lines,25,null);
            return sqls.lines.Count;
        }

        public class FieldHelper
        {
            public string field_name;
            public double? min_value;
            public double? max_value;
            public double? correction_mult;
        }
        public static Dictionary<string,FieldHelper> GetMults(string server,int tapemap_id)
        {
            
            string sql = "select db_field,max_value,min_value,coalesce(tmd.correction_mult,f.correction_mult) [correction_mult] from vTapeMapDetail tmd left join Fields f on 1=2 and f.field = tmd.field where tmd.tapemap_id = @tapemap_id and (tmd.correction_mult is not null or f.max_value is not null) and db_field is not null";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@tapemap_id", tapemap_id);
            var t = q.ExecuteTable();
            var s = t.AsEnumerable().Select(n => new FieldHelper { field_name = n["db_field"].ToString(), min_value = n["min_value"].AsDouble(), max_value = n["max_value"].AsDouble(), correction_mult = n["correction_mult"].AsDouble() }).ToList();
            return s.ToDictionary(x => x.field_name, x => x);
        }
        public static LoadOutput TransformTape(string server,int? tapemap_id,DataTable raw_tape,bool perform_generic_transform,bool apply_asset_ids,bool remove_excel_errors)
        {
            
            List<string> cols_2_remove = new List<string>();
            DataTable removed_data = raw_tape.Copy();

            foreach (DataColumn col in raw_tape.Columns)
            {
                foreach (DataRow row in raw_tape.Rows)
                {
                    row[col] = UtilsLib.Clean.CleanObject(row[col]);
                }
            }

            Dictionary<string, FieldHelper> tape_specific = null;
             if (null != tapemap_id)
                tape_specific = GetMults(server, tapemap_id.Value);
           
            
            foreach(DataColumn col in raw_tape.Columns)
            {
                string map_name = GetMappedColumn(server,tapemap_id,col.ColumnName);
                if(null != map_name)
                {
                    removed_data.Columns.Remove(col.ColumnName);
                    col.ColumnName = map_name;
                    
                    
                    
                    
                }
                else
                {
                    cols_2_remove.Add(col.ColumnName);
                }
            }

            foreach(string s in cols_2_remove)
            {
                raw_tape.Columns.Remove(s);
            }

            if (null != tape_specific)
            {
                foreach (var c in tape_specific)
                {
                    foreach (DataRow row in raw_tape.Rows)
                    {
                        if (!raw_tape.Columns.Contains(c.Key))
                            continue;
                        var value = row[c.Key].AsDouble();
                        if (null != value)
                        {
                            row[c.Key] = value.Value * c.Value.correction_mult;
                        }
                        
                        
                        
                        

                    }
                }
            }

            if(perform_generic_transform && null == tape_specific)
            {
                Fields f = Fields.GetInstance(server, Database.FieldHelper.GetFieldTableInternal);

                foreach (var c in f.GetFields())
                {
                    if (null == c.correction_mult)
                        continue;
                    if (!raw_tape.Columns.ContainsIns(c.field_name))
                        continue;
                    bool entire_column_over = raw_tape.Columns[c.field_name].EntireColumnOverValue(c.max_value.Value);
                    bool entire_column_under = raw_tape.Columns[c.field_name].EntireColumnUnderValue(c.max_value.Value);
                    foreach (DataRow row in raw_tape.Rows)
                    {
                        if (!raw_tape.Columns.Contains(c.field_name.ToUpper()) || (null != tape_specific && tape_specific.ContainsKey(c.field_name.ToUpper())))
                            continue;
                        var value = row[c.field_name].AsDouble();
                        if (null != value)
                        {
                            if (entire_column_over)
                            {
                                row[c.field_name] = value.Value / c.correction_mult;
                            }
                            if (entire_column_under)
                            {
                                row[c.field_name] = value.Value * c.correction_mult;
                            }
                        }

                    }
                }

            }

            if(apply_asset_ids && null == raw_tape.Columns["asset_id"])
            {
                raw_tape.Columns.Add("asset_id", typeof(int));
                foreach (DataRow row in raw_tape.Rows)
                {
                    string originator = null;
                    string property_address = null;
                    if (raw_tape.Columns.Contains("originator"))
                        originator = row["originator"] as string;
                    if (raw_tape.Columns.Contains("property_address"))
                        property_address = row["property_address"] as string;

                    long asset_id = PistonLib.Assets.GetAssetId(server, row["loan_id"] as string,originator,property_address,true).Value;
                    row["asset_id"] = asset_id;
                }
                raw_tape.AcceptChanges();
            }

            LoadOutput lo = new LoadOutput { removed_data =  removed_data, clean_tape = raw_tape };
            return lo;
        }

        public static DataSet GetRemitSummary(string server)
        {
            
            string sql = "select t.tape_id, t.account_id, t.tape_type, t.account, t.asof, t.cutoff_date, sum(case when td.LOAN_ID is not null then 1 else 0 end) [loans], sum(td.balance) [balance], sum(td.gwac*td.balance)/sum(NULLIF(td.balance,0)) [gwac], sum(td.margin*td.balance)/sum(NULLIF(td.balance,0)) [margin], t.update_time [load_time],t.note,max(replace(replace(t.loaded_by,'@saludagrade.com',''),'@unlock.com','')) [loaded_by],case when t.tapetype_id = 2 and t.latest_tapetype_month = 0 then 'DarkGray' else null end [txt_color]  from     vTapesEx t    left join vTapeDetail td on td.tape_id = t.tape_id group by t.tape_id , t.account_id, t.tape_type, t.account, t.cutoff_date, t.update_time , t.asof,t.note,case when t.tapetype_id = 2 and t.latest_tapetype_month = 0 then 'DarkGray' else null end  order by t.tape_id desc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            
            DataSet s = q.Execute();
            
            
            return s;
        }

        public static int? GetTapeId(string server,int? tapetype_id,int account_id,DateTime cutoff_date, DateTime asOf,string note,bool create_if_no_exists,Nullable<int> tapemap_id,string filename)
        {
            int? remitload_id = GetLoadId(server, account_id, asOf, cutoff_date);
            if (create_if_no_exists && remitload_id == null)
                remitload_id = CreateTape(server, tapetype_id.Value, account_id,cutoff_date, asOf, note,tapemap_id, filename);
            return remitload_id;
        }

        public static string ArchiveTape(string server,int tape_id,string src_filename)
        {
            string base_tape_dir = Database.Common.GetGlobal<string>(server, "TAPE_DIR", true, true);
            int account_id = PistonLib.Tapes.GetAccountIdFromTape(server, tape_id);
            string account_name = PistonLib.Accounts.GetSingleAttribute<string>(server, account_id, "name");
            DateTime asOf = PistonLib.Tapes.GetGeneric<DateTime>(server, tape_id, "asOf");
            string folder = Path.Combine(base_tape_dir, $"{tape_id} - {account_name}");
            string new_folder = Path.Combine(base_tape_dir, folder);
            string new_file = UtilsLib.FileLib.CopyFileToDirectorySmartly(src_filename, new_folder, true);
            FileLib.MarkFileReadOnly(new_file);
            return new_folder;
        }


        public static void RecordMappingIssues(string server,int tape_id, List<string> missing)
        {
            string sql = "insert into TapeMapIssues (tape_id,[column]) values (@tape_id,@column)";
            foreach(string s in missing)
            {
                Query q = new Query(sql, server);
                q.AddParameter("@tape_id", tape_id);
                q.AddParameter("@column", s);
                q.Execute();
            }
        }
        public class TapeLoaderHelper
        {
            public int? tape_id;
            public string archive_tape_name;
            public int lines_loaded = 0;
            public bool tape_processed = false;
            public string error = null;
        }
        public static TapeLoaderHelper CreateAndLoadTape(string server,bool archive_tape, int tapetype_id,int account_id,DateTime cutoff_date,DateTime asOf,string notes,int? tapemap_id,string full_filename,IETA eta,LoadOutput lo,bool process_tape)
        {
            TapeLoaderHelper tlh = new TapeLoaderHelper();
            if(null == lo)
            {
                
                var tape_table = XL.FileReaderSimple.ReadFileSimple(full_filename, true);
                if(null == tape_table)
                {
                    tlh.error = "File Not Found";
                    return tlh;
                }
                lo = PistonLib.Tapes.TransformTape(server, tapemap_id, tape_table, true, true, true);
 
            }
            tlh.tape_id = PistonLib.Tapes.CreateTape(server, tapetype_id, account_id, cutoff_date, asOf, notes, tapemap_id, Path.GetFileName(full_filename));
            if (archive_tape && null != tlh.tape_id)
            {
                if (!File.Exists(full_filename))
                    tlh.error = "File Not Archived";
                else
                    tlh.archive_tape_name = PistonLib.Tapes.ArchiveTape(server, tlh.tape_id.Value, full_filename);
            }
            bool missing_fields = lo.clean_tape.RowsAllHaveValue("loan_id");
            if (!missing_fields)
            {
                tlh.error = "Missing Fields (loan_id)";
                return tlh;
            }
            RecordMappingIssues(server, tlh.tape_id.Value, lo.removed_data.Columns.Cast<DataColumn>().Select(x => x.ColumnName).ToList());
                                 
            tlh.lines_loaded = PistonLib.Tapes.LoadTape(server, tlh.tape_id.Value, lo.clean_tape, eta);
            if(null != eta)
                eta.Complete();
            if(process_tape)
            {
                tlh.tape_processed = true;
                PistonLib.Tapes.ProcessTapes(server, tlh.tape_id.Value, null);
            }
            return tlh;
        }

        public static void ViewArchivedTape(string server,int tape_id)
        {
            string base_tape_dir = Database.Common.GetGlobal<string>(server, "TAPE_DIR", true, true);
            string search = $"{tape_id} -";
            string[] matching_folders = Directory.GetDirectories(base_tape_dir, search + "*");
            if(matching_folders.Length == 1)
            {
                UtilsLib.FileLib.SpawnProcess(matching_folders[0],true,true);
            }
            else
                throw new Exception("Couldn't match dir");
        }

        public static bool TapeExists(string server, int account_id, DateTime asOf, DateTime cutoff_date) 
        {
            return null != GetLoadId(server, account_id, asOf, cutoff_date);
        }
        public static int? GetLoadId(string server, int account_id, DateTime asOf,DateTime cutoff_date)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vTapes where account_id = @account_id and asOf = @asOf and cutoff_date = @cutoff_date";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asOf", asOf);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            q.AddParameter("@cutoff_date", cutoff_date);
            return q.ExecuteSingleNullable<int>("tape_id");
        }

namespace PistonLib
{
    public static class Trades
    {


        public class Trade
        {
            public int id { get; set; }
            public int trade_id { get; set; }
            public string loan_id { get; set; }
            public int asset_id { get; set; }
            public double oface { get; set; }
            public double cface { get; set; }
            public double price { get; set; }
            public double accrued_interest { get; set; }
            public string buy_sell { get; set; }
            public int account_id { get; set; }
            public int counterparty_id { get; set; }
            public DateTime trade_date { get; set; }
            public DateTime settle_date { get; set; }
            public int? tape_id { get; set; }
            public string note { get; set; }
            public string ticket_type { get; set; }
            public long? linker_id { get; set; }
            public double? net_proceeds { get; set; }

            public int? wiretemplatetype_id { get; set; }
            public string counterparty { get; set; }
            public Trade(int id_, int trade_id_, int asset_id_,string loan_id_, double oface_, double cface_, double price_, double accrued_interest_, DateTime? update_time_, string update_by_, DateTime? update_time_ny_, string buy_sell_, int account_id_, int counterparty_id_, DateTime trade_date_, DateTime settle_date_, int? tape_id_, string note_, string ticket_type_, long? linker_id, double net_proceeds,int? wiretemplatetype_id,string counterparty_)
            {
                this.id = id_;
                this.trade_id = trade_id_;
                this.asset_id = asset_id_;
                this.loan_id = loan_id_;
                this.oface = oface_;
                this.cface = cface_;
                this.price = price_;
                this.accrued_interest = accrued_interest_;
                this.buy_sell = buy_sell_;
                this.account_id = account_id_;
                this.counterparty_id = counterparty_id_;
                this.trade_date = trade_date_;
                this.settle_date = settle_date_;
                this.tape_id = tape_id_;
                this.note = note_;
                this.ticket_type = ticket_type_;
                this.linker_id = linker_id;
                this.net_proceeds = net_proceeds;
                this.wiretemplatetype_id = wiretemplatetype_id;
                this.counterparty = counterparty_;

            }
        }


        public static List<Trade> GetTrades(string server, int trade_id)
        {
            List<Trade> t = new List<Trade>();
            List<int> tradedetail_ids = GetTradeDetailIds(server, trade_id);
            foreach(int tradedetail_id in tradedetail_ids)
                t.Add(GetTradeSingle(server, tradedetail_id));
            return t;
        }
        public static Trade GetTradeSingle(string server, int tradedetail_id)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vTradesEx t where t.tradedetail_id = @tradedetail_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@tradedetail_id", tradedetail_id);
            var t = q.ExecuteDictSingleRow<object>();

            return new Trade(t["tradedetail_id"].AsInt().Value, t["trade_id"].AsInt().Value, t["asset_id"].AsInt().Value, t["loan_id"].ToString(), t["oface"].AsDouble().Value, t["cface"].AsDouble().Value, t["price"].AsDouble().Value, t["accrued_interest"].AsDouble().Value, null, null, null, t["buy_sell"] as string, t["account_id"].AsInt().Value, t["counterparty_id"].AsInt().Value, t["trade_date"].AsDate().Value, t["settle_date"].AsDate().Value, t["tape_id"].AsInt(), t["note"] as string, t["ticket_type"] as string, t["linker_id"].AsInt(), t["net_proceeds"].AsDouble().Value, t["wiretemplatetype_id"].AsInt(), t["counterparty"]?.ToString());
        }

        public static DataTable GetTrades(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select t.trade_id,count(*) [ln_count],account_id,buy_sell,counterparty_id,sum(t.cface) [cface],trade_date,settle_date,max(t.update_time_ny) [load_time],max(t.update_by) [who_loaded],sum(net_proceeds) [net_proceeds],t.ticket_type,max(tape_id) [tape_id_latest] from vTradesEx t group by t.trade_id,account_id,buy_sell,counterparty_id,trade_date,settle_date,t.update_by,t.ticket_type,account order by settle_date,account desc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static int LinkTrades(string server,List<int> tradedetail_ids)
        {
            int new_trade_id = Database.Common.GetNextId(server, "TRADE_ID");
            string sql = "update t set trade_id = @new_trade_id from Trades t join @tradedetail_ids td on td.item = t.id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@new_trade_id", new_trade_id);
            q.AddParameter("@tradedetail_ids", tradedetail_ids);
            q.Execute();
            return new_trade_id;
        }

        public static T? GetSingleAttributeNullable<T>(string server, string asset_id, string db_field, bool use_cache) where T : struct
        {
            string sql = "select top 1 * from vTradesEx t join vAssets a on a.asset_id = t.asset_id where t.buy_sell = 'B' and t.counterparty_id != 0 and  (t.asset_id = try_convert(bigint,@asset_id) or a.loan_id = @asset_id) order by t.trade_date desc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.UseCache = use_cache;
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            return q.ExecuteSingleNullable<T>(db_field);
        }

        public static T? GetSingleAttributeNullableDetail<T>(string server, int tradedetail_id, string db_field, bool use_cache) where T : struct
        {
            string sql = "select top 1 * from vTradesEx t where tradedetail_id = @tradedetail_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.UseCache = use_cache;
            q.AddParameter("@tradedetail_id", tradedetail_id);
            return q.ExecuteSingleNullable<T>(db_field);
        }
        public static T GetSingleAttribute<T>(string server, string asset_id, string db_field, bool use_cache)
        {
            string sql = "select top 1 * from vTradesEx t join vAssets a on a.asset_id = t.asset_id where t.buy_sell = 'B' and t.counterparty_id != 0 and (t.asset_id = try_convert(bigint,@asset_id) or a.loan_id = @asset_id) order by t.trade_date desc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.UseCache = use_cache;
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<T>(db_field);
        }

        public static T GetSingleAttributeFromTrade<T>(string server,int trade_id, string db_field, bool use_cache)
        {
            string sql = "select top 1 * from vTradesEx t where t.buy_sell = 'B' and t.counterparty_id != 0 and t.trade_id = @trade_id order by t.trade_date desc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.UseCache = use_cache;
            q.AddParameter("@trade_id", trade_id);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<T>(db_field);
        }
        public static Query GetTradesQuery(string server, List<int> asset_ids)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vTradesEx c join @assets a on a.item = c.asset_id order by c.trade_date desc";
            if (null == asset_ids)
                sql = "select * from vTradesEx c order by trade_date desc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@assets", asset_ids);

            return q;
        }

        public static List<int> GetDetailIdsFromDrawIds(string server,List<long> draw_ids,bool only_blank_trade_ids)
        {
            
            string sql = "select tradedetail_id from vTrades t join vLinker l on l.linker_id = t.linker_id join @draw_ids d on d.item = l.foreign_id where t.ticket_type = 'D' and ((@only_blank_trade_ids = 1 and t.trade_id is null) or (@only_blank_trade_ids = 0))";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@draw_ids", draw_ids);
            q.AddParameter("@only_blank_trade_ids", only_blank_trade_ids);
            return q.ExecuteList<int>("tradedetail_id");
        }

        public static int InsertTradeDetail(string server, int trade_id,int asset_id,double oface,double cface,double price,double accrued,DateTime trade_date,DateTime settle_date,string buy_sell,int account_id,int counterparty_id,int? tape_id,string note,string ticket_type)
        {
            string sql = "insert into Trades (trade_id,asset_id,oface,cface,price,accrued_interest,trade_date,settle_date,buy_sell,account_id,counterparty_id,tape_id,note,ticket_type) output inserted.id values (@trade_id,@asset_id,@oface,@cface,@price,@accured,@trade_date,@settle_date,@buy_sell,@account_id,@counterparty_id,@tape_id,@note,@ticket_type)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@trade_id", trade_id);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.AddParameter("@oface", oface);
            q.AddParameter("@cface", cface);
            q.AddParameter("@price", price);

            q.AddParameter("@trade_date", trade_date);
            q.AddParameter("@settle_date", settle_date);

            q.AddParameter("@tape_id", tape_id);
            q.AddParameter("@note", note);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            q.AddParameter("@counterparty_id", counterparty_id);
            q.AddParameter("@ticket_type", ticket_type);

        public static bool TradeExists(string server, long asset_id, char buy_sell, double oface, int account_id, int counterparty_id, DateTime settle_or_trade_date, string ticket_type, bool use_cache,int days_before_or_after)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vTrades t where t.asset_id = @asset_id and buy_sell = @buy_sell and t.oface = @oface and account_id = @account_id and counterparty_id = @counterparty_id and ((settle_date between dateadd(d,-@days_before_or_after,@settle_or_trade_date) and dateadd(d,@days_before_or_after,@settle_or_trade_date))  or (trade_date between dateadd(d,-@days_before_or_after,@settle_or_trade_date) and dateadd(d,@days_before_or_after,@settle_or_trade_date))) and ticket_type=@ticket_type";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.AddParameter("@buy_sell", buy_sell);
            q.AddParameter("@oface", oface);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            q.AddParameter("@counterparty_id", counterparty_id);
            q.AddParameter("@settle_or_trade_date", settle_or_trade_date);
            q.AddParameter("@ticket_type", ticket_type);
            q.AddParameter("@days_before_or_after", days_before_or_after);
            q.UseCache = use_cache;
            return q.ExecuteTable().Rows.Count > 0;
        }
        public static int NewTrade(string server, int account_id,char buy_sell,double oface,int counterparty_id,DateTime trade_date,DateTime settle_date,string note,int? tape_id,string ticket_type)
        {
            string sql = "insert into Trades (account_id,buy_sell,counterparty_id,trade_date,settle_date,note,tape_id,oface,cface,ticket_type) output inserted.id values (@account_id,@buy_sell,@counterparty_id,@trade_date,@settle_date,@note,@tape_id,@oface,@cface,@ticket_type)";
            Query q = new Query(sql,server);
            q.AddParameter("account_id", account_id);
            q.AddParameter("@buy_sell", buy_sell);
            q.AddParameter("@counterparty_id", counterparty_id);
            q.AddParameter("@trade_date", trade_date);
            q.AddParameter("@settle_date", settle_date);
            q.AddParameter("@note", note);
            q.AddParameter("@oface", oface);
            q.AddParameter("@oface", oface);
            q.AddParameter("@tape_id", tape_id);
            q.AddParameter("@ticket_type", ticket_type);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<int>();
        }

        }
        public static DataTable BuySellTable()
        {
            DataTable dataTable = new DataTable();
            dataTable.Columns.Add("BUY/SELL", typeof(string));
            dataTable.Columns.Add("id", typeof(string));
            dataTable.Rows.Add("BUY", "B");
            dataTable.Rows.Add("SELL", "S");
            return dataTable;
        }
    }

--- FILE: Saluda\PistonLib\Transactions.cs ---
namespace PistonLib
{
    public static class Transactions
    {
        public static int? LoadBuilderTransactions(string server,string filename)
        {
            int loaded = 0;
            try
            {
                bool file_loaded = LoadedTransFile(server, filename);
                if (file_loaded)
                    return 0;
                string transaction_range = "transactions";
                
                XLHelper xlh = new XLHelper(null);
                xlh.CreateNewApp(false);
                xlh.ToggleAppVisible(true);
                xlh.OpenSheet(filename, true);
                string transaction_tab = xlh.AllTabNames().FindAll(n => n.Contains("Transaction")).First().ToString();
                if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(transaction_tab))
                {
                    return null;
                }
                xlh.ActivateSheet(transaction_tab);
                xlh.CreateNamedRangeFromUsed(transaction_range);
                XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, transaction_range);
                var rows = xlt.AllRows("Transaction Amount");
                foreach (var row in rows)
                {
                    string loan_field = row.ContainsColumn("Loan") ? "Loan" : "LoanNo";
                    string loan_id = row[loan_field];
                    string desc = row["Loan #"];
                    string transaction_category = row["Transaction Category"];
                    string transaction_type = row["Transaction Type"];
                    double? amount = row["Transaction Amount"].AsDouble();
                    DateTime? effective_date = row["Effective Date"].AsDate();
                    double? extension_fee = row.ContainsColumn("Extension Fee") ? row["Extension Fees"].AsDouble() : null;
                    bool exist = BuilderTransactionExists(server, loan_id, transaction_category, transaction_type, amount, effective_date, extension_fee);
                    if (!exist)
                    {
                        InsertBuilderTransaction(server, loan_id, desc, transaction_category, transaction_type, amount, effective_date, extension_fee, filename);
                        loaded++;
                    }
                }
                xlh.CloseAllSheets(false);
                xlh.Quit();
            }catch { return null; }
            return loaded;
        }


        public static bool LoadedTransFile(string server, string filename)
        {
            string sql = "select * from BuilderTransactions t where t.filename = @filename";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@filename", filename);
            return q.ExecuteTable().Rows.Count > 0;
        }
        public static void InsertBuilderTransaction(string server, string loan_id, string desc, string category, string type, double? amount, DateTime? effective_date, double? extension_fees,string filename)
        {
            string sql = "insert into BuilderTransactions (loan_id,description,category,[type],amount,effective_date,extension_fees,filename) values (@loan_id,@desc,@category,@type,@amount,@effective_date,@extension_fees,@filename)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@loan_id", loan_id);
            q.AddParameter("@category", category);
            q.AddParameter("@desc", desc);
            q.AddParameter("@type", type);
            q.AddParameter("@amount", amount);
            q.AddParameter("@effective_date", effective_date);
            q.AddParameter("@extension_fees", extension_fees);
            q.AddParameter("@filename", filename);
            q.Execute();
        }
        public static bool BuilderTransactionExists(string server, string loan_id, string category, string type, double? amount, DateTime? effective_date, double? extension_fees)
        {
            string sql = "select * from BuilderTransactions b where b.loan_id = @loan_id and category = @category and type = @type and amount = @amount and effective_date = @effective_date and extension_fees = @extension_fees";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@loan_id", loan_id);
            q.AddParameter("@category", category);
            q.AddParameter("@type", type);
            q.AddParameter("@amount", amount);
            q.AddParameter("@effective_date", effective_date);
            q.AddParameter("@extension_fees", extension_fees);
            return q.ExecuteTable().Rows.Count > 0;
        }


    }
}


--- FILE: Saluda\PistonLib\Usage.cs ---
namespace PistonLib
{
    public class Usage
    {
        public enum UsageTypes { STARTUP=1,TAPE_LOADED=2,SEARCH=3,DOCS_GENERATED=4,TAPES_LOADED=5}
        public static void RecordUsage(string server, UsageTypes usagetype_id, int? number, int? number_two, string note, string optNote2, string optnote3, int? userID)
        {
            
            DateTime build_time = Assembly.GetExecutingAssembly().GetBuildTime();
            string machine = Environment.MachineName;

            
            string sql = "insert into Usage (user_id,usagetype_id,number,number_2,note,note_2,note_3,build_time,machine) values (@user_id, @usagetype_id, @number, @number_2, @note, @note_2, @note_3,@build_time,@machine)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@usagetype_id", (int)usagetype_id);
            q.AddParameter("@number", number);
            q.AddParameter("@number_2", number_two);
            q.AddParameter("@note", note);
            q.AddParameter("@note_2", optNote2);
            q.AddParameter("@note_3", optnote3);
            q.AddParameter("@user_id", userID);
            q.AddParameter("@build_time", build_time);
            q.AddParameter("@machine", machine);
            q.ExecuteAsync(null);

        }
    }
}

        public static DataSet GetWireSet(string server,string table_prefix, int linker_id)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vWiresEx w where linker_id=@linker_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@linker_id", linker_id);
            DataTable wires = q.ExecuteTable();
            return wires.SplitByRowsIntoTables<int>("wire_num", table_prefix, true);
        }

        public static DataTable GetWireTemplateTypes(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vWireTemplateTypes";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }
        public static int? GetPrimaryWireTemplate(string server,int account_id)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vWireTemplates wt where wt.account_id = @account_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            var tbl = q.ExecuteTable();
            if (tbl.Rows.Count == 1)
                return System.Convert.ToInt32(tbl.Rows[0]["wiretemplate_id"]);
            return null;
        }

        public static List<int> GetWireTemplates(string server, int account_id,int? wiretemplatetype_id)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vWireTemplates wt where wt.account_id = @account_id and (@wiretemplatetype_id is null or wiretemplatetype_id=@wiretemplatetype_id)";

            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            q.AddParameter("@wiretemplatetype_id", wiretemplatetype_id);
            return q.ExecuteList<int>("wiretemplate_id");
        }

            q.AddParameter("@wiretemplate_id", wiretemplate_id);

--- FILE: Saluda\Saluda Toolkit\Saluda Toolkit\Clean.cs ---
namespace Saluda_Toolkit
{
    public static class Clean
    {
        [ExcelFunction(Description = "Find FTF Loan ID")]
        public static object FindFTFLoanID(string loan_id)
        {
            string sql = $"select loan_id from Assets where loan_id like '%{loan_id}'";
            Query q = new Query(sql, SaludaToolkit.DB);
            q.UseCache = true;
            DataTable t = q.ExecuteTable();
            if (t.Rows.Count == 1)
                return t.Rows[0][0];
            return "";
        }

        [ExcelFunction(Description = "Find Loan ID from Address")]
        public static object FindLoanIdFromAddress(string address)
        {
            string address_1 = address;
            if (address.Contains(","))
                address_1 = address_1.Split(',')[0].Trim();
            string sql = $"select loan_id from Assets where address_full like '{address_1}%'";
            Query q = new Query(sql, SaludaToolkit.DB);
            q.UseCache = true;
            DataTable t = q.ExecuteTable();
            if (t.Rows.Count == 1)
                return t.Rows[0][0];
            return "";
        }

    }
}

--- FILE: Saluda\Saluda Toolkit\Saluda Toolkit\Draws.cs ---
namespace Saluda_Toolkit
{
    public static class Draws
    {
        [ExcelFunction(Name = "Piston.DrawExists")]
        public static object DrawExist(long asset_id,int account_id,int counterparty_id,double oface,DateTime settle_date)
        {
            return PistonLib.Trades.TradeExists(SaludaToolkit.DB, asset_id, 'B', oface, account_id, counterparty_id, settle_date, "D", false,7);
        }

        [ExcelFunction(Name = "Piston.InsertDrawIfNoExist")]
        public static object InsertDrawIfNoExists(long asset_id, int account_id, int counterparty_id, double oface, DateTime settle_date)
        {
            bool exists = PistonLib.Trades.TradeExists(SaludaToolkit.DB, asset_id, 'B', oface, account_id, counterparty_id, settle_date, "D", false, 7);
            if(!exists)
            {
                return PistonLib.Trades.NewTrade(SaludaToolkit.DB, account_id, 'B', oface, counterparty_id, settle_date, settle_date, "Toolkit - Manual",null,"D");
            }
            return "<TRADE ALREADY EXISTS>";
        }


    }
}


--- FILE: Saluda\Saluda Toolkit\Saluda Toolkit\Files.cs ---
namespace Saluda_Toolkit
{
    public static class Files
    {
        [ExcelFunction(Description = "RenameFile")]
        public static string RenameFile(string source_full_path,string dest_full_path)
        {
            try
            {
                System.IO.File.Copy(source_full_path, dest_full_path, true);
                return "DONE";
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                return ex.Message;
            }

        }

    }

--- FILE: Saluda\Saluda Toolkit\Saluda Toolkit\Position.cs ---
namespace Saluda_Toolkit
{
    public static class Position
    {
        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object HistoricalOwner(string asset_id_or_loan_id,DateTime? asOf)
        {
            
            int? asset_id = PistonLib.Assets.FindAssetID<int>(SaludaToolkit.DB, asset_id_or_loan_id);
            if (null == asset_id)
                return "<ASSET ID NOT MATCHED>";
            return PistonLib.Positions.HistoricalOwner(SaludaToolkit.DB,asset_id.Value, asOf,"account_id");
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object CurrentOwner(string asset_id_or_loan_id)
        {
            int? account_id = PistonLib.Trades.GetSingleAttributeNullable<int>(SaludaToolkit.DB, asset_id_or_loan_id, "primary_owner_account_id", true);
            if (null != account_id)
                return PistonLib.Accounts.GetSingleAttribute<string>(SaludaToolkit.DB, account_id.Value, "name");
            return "";
        }
    }
}
