--- FILE: Saluda\Saluda Toolkit\Saluda Toolkit\Registration\ArrayResizer.cs ---
namespace Saluda_Toolkit
{
    
    public static class ResizeTestFunctions
    {
        
        public static object[,] MakeArray(int rows, int columns)
        {
            object[,] result = new object[rows, columns];
            for (int i = 0; i < rows; i++)
            {
                for (int j = 0; j < columns; j++)
                {
                    result[i, j] = i + j;
                }
            }

            return result;
        }

        public static double[,] MakeArrayDoubles(int rows, int columns)
        {
            double[,] result = new double[rows, columns];
            for (int i = 0; i < rows; i++)
            {
                for (int j = 0; j < columns; j++)
                {
                    result[i, j] = i + (j / 1000.0);
                }
            }

            return result;
        }

        public static object MakeMixedArrayAndResize(int rows, int columns)
        {
            object[,] result = new object[rows, columns];
            for (int j = 0; j < columns; j++)
            {
                result[0, j] = "Col " + j;
            }
            for (int i = 1; i < rows; i++)
            {
                for (int j = 0; j < columns; j++)
                {
                    result[i, j] = i + (j * 0.1);
                }
            }

            return ArrayResizer.Resize(result);
        }

        
        public static object MakeArrayAndResize(int rows, int columns, string unused, string unusedtoo)
        {
            object[,] result = MakeArray(rows, columns);
            return ArrayResizer.Resize(result);

            
            
            
        }

        public static double[,] MakeArrayAndResizeDoubles(int rows, int columns)
        {
            double[,] result = MakeArrayDoubles(rows, columns);
            return ArrayResizer.ResizeDoubles(result);
        }
    }

    public class ArrayResizer : XlCall
    {
        
        
        public static object Resize(object[,] array)
        {
            var caller = Excel(xlfCaller) as ExcelReference;
            if (caller == null)
                return array;

            int rows = array.GetLength(0);
            int columns = array.GetLength(1);

            if (rows == 0 || columns == 0)
                return array;

            if ((caller.RowLast - caller.RowFirst + 1 == rows) &&
                (caller.ColumnLast - caller.ColumnFirst + 1 == columns))
            {
                
                return array;
            }

            var rowLast = caller.RowFirst + rows - 1;
            var columnLast = caller.ColumnFirst + columns - 1;

            
            if (rowLast > ExcelDnaUtil.ExcelLimits.MaxRows - 1 ||
                columnLast > ExcelDnaUtil.ExcelLimits.MaxColumns - 1)
            {
                
                
                return ExcelError.ExcelErrorValue;
            }

            
            ExcelAsyncUtil.QueueAsMacro(() =>
            {
                
                var target = new ExcelReference(caller.RowFirst, rowLast, caller.ColumnFirst, columnLast, caller.SheetId);
                DoResize(target); 
            });
            
            return array;
        }

        public static double[,] ResizeDoubles(double[,] array)
        {
            var caller = Excel(xlfCaller) as ExcelReference;
            if (caller == null)
                return array;

            int rows = array.GetLength(0);
            int columns = array.GetLength(1);

            if (rows == 0 || columns == 0)
                return array;

            if ((caller.RowLast - caller.RowFirst + 1 == rows) &&
                (caller.ColumnLast - caller.ColumnFirst + 1 == columns))
            {
                
                return array;
            }

            var rowLast = caller.RowFirst + rows - 1;
            var columnLast = caller.ColumnFirst + columns - 1;

            if (rowLast > ExcelDnaUtil.ExcelLimits.MaxRows - 1 ||
                columnLast > ExcelDnaUtil.ExcelLimits.MaxColumns - 1)
            {
                
                
                return null;
            }

            
            ExcelAsyncUtil.QueueAsMacro(() =>
            {
                
                var target = new ExcelReference(caller.RowFirst, rowLast, caller.ColumnFirst, columnLast, caller.SheetId);
                DoResize(target); 
            });
            
            return array;
        }

        static void DoResize(ExcelReference target)
        {
            
            using (new ExcelEchoOffHelper())
            using (new ExcelCalculationManualHelper())
            {
                ExcelReference firstCell = new ExcelReference(target.RowFirst, target.RowFirst, target.ColumnFirst, target.ColumnFirst, target.SheetId);

                
                string formula = (string)Excel(xlfGetCell, 41, firstCell);
                bool isFormulaArray = (bool)Excel(xlfGetCell, 49, firstCell);
                if (isFormulaArray)
                {
                    
                    using (new ExcelSelectionHelper(firstCell))
                    {
                        
                        Excel(xlcSelectSpecial, 6);
                        ExcelReference oldArray = (ExcelReference)Excel(xlfSelection);

                        oldArray.SetValue(ExcelEmpty.Value);
                    }
                }
                
                bool isR1C1Mode = (bool)Excel(xlfGetWorkspace, 4);
                string formulaR1C1 = formula;
                if (!isR1C1Mode)
                {
                    object formulaR1C1Obj;
                    XlReturn formulaR1C1Return = TryExcel(xlfFormulaConvert, out formulaR1C1Obj, formula, true, false, ExcelMissing.Value, firstCell);
                    if (formulaR1C1Return != XlReturn.XlReturnSuccess || formulaR1C1Obj is ExcelError)
                    {
                        string firstCellAddress = (string)Excel(xlfReftext, firstCell, true);
                        Excel(xlcAlert, "Cannot resize array formula at " + firstCellAddress + " - formula might be too long when converted to R1C1 format.");
                        firstCell.SetValue("'" + formula);
                        return;
                    }
                    formulaR1C1 = (string)formulaR1C1Obj;
                }
                
                object ignoredResult;
                
                XlReturn formulaArrayReturn = TryExcel(xlcFormulaArray, out ignoredResult, formulaR1C1, target);
                

                

                if (formulaArrayReturn != XlReturn.XlReturnSuccess)
                {
                    string firstCellAddress = (string)Excel(xlfReftext, firstCell, true);
                    Excel(xlcAlert, "Cannot resize array formula at " + firstCellAddress + " - result might overlap another array.");
                    
                    firstCell.SetValue("'" + formula);
                }
            }
        }
    }

    
    
    public class ExcelEchoOffHelper : XlCall, IDisposable
    {
        object oldEcho;

        public ExcelEchoOffHelper()
        {
            oldEcho = Excel(xlfGetWorkspace, 40);
            Excel(xlcEcho, false);
        }

        public void Dispose()
        {
            Excel(xlcEcho, oldEcho);
        }
    }

    public class ExcelCalculationManualHelper : XlCall, IDisposable
    {
        object oldCalculationMode;

        public ExcelCalculationManualHelper()
        {
            oldCalculationMode = Excel(xlfGetDocument, 14);
            Excel(xlcOptionsCalculation, 3);
        }

        public void Dispose()
        {
            Excel(xlcOptionsCalculation, oldCalculationMode);
        }
    }

    
    
    
    public class ExcelSelectionHelper : XlCall, IDisposable
    {
        object oldSelectionOnActiveSheet;
        object oldActiveCellOnActiveSheet;

        object oldSelectionOnRefSheet;
        object oldActiveCellOnRefSheet;

        public ExcelSelectionHelper(ExcelReference refToSelect)
        {
            
            oldSelectionOnActiveSheet = Excel(xlfSelection);
            oldActiveCellOnActiveSheet = Excel(xlfActiveCell);

            
            string refSheet = (string)Excel(xlSheetNm, refToSelect);
            Excel(xlcWorkbookSelect, new object[] { refSheet });

            
            oldSelectionOnRefSheet = Excel(xlfSelection);
            oldActiveCellOnRefSheet = Excel(xlfActiveCell);

            
            Excel(xlcFormulaGoto, refToSelect);
        }

        public void Dispose()
        {
            
            Excel(xlcSelect, oldSelectionOnRefSheet, oldActiveCellOnRefSheet);

            
            string oldActiveSheet = (string)Excel(xlSheetNm, oldSelectionOnActiveSheet);
            Excel(xlcWorkbookSelect, new object[] { oldActiveSheet });

            
            Excel(xlcSelect, oldSelectionOnActiveSheet, oldActiveCellOnActiveSheet);
        }
    }

}


--- FILE: Saluda\Saluda Toolkit\Saluda Toolkit\Registration\CacheFunctionExecutionHandler.cs ---
namespace Saluda_Toolkit
{
    
    [AttributeUsage(AttributeTargets.Method)]
    public class CacheAttribute : Attribute
    {
        public TimeSpan CacheTimeout;
        public CacheAttribute(int cacheTimeoutSeconds)
        {
            CacheTimeout = TimeSpan.FromSeconds(cacheTimeoutSeconds);
        }
    }

    
    public class CacheFunctionExecutionHandler : FunctionExecutionHandler
    {
        static readonly ObjectCache _cache = MemoryCache.Default;
        readonly TimeSpan _cacheTimeout;

        public CacheFunctionExecutionHandler(TimeSpan cacheTimeout)
        {
            _cacheTimeout = cacheTimeout;
        }

        public override void OnEntry(FunctionExecutionArgs args)
        {
            string key = GenerateKey(args);
            args.Tag = key;

            object result = _cache[key];
            if (result != null)
            {
                
                args.ReturnValue = result;
                args.FlowBehavior = FlowBehavior.Return;
            }
        }

        public override void OnSuccess(FunctionExecutionArgs args)
        {
            
            _cache.Add((string)args.Tag, args.ReturnValue, 
                new CacheItemPolicy { AbsoluteExpiration = DateTime.UtcNow + _cacheTimeout });
        }

        string GenerateKey(FunctionExecutionArgs args)
        {
            var keyBuilder = new StringBuilder(args.FunctionName);
            foreach (var arg in args.Arguments)
            {
                keyBuilder.Append('\0');    
                keyBuilder.Append(arg);
            }
            return keyBuilder.ToString();
        }
        

        
        public static FunctionExecutionHandler CacheHandlerSelector(ExcelFunctionRegistration functionRegistration)
        {
            
            if (functionRegistration.CustomAttributes.OfType<CacheAttribute>().Any())
            {
                
                var cacheAtt = functionRegistration.CustomAttributes.OfType<CacheAttribute>().First();
                functionRegistration.CustomAttributes.RemoveAll(att => att is CacheAttribute);

                return new CacheFunctionExecutionHandler(cacheAtt.CacheTimeout);
            }
            return null;
        }

    }

    
}


--- FILE: Saluda\Saluda Toolkit\Saluda Toolkit\Registration\InstanceMemberRegistration.cs ---
namespace Saluda_Toolkit
{
    
    [AttributeUsage(AttributeTargets.All)]
    public class ExcelObjectAttribute : Attribute
    {
    }

    [ExcelObject]
    public class TestClass
    {
        string _content;

        public TestClass(string content)
        {
            _content = content;
        }

        public string GetContent()
        {
            return "Content is " + _content;
        }

        
        
        
        
        
    }

    class InstanceMemberRegistration
    {
        public static LambdaExpression WrapInstanceMethod(MethodInfo method)
        {
            
            
            
            

            var instanceParam = Expression.Parameter(method.DeclaringType, method.DeclaringType.Name);
            var callParams = method.GetParameters().Select(p => Expression.Parameter(p.ParameterType, p.Name)).ToList();
            var allParams = new List<ParameterExpression>();
            allParams.Add(instanceParam);
            allParams.AddRange(callParams);

            var callExpr = Expression.Call(instanceParam, method, callParams);
            return Expression.Lambda(callExpr, method.Name, allParams);
        }

        public static void TestInstanceRegistration()
        {
            var instanceMethod = typeof(TestClass).GetMethod("GetContent");
            var lambda = WrapInstanceMethod(instanceMethod);

            
            var paramConversionConfig = new ParameterConversionConfiguration()
                .AddParameterConversion((string content) => new TestClass(content));

            
            var reg = new ExcelFunctionRegistration(lambda);
            var processed = ParameterConversionRegistration.ProcessParameterConversions(new[] { reg }, paramConversionConfig);
            processed.RegisterFunctions();
        }
    }
}

namespace Saluda_Toolkit
{
    
    

    

    [AttributeUsage(AttributeTargets.Method)]
    public class SuppressInDialogAttribute :  Attribute, IFunctionExecutionHandler
    {
        readonly string _dialogResult;
        public SuppressInDialogAttribute(string dialogMessage = "!!! NOT CALCULATED IN DIALOG !!!")
        {
            _dialogResult = dialogMessage;
        }

        public void OnEntry(FunctionExecutionArgs args)
        {
            if (ExcelDnaUtil.IsInFunctionWizard())
            {
                args.ReturnValue = _dialogResult;
                args.FlowBehavior = FlowBehavior.Return;
            }
            
        }

        
        public void OnSuccess(FunctionExecutionArgs args) { }
        public void OnException(FunctionExecutionArgs args) { }
        public void OnExit(FunctionExecutionArgs args) { }
    }

    public static class SuppressInDialogFunctionExecutionHandler
    {
        public static IFunctionExecutionHandler SuppressInDialogSelector(ExcelFunctionRegistration functionRegistration)
        {
            
            if (functionRegistration.CustomAttributes.OfType<SuppressInDialogAttribute>().Any() &&
                (functionRegistration.FunctionLambda.ReturnType == typeof(object) || 
                 functionRegistration.FunctionLambda.ReturnType == typeof(string)))
            {
                
                var suppressAtt = functionRegistration.CustomAttributes.OfType<SuppressInDialogAttribute>().First();
                functionRegistration.CustomAttributes.RemoveAll(att => att is SuppressInDialogAttribute);

                return suppressAtt;
            }
            return null;

        }

    }
}


--- FILE: Saluda\Saluda Toolkit\Saluda Toolkit\Registration\TimingFunctionExecutionHandler.cs ---
namespace Saluda_Toolkit
{
    [AttributeUsage(AttributeTargets.Method)]
    public class TimingAttribute : Attribute
    {
    }

    public class TimingFunctionExecutionHandler : FunctionExecutionHandler
    {
        public override void OnEntry(FunctionExecutionArgs args)
        {
            args.Tag = Stopwatch.StartNew();
        }

        public override void OnExit(FunctionExecutionArgs args)
        {
            var sw = (Stopwatch)args.Tag;
            sw.Stop();

            Debug.WriteLine("{0} executed in {1} milliseconds", args.FunctionName, sw.ElapsedMilliseconds);
        }

        
        static readonly Lazy<TimingFunctionExecutionHandler> _handler =
            new Lazy<TimingFunctionExecutionHandler>(() => new TimingFunctionExecutionHandler());

        internal static FunctionExecutionHandler TimingHandlerSelector(ExcelFunctionRegistration functionRegistration)
        {
            
            if (functionRegistration.CustomAttributes.RemoveAll(att => att is TimingAttribute) == 0)
            {
                
                return null;
            }
            return _handler.Value;
        }
    } 
}


--- FILE: Saluda\Saluda Toolkit\Saluda Toolkit\Registration.cs ---
namespace Saluda_Toolkit
{
    public partial class SaludaToolkit
    {
        static ParameterConversionConfiguration GetPostAsyncReturnConversionConfig()
        {
            
            
            
            
            return new ParameterConversionConfiguration()
                .AddReturnConversion((type, customAttributes) => type != typeof(object) ? null : ((Expression<Func<object, object>>)
                    ((object returnValue) => returnValue.Equals(ExcelError.ExcelErrorNA) ? ExcelError.ExcelErrorGettingData : returnValue)));


        }

        static ParameterConversionConfiguration GetParameterConversionConfig()
        {
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            




            var paramConversionConfig = new ParameterConversionConfiguration()

                
                .AddParameterConversion(ParameterConversions.GetOptionalConversion(treatEmptyAsMissing: true))


                
                .AddParameterConversion((TestType1 value) => new TestType2(value))
                .AddParameterConversion((string value) => new TestType1(value))

                
                .AddReturnConversion((TestType1 value) => value.ToString())
                .AddReturnConversion((Complex value) => new double[2] { value.Real, value.Imaginary })

                

                
                
                
                .AddParameterConversion((object[] inputs) => inputs.Select(TypeConversion.ConvertToString).ToArray())

                
                .AddReturnConversion((Enum value) => value.ToString(), handleSubTypes: true)
                .AddParameterConversion(ParameterConversions.GetEnumStringConversion())

                .AddParameterConversion((object[] input) => new Complex(TypeConversion.ConvertToDouble(input[0]), TypeConversion.ConvertToDouble(input[1])))
                .AddNullableConversion(treatEmptyAsMissing: true, treatNAErrorAsMissing: true);

            return paramConversionConfig;
        }

        static FunctionExecutionConfiguration GetFunctionExecutionHandlerConfig()
        {
            return new FunctionExecutionConfiguration()
                
                .AddFunctionExecutionHandler(CacheFunctionExecutionHandler.CacheHandlerSelector)
                .AddFunctionExecutionHandler(TimingFunctionExecutionHandler.TimingHandlerSelector)
                .AddFunctionExecutionHandler(SuppressInDialogFunctionExecutionHandler.SuppressInDialogSelector);
        }

        
        public class TestType1
        {
            public string Value;
            public TestType1(string value)
            {
                Value = value;
            }

            public override string ToString()
            {
                return "From Type 1 with " + Value;

            public static string dnaTestFunction1(TestType1 tt)
            {
                return "The Test (1) value is " + tt.Value;
            }
        }

        {
            readonly TestType1 _value;
            public TestType2(TestType1 value)
            {
                _value = value;
            }

            
            [ExcelFunction]
            public static string dnaTestFunction2(TestType2 tt)
            {
                return "The Test (2) value is " + tt._value.Value;
            }

            [ExcelFunction]
            public static TestType1 dnaTestFunction2Ret1(TestType2 tt)
            {
                return new TestType1("The Test (2) value is " + tt._value.Value);
            }

            [ExcelFunction]
            public static string dnaJoinStrings(string separator, string[] values)
            {
                return string.Join(separator, values);
            }

            class InstanceMemberRegistration
            {
                public static LambdaExpression WrapInstanceMethod(MethodInfo method)
                {
                    
                    
                    
                    

                    var instanceParam = Expression.Parameter(method.DeclaringType, method.DeclaringType.Name);

                }

                .ProcessMapArrayFunctions(conversionConfig)
                .ProcessParameterConversions(conversionConfig)
                .ProcessAsyncRegistrations(nativeAsyncIfAvailable: false)
                .ProcessParameterConversions(postAsyncReturnConfig)
                .ProcessParamsRegistrations()
                .ProcessFunctionExecutionHandlers(functionHandlerConfig)
                .RegisterFunctions();
            ExcelRegistration.GetExcelCommands().RegisterCommands();
        }

namespace Saluda_Toolkit
{
    public static class CommonSheetHelper
    {
        public static void TemplateHelper(string dest_table)
        {
            var xlh = SaludaToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            int? trade_id = xlh.GetRangeDefaultIfNoExistNullable<int>("trade_id");
            int account_id = PistonLib.Trades.GetSingleAttributeFromTrade<int>(SaludaToolkit.DB, trade_id.Value, "account_id", false);
            if (null == trade_id)
            {
                MessageBox.Show("No Trade Selected");
                return;
            }
            

            DataTable tbl = PistonLib.Trades.GetTapeMaster(SaludaToolkit.DB, trade_id.Value, null);

            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, dest_table);
            Fields f = Fields.GetInstance(SaludaToolkit.DB, Database.FieldHelper.GetFieldTableInternal);
            xlt.DumpData(tbl, true, xlh.WriteStatusBar, null, f);

            var vars = PistonLib.Trades.GetTradeDocGenFields<object>(SaludaToolkit.DB, trade_id.Value);
            xlh.WriteRange(vars);
            xlh.ToggleSheetRowGrouping(null, false);
        }
    }
}

--- FILE: Saluda\Saluda Toolkit\Saluda Toolkit\Sheets\DrawSummary.cs ---
namespace Saluda_Toolkit
{
    using DataTable = System.Data.DataTable;
    public static class DrawSummary
    {

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void GenerateDrawSummary()
        {
            var xlh = SaludaToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            int? trade_id = xlh.GetRangeDefaultIfNoExistNullable<int>("trade_id");
            
            if(null == trade_id)
            {
                MessageBox.Show("No Trade Selected");
                return;
            }
            int account_id = PistonLib.Trades.GetSingleAttributeFromTrade<int>(SaludaToolkit.DB, trade_id.Value, "account_id", false);
            
            DataTable tbl = PistonLib.Trades.GetTapeMaster(SaludaToolkit.DB, trade_id.Value, null);

            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "draw_schedule");
            Fields f = (Fields) Fields.GetInstance(SaludaToolkit.DB, Database.FieldHelper.GetFieldTableInternal).Clone();
            f.RemoveField("draw_amount");
            xlt.DumpData(tbl, true, xlh.WriteStatusBar, null, f);
            xlt.TightenUpTable("loan_id");

            XLTable summary = new XLTable(xlh, "lender_summary");
            

            var sellers = tbl.GetUniqueList<string>("loan_seller");
            sellers.Sort();
            DataTable lenders = sellers.ToDataTable("loan_seller");
            summary.ClearColumns("loan_seller");
            summary.DumpData(lenders, false, xlh.WriteStatusBar, new List<string> { "TOTALS"}, f);
            summary.TightenUpTable("loan_seller");
            xlh.ToggleSheetColumnGrouping(null, false);
            xlh.ToggleSheetRowGrouping(null, false);
        }
    }
}

--- FILE: Saluda\Saluda Toolkit\Saluda Toolkit\Sheets\SSCTemplate.cs ---
namespace Saluda_Toolkit
{
    using DataTable = System.Data.DataTable;
    public static class SSCTemplate
    {

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void GenerateSSCSummary()
        {
            var xlh = SaludaToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            int? trade_id = xlh.GetRangeDefaultIfNoExistNullable<int>("trade_id");

            if (null == trade_id)
            {
                MessageBox.Show("No Trade Selected");
                return;
            }
            

            DataTable tbl = PistonLib.Trades.GetSSCTemplate(SaludaToolkit.DB, trade_id.Value);

            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "ssc_template");
            xlt.ClearAllButHeader(null);
            
            xlh.WriteRange("dump_start", tbl);
            
            
            

            xlh.ToggleSheetColumnGrouping(null, false);
            xlh.ToggleSheetRowGrouping(null, false);
        }
    }
}


--- FILE: Saluda\Saluda Toolkit\Saluda Toolkit\Sheets\Strats.cs ---
namespace Saluda_Toolkit
{
    public static class Strats
    {
        public static DataTable GenerateStratTable(string server,int? tape_id,int? account_id, string which,bool only_active)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.GetStrat @tape_id=@tape_id,@account_id=@account_id,@which=@which,@only_active=@only_active";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@tape_id", tape_id);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            q.AddParameter("@which", which);
            q.AddParameter("@only_active", only_active);
            q.UseCache = false;
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }


        [ExcelFunction(Name = "Strats.GetLabel")]
        public static object GetRemitLabel(string db_field)
        {
            return PistonLib.FieldsHelper.GetSingleAttribute<object>(SaludaToolkit.DB, db_field, "remit_label");
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void GenerateStrats()
        {
            var xlh = SaludaToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            int? tape_id = xlh.GetRangeDefaultIfNoExistNullable<int>("tape_id");
            int? account_id = xlh.GetRangeDefaultIfNoExistNullable<int>("account_id");
            bool only_active = xlh.GetRange<bool>(null,"only_active");
            DateTime cutoff = DateTime.Today;
            if(null != tape_id)
                cutoff = PistonLib.Tapes.GetCutoffFromTape(SaludaToolkit.DB, tape_id.Value);
            
            string save_folder = Path.GetTempPath();
            string strat_name = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "strat_name");
            xlh.WriteRange(null,"cutoff", cutoff);
            List<string> ranges = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "strat_buckets").Split(',').ToList();
            ETA eta = new ETA(ranges.Count, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
            DataTable tape = null;
            List<string> strat_files = new List<string>();
            var f = new Fields(SaludaToolkit.DB, Database.FieldHelper.GetFieldTableInternal);
            f.PopulateFieldHelpers();
            foreach (string which in ranges)
            {
                tape = GenerateStratTable(SaludaToolkit.DB, tape_id, account_id,which,only_active);
                xlh.WriteRange(null, "STRAT_CURRENT", which);
                ProcessStratInternal("strat", tape);
                eta.IncrementAndReport();
                
                string long_name = f[which].long_name;
                xlh.WriteRange(null, "strat_long_name", long_name);
                string final_calendar_name = CommonTKLib.PDF.PDFAndSpawnInternal(xlh, "Strats", "Strats - " + strat_name + " - " + long_name.Replace("/", "-"), true, save_folder);
                strat_files.Add(final_calendar_name);
            }

            if (strat_files.Count > 0)
            {
                string combined_file = Path.Combine(Path.GetTempPath(), $"{strat_name} - STRATS - {cutoff:M.d.yyyy}.pdf");
                UtilsLib.PDF.MergePDFs(combined_file, strat_files);
                strat_files.ForEach(n => File.Delete(n));
            }

            ProcessHelper.SpawnDirectory(save_folder, false);
            xlh.ToggleSheetRowGrouping(null, false);
        }
        public static void ProcessStratInternal(string range, DataTable strat)
        {
            var xlh = SaludaToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, range);
            xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.MANUAL);
            xlh.SelectSheetFromRange(null, range);
            
            xlt.ClearColumnsExcept("IGNORE");
            xlt.UnhideAllTable();
            string which = range.Replace("bucket_", "");

            xlh.WriteStatusBar("Processing: " + which);
            xlt.DumpData(strat, false, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
            xlt.TightenUpTable("#");
            xlh.ToggleSheetRowGrouping("Strats", false);
            xlh.ToggleCalcs(XLHelper.XLCalcMode.AUTOMATIC);
            
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void SaveandSpawnStrats()
        {
            SaveandSpawnStratsInternal(false, null, "Strats");
        }
        public static void SaveandSpawnStratsInternal(bool queit, string base_folder, string sheet)
        {
            XLHelper xlh = SaludaToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            string name = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "strat_name");

            CommonTKLib.PDF.PDFAndSpawnInternal(xlh,sheet, name, queit, base_folder);
        }
    }
}


--- FILE: Saluda\Saluda Toolkit\Saluda Toolkit\Sheets\TapeUpdater.cs ---
namespace Saluda_Toolkit
{
    public static class TapeUpdater
    {
        [ExcelFunction]
        public static void CorrectTape()
        {
            var xlh = SaludaToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            int? tape_id = xlh.GetRangeDefaultIfNoExistNullable<int>("tape_id");
            int account_id = xlh.GetRange<int>(null, "account_id");
            DateTime cutoff_date = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>(null, "cutoff_date");
            DateTime asOf = xlh.GetRange<DateTime>(null, "asOf");
            string note = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "note");
            bool new_tape = xlh.GetRange<bool>(null, "new_tape");
            if (null == tape_id && !new_tape)
            {
                MessageBox.Show("No Tape Selected");
                return;
                
            }
            XLTable xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "piston_update");
            var rows = xlt.AllRows("loan_id");
            ETA eta = new ETA(rows.Count, xlh.WriteStatusBar);

            System.Data.DataTable raw = xlh.GetRangeDataTable(null, "piston_update");
            raw.TrimBlankColumns();
            raw.TrimBlankRows();
            foreach (var row in rows)
            {
                string loan_id = row["loan_id"].ToString().Trim();

                long? asset_id = PistonLib.Assets.GetAssetId(SaludaToolkit.DB, loan_id, null, null, false);
                if(null == asset_id)
                {
                    MessageBox.Show($"Failed to match: {loan_id}");
                    return;
                }
                if (!new_tape)
                {
                    foreach (var field in xlt._header_indexes)
                    {
                        if (field.Key.ToUpper() != "LOAN_ID")
                        {
                            PistonLib.TapeDetail.UpdateField(SaludaToolkit.DB, tape_id.Value, asset_id.Value, field.Key, row[field.Key]);
                        }
                    }
                    eta.IncrementAndReport();
                }

            }

            var results = PistonLib.Tapes.TransformTape(SaludaToolkit.DB, null, raw, true, true, true);
            

            var result = PistonLib.Tapes.CreateAndLoadTape(SaludaToolkit.DB, true, 6, account_id, cutoff_date, asOf, note, null, xlh.GetLocalFilename(null), eta, results, false);
            
            PistonLib.Tapes.ProcessTapes(SaludaToolkit.DB,result.tape_id, null);
            if (result.error != null)
                MessageBox.Show(result.error,"Tape *SHOULD* still be loaded");
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "tape_id", result.tape_id);
            MessageBox.Show("DONE!");
        }

    }
}

--- FILE: Saluda\Saluda Toolkit\Saluda Toolkit\Tapes.cs ---
namespace Saluda_Toolkit
{
    public static class Tapes
    {
        [ExcelFunction(Name = "Tape.CheckFieldMap")]
        public static string CheckMapping(int tapemap_id, string field)
        {
            string s = PistonLib.Tapes.GetMappedColumn(SaludaToolkit.DB, tapemap_id, field);
            if (null == s)
                s = "<NO MATCH>";
            return s;
        }
        [ExcelFunction(Name = "Tape.GetFieldConstraint")]
        public static string GetTapeConstraint(int tapemap_id, string field)
        {
            string db_field = CheckMapping(tapemap_id, field);
            if (db_field.Contains("NO MATCH"))
                return db_field;
            string constraint = PistonLib.Tapes.GetConstraintString(SaludaToolkit.DB, db_field);
            if (null == constraint)
                return "";
            return constraint;
        }
    }
}

--- FILE: Saluda\Saluda Toolkit\Saluda Toolkit\TradeTemplate.cs ---
namespace Saluda_Toolkit
{
    public static class TradeTemplate
    {
        [ExcelFunction]

        public static void ExecuteTradesFlip()
        {
            var xlh = SaludaToolkit.GlobalExcel;
             var trade_id = ExecuteTrades();
            string buy_sell = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "buy_sell",false);
            string account_id = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "account_name");
            string counterparty_id = xlh.GetRange<string>(null, "counterparty_name");
            
            if (buy_sell.ToUpper() == "B")
                xlh.WriteRange(null, "buy_sell", "S");
            else
                xlh.WriteRange(null, "buy_sell", "B");
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "counterparty_name", account_id);
            xlh.WriteRange(null, "account_name", counterparty_id);
            ExecuteTrades();
            MessageBox.Show($"Trade ID: {trade_id}", "DONE!");
        }
        public static int ExecuteTrades()
        {
            var xlh = SaludaToolkit.GlobalExcel;
            var xlt = new XLTable(xlh, "piston_trades");
            var trades = xlt.AllRows("asset_id");
            int trade_id = PistonLib.Trades.GetNextTradeID(SaludaToolkit.DB);
            ETA eta = new ETA(trades.Count, xlh.WriteStatusBar);
            foreach(var row in trades)
            {
                int asset_id = row["asset_id"].AsInt().Value;
                double oface = row["oface"].AsDouble().Value;
                double cface = row["cface"].AsDouble().Value;
                double price = row["price"].AsDouble().Value;
                double accrued_interest = row["accrued_interest"].AsDouble().Value;
                string buy_sell = row["buy_sell"];
                int account_id = row["account_id"].AsInt().Value;
                int counterparty_id = row["counterparty_id"].AsInt().Value;
                DateTime trade_date = row["trade_date"].AsDate().Value;
                DateTime settle_date = row["settle_date"].AsDate().Value;
                
                string note = row["note"];
                PistonLib.Trades.InsertTradeDetail(SaludaToolkit.DB, trade_id, asset_id, oface, cface, price, accrued_interest, trade_date, settle_date, buy_sell, account_id, counterparty_id, null, note,"TT");
                eta.IncrementAndReport();
            }
            return trade_id;
        }
    }
}


--- FILE: Saluda\Saluda Toolkit\Saluda Toolkit\Utils.cs ---
namespace Saluda_Toolkit
{
    public static class Utils
    {
        [ExcelFunction]
        public static double Extrapolate(double val, double[] vals, double[] nums)
        {
            return CommonTKLib.Utils.Extrapolate(val, vals, nums);
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object SplitStr(string full_str, string delimiter, int zero_based_index)
        {
            string[] splits = full_str.Split(delimiter);
            if (splits.Length <= zero_based_index)
                return ExcelError.ExcelErrorNA;
            return splits[zero_based_index].Trim();
        }

        [ExcelFunction]
        public static object CalcAge(DateTime origination, DateTime cutoff)
        {
            return UtilsLib.Dates.CalcAge(cutoff, origination);
        }

    }
}


--- FILE: DXHelper\Chart.cs ---
namespace DXHelper
{
    public static class Chart
    {

        public static string AutoPickFormat(DataTable dt,string column)
        {
            if (dt.Columns[column].DataType == typeof(double) || dt.Columns[column].DataType == typeof(int))
            {
                try
                {
                    if (dt.Rows.Count == 0 || dt.Select($"[{column}] is null").Length != 0)
                        return null;
                    double min = Convert.ToDouble(dt.Compute($"min([{column}])", string.Empty));
                    double max = Convert.ToDouble(dt.Compute($"max([{column}])", string.Empty));
                    if (min > 1500)
                        return "{VP:#,##0}";
                } catch(Exception ex)
                {
                }
            }
            return null;
        }
        public static void ProcessChart(this ChartControl cc, DataTable source,string header,string small_text,string data_member,string argument_data_member,string value_members,bool show_legend,int? min_y_value, int? max_y_value)
        {

            

            if (cc.Titles.Count == 0)
            {
                ChartTitle ct = new ChartTitle();
                ct.Text = header;
                cc.Titles.Add(ct);
            }
            cc.SmallChartText.Text = small_text;
            cc.DataSource = source;
            cc.SeriesDataMember = data_member;
            cc.SeriesTemplate.ArgumentDataMember = argument_data_member;
            

            
            cc.SeriesTemplate.ValueDataMembers.AddRange(new string[] { value_members });
            
            cc.SeriesTemplate.View = new LineSeriesView();

            
            ((LineSeriesView)cc.SeriesTemplate.View).MarkerVisibility = DevExpress.Utils.DefaultBoolean.True;

            ((LineSeriesView)cc.SeriesTemplate.View).FirstPoint.Label.LineVisibility = DevExpress.Utils.DefaultBoolean.True;
            ((LineSeriesView)cc.SeriesTemplate.View).LastPoint.Label.LineVisibility = DevExpress.Utils.DefaultBoolean.True;


            ((XYDiagram)cc.Diagram).AxisY.Visibility = DevExpress.Utils.DefaultBoolean.True;
            cc.Legend.Visibility = show_legend ? DevExpress.Utils.DefaultBoolean.True :DevExpress.Utils.DefaultBoolean.False;

            string fmt = AutoPickFormat(source, value_members);
            if (null != fmt)
            {
                XYDiagram diagram = cc.Diagram as XYDiagram;
                diagram.AxisY.Label.TextPattern = fmt;
                
                
            }

            if (null != min_y_value || null != max_y_value)
            {
                XYDiagram diagram = cc.Diagram as XYDiagram;
                
                
                diagram.AxisY.VisualRange.Auto = false;

                diagram.AxisY.WholeRange.SetMinMaxValues(min_y_value.Value, max_y_value.Value);
                
            }

            cc.Animate();

        }
    }
}


--- FILE: DXHelper\CheckedListBoxControl.cs ---
namespace DXHelper
{
    public static class LabelControlHelper
    {


        public static void SetTextSafe(this LabelControl b, string text)
        {
            if (b.InvokeRequired)
            {
                b.Invoke(new MethodInvoker(() => { b.SetTextSafe(text); } ));
            }
            else
            {
                b.Text = text;
            }
        }

    }
}


--- FILE: DXHelper\ColumnView.cs ---
namespace DXHelper
{
    public static class ColumnViewHelpers
    {
        public static List<T> GetFilteredData<T>(this ColumnView view, string column_name)
        {
            List<T> resp = new List<T>();
            int currentRowHandle = view.GetVisibleRowHandle(0);
            while (currentRowHandle != DevExpress.XtraGrid.GridControl.InvalidRowHandle)
            {

                
                object o = view.GetRowCellValue(currentRowHandle, column_name);
                resp.Add((T)System.Convert.ChangeType(o, typeof(T)));
                currentRowHandle = view.GetNextVisibleRow(currentRowHandle);
            }
            return resp;
        }
    }
}

--- FILE: DXHelper\CustomFilterControl.cs ---
namespace DXHelper
{
    [ToolboxItem(true)]
    public class CustomFilterControl : FilterControl
    {
        protected override void OnKeyDown(KeyEventArgs e)
        {
            if (e.KeyCode == Keys.Tab)
                e = new KeyEventArgs(Keys.Right | Keys.Left);
            base.OnKeyDown(e);
        }

        protected override bool IsInputKey(Keys keyData)
        {
            if (keyData == Keys.Tab)
                return true;
            return base.IsInputKey(keyData);
        }
    }
}


--- FILE: DXHelper\CustomPopups.cs ---
namespace DXHelper
{
    public class CustomPopups
    {

        private static Dictionary<GridHelper, CustomPopups> _list = new Dictionary<GridHelper, CustomPopups>();
        public static CustomPopups GetInstance(GridHelper gh)
        {
            if (!_list.ContainsKey(gh))
            {
                _list.Add(gh, new CustomPopups(gh,gh._server));
                
                
            }

            return _list[gh];
        }

        private IWriter _writer;
        public Control _parent_form;
        public CustomPopups(GridHelper gh,string server)
        {
            this.Init(gh,server);
        }
        public virtual void Init(GridHelper gh,string server)
        {
            _gc = gh;
            this.server = server;
        }
        public virtual void RegisterPopupsInternal(CommonInterfaces.Delegates.NewAssetSelected nas, IWriter writer = null, System.Windows.Forms.Control c = null)
        {
            
            _nas = nas;
            _view = _gc._view;
            _writer = writer;
            _parent_form = c;

        }

        
        public void RegisterCustomPopups(CommonInterfaces.Delegates.NewAssetSelected nas, IWriter writer = null, System.Windows.Forms.Control c = null, PopupMenuShowingEventHandler pops = null)
        {
            RegisterPopupsInternal(nas,writer);
            _gc.InsertPopups(_gc._view, pops);
            _gc.AppendStandardPopupMenus();
            _parent_form = c;
        }


        public delegate void EnableEditing();
        private EnableEditing _ee;
        private string _csv_editable_columns;
        public void RegisterEditGridPopup(EnableEditing ee, string csv_editable_columns = null)
        {
            if (null == ee && !String.IsNullOrEmpty(csv_editable_columns))
                _ee = EditGridPopupGeneral;
            else
                _ee = ee;
            _gc.InsertPopups(_gc._view, EditGridPopup);
            _gc.AppendStandardPopupMenus();
            _csv_editable_columns = csv_editable_columns;

        }

        private void EditGridPopupGeneral()
        {
            _gc.SetEditable(_csv_editable_columns, null);
            _gc.ToggleEmbeddedNavigator(true);
        }

        public CommonInterfaces.Delegates.NewAssetSelected _nas;
        public string server 
        { 
            get; 
            set; 
        }
        public GridHelper _gc;
        public GridView _view;

        public void EditGridPopup(object sender, PopupMenuShowingEventArgs e)
        {

            GridView view = sender as GridView;
            DevExpress.XtraGrid.Menu.GridViewMenu menu = e.Menu as GridViewMenu;
            if (null == menu)
            {
                return;
            }
            DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem note = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("Edit Grid", _editGridAction, GridHelper.GetImageCache("notes"));
            menu.Items.Add(note);

        }

        public void EnableGridEditing()
        {
            _gc.TogglePreferredEditor(true);
            if (null != _csv_editable_columns)
                _gc.SetEditable(_csv_editable_columns, CommonInterfaces.Constants.BADGER.EDIT_COLOR);

            if (null != _ee)
                _ee();
        }
        public void _editGridAction(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            EnableGridEditing();
        }


        public void HackDebugWriteline(string write)
        {
            System.Diagnostics.Debug.WriteLine(write);
        }

    }
}

        }

        public void Sort(string csv_cort, DevExpress.Data.ColumnSortOrder co)
        {

            {
                viewDetail.SortInfo.Add(new DevExpress.XtraGrid.Columns.GridColumnSortInfo(viewDetail.Columns[s], co));
            }
            viewDetail.EndSort();
            
        }

        {

using static DXHelper.LazyTable;

namespace DXHelper.Forms
{
    public partial class LazyTableEditor : DevExpress.XtraEditors.XtraForm
    {
        public LazyTableEditor()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        private string server;
        GridHelper _main;
        string cols_2_update;
        string csv_cols_2_show;
        public void Init(string server,DataTable starting_table,string csv_cols_2_show,string table_to_update,string table_key_column,string csv_cols_2_update,bool check_if_exists, Dictionary<string, string> key_remap,List<string> columns_to_return_on_insert)
        {
            this.server = server;
            _main = new GridHelper(mainGrid, server, true, null);
            this.cols_2_update = csv_cols_2_update;
            this.csv_cols_2_show = csv_cols_2_show;
            CustomPopups.GetInstance(_main).RegisterEditGridPopup(SetGenericEditable);
            _main.SetupGenericLazyTable(table_to_update, table_key_column, check_if_exists, key_remap, null, null, columns_to_return_on_insert);
            _main.SetGrid(starting_table,csv_cols_2_show);
            SetGenericEditable();
            
        }

        public void SetupDropDown(DataTable tbl,string which_column_to_apply_on,string display_column,string value_column)
        {
            _main.SetUpDropdown(tbl, which_column_to_apply_on, display_column, value_column);
        }


        public void ShowFindPanel()
        {
            _main.ShowFindPanel();
        }
        public void SetGenericEditable()
        {
            if (null == cols_2_update)
                cols_2_update = _main._DataTable.Columns.ToCSVCols();
            _main.SetEditable(cols_2_update.Split(','), null, true);
            _main.ToggleEmbeddedNavigator(true);
        }

        public void EnableHorizontalScroll()
        {
            mainView.OptionsView.ColumnAutoWidth = false;
            mainView.HorzScrollVisibility = DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Base.ScrollVisibility.Always;
        }
        public void SetDimentions(int height,int width)
        {
            this.Width = width;
            this.Height = height;
        }
        private void btnDone_Click_1(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            this.Close();
        }
    }
}

using static DXHelper.GridHelper;

namespace DXHelper.Forms
{
    public partial class QuickView : DevExpress.XtraBars.ToolbarForm.ToolbarForm
    {
        public QuickView()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        private string _server;
        public void Init(string server, GridHelper.GridSetSearchGrid action)
        {
            _server = server;
            _grid = new GridHelper(gridDetail, _server, true,action);
        }

        


        public void InitAndShowLazy(string server,DataTable table,string title_text, GridSetSearchGrid dca )
        {
            Init(server, dca);
            this.Text = title_text;
            this.Populate(table, null);
            this.ToggleMinimizeButton(true);

            this.ExpandAllGroupBy();
            this.ToggleAutoFilterRow(true);

            this.SetSize(2200, 650);

            this.ToggleAutoFilterRow(true);

            this.SetFormBorderStyle(FormBorderStyle.Sizable);
            this.ToggleMinimizeButton(true);
            
            this.ToggleSearchPanel(true);
            this.BestFit();
            this.Show();
        }




        private GridHelper _grid;
        private string _format;
        public void Populate(DataTable tbl,string format)
        {
            _grid.SetGrid(tbl, format);
            
            _format = format;
        }

        public void ToggleSearchPanel(bool visible)
        {
            _grid.ToggleSearchPanel(visible);
        }
        public GridHelper Grid { get { return _grid; } }

        
        
        
        

        public void ToggleFooter(bool show)
        {
            _grid.ShowFooter(show);
        }

        Query _refresh_query;
        public void SetRefreshQuery(Query refresh_query)
        {
            _refresh_query = refresh_query;
            btnRefresh.Enabled = true;
        }

        public void AddSumsFooters(string csv)
        {
            _grid.ShowSums(csv);
        }

        public void Populate(DataTable tbl,string format, string select_row_column_name, object matching, bool clear_filter, string filter, bool repopulate_columns)
        {
            _grid.SetGrid(tbl, format, select_row_column_name, matching, clear_filter, filter, repopulate_columns);

            _format = format;
        }

        private void RefreshQuery()
        {
            if (null != _refresh_query)
            {
                var table = _refresh_query.ExecuteTable();
                _grid.SetGrid(table, _format);
            }
        }
            private void frmQuickView_KeyUp(object sender, KeyEventArgs e)
        {
            if (e.KeyCode == Keys.F5 && null != _refresh_query)
            {
                RefreshQuery();
            }
        }
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        

        public void SetFindFilterText(string filter)
        {
            DevExpress.XtraGrid.Controls.FindControl find = gridDetail.Controls.Find("FindControlCore", true)[0] as DevExpress.XtraGrid.Controls.FindControl;
            find.SetFilterText(filter);
        }
        public void SetFilter(string filter)
        {
            _grid.SetActiveFilterSafe(filter);
        }





        public void ToggleMinimizeButton(bool visible)
        {
            this.MinimizeBox = visible;
        }

        public void EnableInlineEditor()
        {
            viewDetail.OptionsBehavior.EditingMode = DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Grid.GridEditingMode.EditFormInplace;
        }
        public void Sort(string csv_cort, DevExpress.Data.ColumnSortOrder co)
        {
            
            viewDetail.BeginSort();
            foreach (string s in csv_cort.Split(','))
            {
                viewDetail.SortInfo.Add(new DevExpress.XtraGrid.Columns.GridColumnSortInfo(viewDetail.Columns[s], co));
            }
            viewDetail.EndSort();
            
        }

        public void SetColumnWidth(string column, int width)

--- FILE: DXHelper\Grid.cs ---
namespace DXHelper
{
    public static class Grid
    {

        public static GridView MainView(this GridControl gc)
        {
            return gc.MainView as GridView;
        }

        public static void FormatGridViewNicely(this GridView gv)
        {
            GView.CleanColumns(gv, null);
        }

        public static void SetupStandardFeatures(this GridControl gc)
        {
            gc.ProcessGridKey += Gc_ProcessGridKey;
        }


        private static void Gc_ProcessGridKey(object sender, System.Windows.Forms.KeyEventArgs e)
        {
            

            

            if (e.KeyCode == System.Windows.Forms.Keys.V && e.Modifiers == System.Windows.Forms.Keys.Control)
            {
                GridControl gc = sender as GridControl;
                gc.MainView().HandleCopyPaste(false, true);
            }
            e.Handled = true;

        }

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        


        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        

        
        


        public static void SetFormat(this GridControl gc, string column, string format)
        {
            gc.MainView().SetFormat(column, format);
        }
        public static void SetWidth(this GridControl gc, string column, int width)
        {
            gc.MainView().SetWidth(column, width);
        }

        public static void HideColumn(this GridControl gc, string column)
        {
            SetVisibleSafe(gc, new string[] { column }, false);
        }

        public static void SetColumnVisibleUnsafe(this GridControl gc, IEnumerable<string> columns, bool visible)
        {
            foreach (DevExpress.XtraGrid.Columns.GridColumn c in ((GridView)gc.MainView).Columns)
            {
                if (columns.Contains(c.FieldName))
                {
                    c.Visible = visible;
                }
            }
        }

        public static void SetVisibleSafe(this GridControl gc, IEnumerable<string> columns, bool visible)
        {
            if (gc.InvokeRequired)
            {
                gc.Invoke(new MethodInvoker(() => { gc.SetVisibleSafe(columns, visible); }));
            }
            else
            {
                gc.SetColumnVisibleUnsafe(columns, visible);
            }
        }



        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        public static void SetNormal(this GridControl gc)
        {
            SetReadOnlyNew(gc);

        }
        public static void SetReadOnlyNew(this GridControl gc)
        {
            ((GridView)gc.MainView).OptionsBehavior.Editable = false;
            ((GridView)gc.MainView).OptionsBehavior.ReadOnly = true;
        }

    }
}

namespace DXHelper
{
    public static class GridColumnnHelper
    {
        public static void SetColumnEditSafe(this GridColumn col, Control c, RepositoryItem ri)
        {

           if (c.InvokeRequired)
            {
                c.Invoke(new MethodInvoker(() => { SetColumnEditSafe(col, c, ri); }));
            }
            else
            {
                col.ColumnEdit = ri;
            }
        }




        public static void SortModeSafe(this GridColumn col, Control c, DevExpress.XtraGrid.ColumnSortMode csm)
        {

            if (c.InvokeRequired)
            {
                c.Invoke(new MethodInvoker(() => { SortModeSafe(col, c, csm); }));
            }
            else
            {
                col.SortMode = csm;
            }
        }

    }
}


--- FILE: DXHelper\GridColumnCollection.cs ---
namespace DXHelper
{
    public static class GridColumnCollectionHelper
    {
        public static bool ContainsColumn(this GridColumnCollection collection,string field)
        {
            return null != collection.ColumnByFieldName(field);
        }
        public static int IndexOfColumnContaing(this GridColumnCollection collection, string txt_to_match)
        {
            foreach (GridColumn column in collection)
            {
                if (column.FieldName.IndexOf(txt_to_match) != -1)
                    return column.FieldName.IndexOf(txt_to_match);
            }
            return -1;
        }

    }
}

namespace DXHelper

    [ToolboxItem(true)]
    public class GridControlCustom : GridControl

        }
        protected override void RegisterAvailableViewsCore(InfoCollection collection)
        {
            base.RegisterAvailableViewsCore(collection);
            collection.Add(new GridViewInfoRegistratorCustom());
        }
    }

    class GridHandlerCustom : GridHandler
    {
        public GridHandlerCustom(GridView gridView) : base(gridView) { }

    }

    class GridViewInfoRegistratorCustom : GridInfoRegistrator
    {
        public override string ViewName { get { return "MyCustomGridView"; } }
        public override BaseView CreateView(GridControl grid) { return new GridViewCustom(grid as GridControl); }
        public override BaseViewInfo CreateViewInfo(BaseView view) { return new GridViewInfoCustom(view as GridViewCustom); }
        public override BaseViewHandler CreateHandler(BaseView view) { return new GridHandlerCustom(view as GridViewCustom); }
    }

            {
                SetUpView(_view);

                _gc.MouseWheel += _gc_MouseWheel;
                
                _view.OptionsView.RowAutoHeight = true;
                

                _view.OptionsSelection.EnableAppearanceFocusedRow = false;
                _view.OptionsSelection.EnableAppearanceFocusedCell = false;
                _view.OptionsSelection.EnableAppearanceHideSelection = true;


                _view.OptionsView.ColumnAutoWidth = true;


                _view.CustomDrawGroupRow += _view_CustomDrawGroupRow;
                _view.CustomDrawCell += _view_CustomDrawCell;
                _view.OptionsView.ShowGroupedColumns = false;
                _view.OptionsDetail.SmartDetailExpandButtonMode = DetailExpandButtonMode.CheckAllDetails;
                _view.MouseDown += _view_MouseDown;
                _view.CustomColumnDisplayText += _view_CustomColumnDisplayText;

                _view.OptionsSelection.EnableAppearanceHotTrackedRow = DefaultBoolean.True;

                _view.CustomRowCellEdit += _view_CustomRowCellEdit;

        public void AddRowCountsToGroup()
        {
            _view.CustomColumnDisplayText += ViewOffenders_CustomColumnDisplayText;
        }
        private void ViewOffenders_CustomColumnDisplayText(object sender, DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Base.CustomColumnDisplayTextEventArgs e)
        {
            if (e.GroupRowHandle != GridControl.InvalidRowHandle)
            {
                GridView view = sender as GridView;
                e.DisplayText += string.Format("  ({0:#,000})", view.GetFullChildRowsCount(e.GroupRowHandle));
            }
        }
        private void _view_CustomRowCellEdit(object sender, CustomRowCellEditEventArgs e)
        {
            if (e.Column.FieldName.IndexOf("url") != -1)
            {
                if ((e.Column.FieldName.Substring(0, 3) == "url") && e.RowHandle >= 0)
                {
                    if (e.Column.FieldName.Length == 3)
                    {
                        object caption = _view.GetRowCellValue(e.RowHandle, "url_caption");
                        if (null != caption && DBNull.Value != caption)
                        {
                            var item = new DevExpress.XtraEditors.Repository.RepositoryItemHyperLinkEdit();
                            item.Caption = caption.ToString();
                            e.RepositoryItem = item;
                        }
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        string url_idx = e.Column.FieldName.Substring(e.Column.FieldName.Length - 1);
                        object caption = _view.GetRowCellValue(e.RowHandle, "url_caption_" + url_idx);
                        if (null != caption && DBNull.Value != caption)
                        {
                            var item = new DevExpress.XtraEditors.Repository.RepositoryItemHyperLinkEdit();
                            item.Caption = caption.ToString();
                            e.RepositoryItem = item;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            if (e.Column.FieldName.IndexOf("_link") != -1)
            {
                var item = new DevExpress.XtraEditors.Repository.RepositoryItemHyperLinkEdit();
                item.Caption = "Link";
                e.RepositoryItem = item;
                
                

            }
        }

        private void _view_FocusedRowChanged(object sender, FocusedRowChangedEventArgs e)
        {
            
            
            

            
            
        }

        public List<int> selected_row_order = new List<int>();
        private void _view_SelectionChanged(object sender, DevExpress.Data.SelectionChangedEventArgs e)
        {
            int[] selected_rows = _view.GetSelectedRows();
            if (selected_rows.Count() == 1 || selected_rows.Count() == 0)
                selected_row_order.Clear();

            if (selected_rows.Count() != 0)
            {
                if (selected_rows.Count() == 1)
                {
                    GridView v = sender as GridView;
                    int row_handle = selected_rows[0];
                    selected_row_order.Add(row_handle);
                }
                else if (e.ControllerRow < 0)
                    selected_row_order.AddRange(selected_rows);
                else
                    selected_row_order.Add(e.ControllerRow);
            }
        }

        public List<T> GetUniqueListInternal<T>(string column, bool unique_only, bool only_selected, bool formatted, bool ignore_blank, bool only_visible, int[] iteration_order)
        {
            return _view.GetUniqueListInternal<T>(column, unique_only, only_selected, formatted, ignore_blank, only_visible, iteration_order);
        }

        private void _view_CustomColumnDisplayText(object sender, CustomColumnDisplayTextEventArgs e)
        {
            ColumnView view = sender as ColumnView;
            if (e.Column.FieldName == "asof" && e.ListSourceRowIndex != DevExpress.XtraGrid.GridControl.InvalidRowHandle && e.Column.ColumnType == typeof(DateTime) && DBNull.Value != e.Value)
            {
                
                DateTime date = Convert.ToDateTime(e.Value);
                if (date.Date == DateTime.Today && date.Hour != 0)
                {
                    e.DisplayText = String.Format("{0:M/d/yy h:mm tt}", e.Value);
                }
                
                
                
                
                
            }
        }

            GridViewInfoCustom gvic = (GridViewInfoCustom)gvc.GetViewInfo();
            
            gvic.SetZoom(0);

        }
        private void _view_MouseDown(object sender, MouseEventArgs e)
        {
            GridView v = sender as GridView;
            var hitInfo = v.CalcHitInfo(e.Location);
            if (hitInfo.InColumn && Control.ModifierKeys == System.Windows.Forms.Keys.Control)
            {
                string existing_clipboard = System.Windows.Forms.Clipboard.GetText();
                int length = existing_clipboard.Split(Environment.NewLine).Length;

                
                
                
                List<string> vals = v.GetUniqueListInternal<string>(hitInfo.Column.FieldName, false, false, true, false, false, null);
                vals.Insert(0, hitInfo.Column.Caption);
                string s = String.Join(Environment.NewLine, vals.ToArray());

                if (s.Split(Environment.NewLine).Length == length && length > 0)
                {
                    string last_col = existing_clipboard.Split(Environment.NewLine)[0];
                    if (existing_clipboard.Contains('\t'))
                    {
                        last_col = last_col.Split('\t')[last_col.Split('\t').Length - 1];
                    }
                    string this_col = hitInfo.Column.Caption;
                    if (this_col == last_col)
                    {
                        Clipboard.Clear();
                        return;
                    }
                    List<string> newCopy = new List<string>();

                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    for (int i = 0; i != vals.Count; i++)
                    {
                        string format = String.Format("{0}\t{1}", existing_clipboard.Split(Environment.NewLine)[i], vals[i]);
                        newCopy.Add(format);
                    }


                    s = String.Join(Environment.NewLine, newCopy.ToArray());
                }
                else
                {
                    int max_length = 0;
                    for (int i = 0; i != vals.Count; i++)
                    {
                        if (vals[i].Length > max_length)
                            max_length = vals[i].Length;
                    }
                    for (int i = 0; i != vals.Count; i++)
                    {
                        vals[i] = vals[i].PadRight(max_length, ' ');
                    }
                    s = String.Join(Environment.NewLine, vals.ToArray());
                }

                System.Windows.Forms.Clipboard.SetText(s);
            }

        }


        public Nullable<int> GetProductIdFromGrid(string product_id_column, double threshold, bool visible_only)
        {
            
            
            
            return GetMajorityItem<int>(product_id_column, threshold, false, visible_only);
        }

        
        
        
        
        

        public void PriorityColumns(IEnumerable<string> fields)
        {
            ResetWidths(fields, false);
        }

        public void ResetWidths(IEnumerable<string> fields, bool use_best_fit)
        {
            foreach (string f in fields)
            {
                GridColumn gc = _view.Columns[f];
                if (null != gc && gc.Visible)
                {
                    if (use_best_fit)
                        gc.Width = _view.CalcColumnBestWidth(gc);
                    else
                    {
                        Fields all_fields = Fields.GetInstance(_server,Database.FieldHelper.GetFieldTableInternal);
                        if (all_fields.ContainsField(f))
                        {
                            var fld = all_fields[f];
                            if (null != fld.force_width)
                                gc.Width = fld.force_width.Value;
                        }


                    }
                }
            }
        }

        private string _cell_format_apply_to = null;
        private Dictionary<string, string> cell_formats = new Dictionary<string, string>();
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        

        public void SetCellFormatApplyTo(string cell_color_field, string field_to_apply_to)
        {
            if (null == cell_formats)
                cell_formats = new Dictionary<string, string>();

            if (cell_formats.ContainsKey(cell_color_field))
                cell_formats[cell_color_field] = field_to_apply_to;
            else
                cell_formats.Add(cell_color_field, field_to_apply_to);
        }
        private void _view_CustomDrawCell(object sender, RowCellCustomDrawEventArgs e)
        {

            if (null == cell_formats)
                return;
            foreach (KeyValuePair<string, string> kvp in cell_formats)
            {
                if (null != _view.Columns[kvp.Key] && e.Column.FieldName == kvp.Value)
                {
                    object col = _view.GetRowCellValue(e.RowHandle, kvp.Key);
                    if (null != col)
                    {
                        string color = col.ToString();
                        System.Drawing.Color c = System.Drawing.Color.FromName(color);
                        e.Appearance.ForeColor = c;
                    }
                }
            }
          
        }

        public void TwistGrid(string table)
        {
            DataSet set = this._DataSet;
            if (null == set)
                return;
            if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(this.SelectedTableName))
            {
                if (table == this.SelectedTableName)
                {
                    return;
                }
            }
            if (set.Tables.Contains(table))
            {

                string format = null;

                DataTable tbl = set.Tables[table];
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                int hash = set.Tables[table].GetHashCode();
                format = GetLoadedFormats(hash);
                Nullable<int> product_id = null;
                if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(format))
                {
                    if (null != tbl.Columns["product_id"])
                    {
                        if (tbl.Columns.Contains("cface"))
                            product_id = tbl.GetMaxBasedOnThreshold<int>("product_id", "cface", .70);
                        
                        
                    }
                    

                    
                }

                
                this.SetGrid(tbl, format, null, null, true, null, true);
                
                if (null != _view.Columns["ticker"])
                {
                    _view.Columns["ticker"].Visible = true;
                }

                if (null != _view.Columns["asof"])
                {
                    if (_view.SortInfo.Count == 0)
                    {
                        _view.Columns["asof"].Visible = true;
                        if (_view.Columns["asof"].ColumnType == typeof(DateTime))
                            _view.Columns["asof"].SortOrder = DevExpress.Data.ColumnSortOrder.Descending;
                        else
                            _view.Columns["asof"].SortOrder = DevExpress.Data.ColumnSortOrder.Ascending;
                        _view.FocusedRowHandle = 0;
                    }

                }

                if (null != _view.Columns["note"])
                {
                    RepositoryItemMemoEdit color = new RepositoryItemMemoEdit();
                    color.WordWrap = true;
                    _view.Columns["note"].ColumnEdit = color;
                    _view.AutoFillColumn = _view.Columns["note"];
                }
            }
        }

        public string SelectedTableName { get; internal set; }
        public string CurrentColumnVisible { get; internal set; }

        public void SetVisibleColumns(string csv_columns_visible, bool do_begin_updates = false, bool mark_columns_read_only = false, bool repopoulate_columns = false)
        {
            Fields f = Fields.GetInstance(this._server, Database.FieldHelper.GetFieldTableInternal);
            GView.CleanColumns(_view, f, csv_columns_visible, do_begin_updates, mark_columns_read_only, repopoulate_columns);
            this.CurrentColumnVisible = csv_columns_visible;
        }

        public static void Donk()
        {
            System.Diagnostics.Debug.WriteLine("HERE");
        }
        public void SetGrid(object table, string csv_columns_visible, string select_row_column_name, object matching, bool clear_filter, string filter, bool repopulate_columns)
        {

            GridView _view = _gc.MainView();
            
            try
            {
                object ds = table;
                _view.BeginUpdate();
                _gc.BeginUpdate();


                if (null != filter)
                    _view.ActiveFilterString = filter;

                CriteriaOperator view_filter = _view.ActiveFilterCriteria;

                if (null != table)
                {
                    DataTable t = null;
                    if (table.GetType() == typeof(DataSet))
                    {
                        t = ((DataSet)table).Tables[0];
                        try
                        {
                            if (null != _gc.DataMember && _gc.DataMember != t.TableName)
                                _gc.DataMember = t.TableName;
                        }
                        catch (Exception n)
                        {

                        }
                        
                    }
                    if (table.GetType() == typeof(DataTable))
                    {
                        t = (DataTable)table;
                        if(t.Rows.Count > 1000)
                            _view.ShowLoadingPanel();
                    }
                    if (null != t)
                    {
                        SelectedTableName = t.TableName;
                    }
                }


                
                

                
                _view.SetHeaderFont(new System.Drawing.Font(_view.Appearance.HeaderPanel.Font, FontStyle.Bold));

                _gc.SetDataSourceSafe(table);
                
                _datasource = table;
                
                
                if (null != table && typeof(DataTable) == table.GetType() && ((DataTable)table).Rows.Count < 1000 && _view.IsFindPanelVisible)
                {
                    this.SetFindPanelDelaySafe(0);
                    
                }
                SetVisibleColumns(csv_columns_visible, false, false, repopulate_columns);


                
                


                if (null != table)
                {
                    if (table.GetType() == typeof(DataSet))
                    {
                        _DataSet = (DataSet)table;
                        _DataTable = _DataSet.Tables[0];
                    }
                    if (table.GetType() == typeof(DataTable))
                    {
                        _DataSet = ((DataTable)table).DataSet;
                        _DataTable = (DataTable)table;
                    }
                }

                if (null != _DataTable)
                {
                    int hash = _DataTable.GetHashCode();

                    if (!table_formats.ContainsKey(hash))
                        table_formats.Add(hash, null);
                    table_formats[hash] = csv_columns_visible;
                }
                this.csv_visible_cols = csv_columns_visible;


                if (!clear_filter)
                {
                    _view.ActiveFilterCriteria = view_filter;
                }

                if (_view.DataRowCount == 1)
                {
                    _view.UnselectRow(0);
                    _view.FocusedRowHandle = -1;
                    _view.ClearSelection();
                    _view.OptionsSelection.EnableAppearanceFocusedRow = false;
                }
                else
                {
                    _view.OptionsSelection.EnableAppearanceFocusedRow = true;
                }
                if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(select_row_column_name))
                    _view.SelectRowBasedOnID(select_row_column_name, matching);


            }
            catch (Exception n)
            {

                _view.EndUpdateSafe();
                _gc.EndUpdateSafe();
                throw n;
            }
            finally
            {
                
                
                
                
                _view.EndUpdateSafe();
                _gc.EndUpdateSafe();
            }
            _view.HideLoadingPanel();
            
            
            
        }


        private void _view_CustomDrawGroupRow(object sender, RowObjectCustomDrawEventArgs e)
        {
            e.Appearance.BackColor = System.Drawing.Color.Transparent;
        }
        public DataRelation AddRelationSafe(string relation_name, DataColumn parent, DataColumn child)
        {
            if (_gc.InvokeRequired)
            {
                return _gc.Invoke(new MethodInvoker(() => { AddRelationSafe(relation_name, parent, child); })) as DataRelation;
            }
            else
            {
                return _DataSet.Relations.Add(relation_name, parent, child);
            }
        }
        public void RefreshGridFormats(bool repopulate_columns)
        {
            SetVisibleColumns(this.csv_visible_cols, true, true, repopulate_columns);
        }
        public Nullable<T> GetMajorityItem<T>(string column, double pct, bool only_selected, bool only_visible) where T : struct
        {
            List<T> items = _view.GetActiveRowList<T>(column, only_selected);
            return GetMajorityItemInternal<T>(items, pct);
        }

        public Nullable<T> GetMajorityItemInternal<T>(List<T> items, double pct) where T : struct
        {
            Nullable<T> t = items.GetMajorityItem(pct);
            return t;
        }
