        private void _gc_MouseWheel(object sender, MouseEventArgs e)
        {

            bool ctrl = ((Control.ModifierKeys & System.Windows.Forms.Keys.Control) == System.Windows.Forms.Keys.Control);
            if (!ctrl)
                return;
            if (e.Delta > 0)
            {
                if (_view.Appearance.FilterPanel.FontSizeDelta < 20)
                {
                    _view.Appearance.FilterPanel.FontSizeDelta++;
                    _view.Appearance.Row.FontSizeDelta++;
                    _view.Appearance.HeaderPanel.FontSizeDelta++;
                }
            }
            else
            {
                if (_view.Appearance.FilterPanel.FontSizeDelta > -5)
                {
                    _view.Appearance.FilterPanel.FontSizeDelta--;
                    _view.Appearance.Row.FontSizeDelta--;
                    _view.Appearance.HeaderPanel.FontSizeDelta--;
                    
                }
            }
            _view.BestFitColumns();
        }

        public void SetUpView(GridView v, bool apply_default_popup = true)
        {


            v.ShowingEditor -= _view_ShowingEditor;
            v.HiddenEditor -= _view_HiddenEditor;
            v.KeyDown -= _view_KeyDown;
            v.ValidateRow -= _view_ValidateRow;
            v.DoubleClick -= _view_DoubleClick;
            v.PopupMenuShowing -= _view_DefaultPopups;
            v.CustomRowCellEdit -= _view_CustomRowCellEdit;

            v.ShowingEditor += _view_ShowingEditor;
            v.HiddenEditor += _view_HiddenEditor;
            v.KeyDown += _view_KeyDown;
            v.ValidateRow += _view_ValidateRow;
            v.DoubleClick += _view_DoubleClick;
            v.CustomRowCellEdit += _view_CustomRowCellEdit;

            if (apply_default_popup)
                v.PopupMenuShowing += _view_DefaultPopups;

            v.OptionsBehavior.ReadOnly = false;
            v.OptionsBehavior.Editable = true;

            
            v.RowCellStyle += V_RowCellStyle;
        }

        private void V_RowCellStyle(object sender, RowCellStyleEventArgs e)
        {
            if (e.RowHandle >= 0)
            {
                GridView view = sender as GridView;
                if (view.GetSelectedRows().Contains(e.RowHandle))
                    return;
                if (null != view && null != view.Columns["row_color"])
                {
                    object row_color = view.GetRowCellValue(e.RowHandle, "row_color");
                    if (null != row_color)
                    {
                        System.Drawing.Color c = System.Drawing.Color.FromName(row_color.ToString());
                        if (null != view.Columns["col_color"])
                        {
                            object col = view.GetRowCellValue(e.RowHandle, "col_color");
                            if (null != col && DBNull.Value != col)
                            {
                                if (e.Column.FieldName == col.ToString())
                                {
                                    e.Appearance.ForeColor = c;
                                }
                            }

                        }
                        else
                            e.Appearance.BackColor = c;

                        
                    }
                }
                
                
                    
                
                if (null != view && null != view.Columns["txt_color"])
                {
                    object txt_color = view.GetRowCellValue(e.RowHandle, "txt_color");
                    if (null != txt_color && DBNull.Value != txt_color)
                    {
                        string full_boi = txt_color.ToString();
                        string col = full_boi.Contains('|') ? full_boi.Split('|')[0] : full_boi;    
                        if(e.Column.FieldName.ToLower() == col.ToLower() || !full_boi.Contains('|'))
                        {
                            string color = full_boi.Contains('|') ?  txt_color.ToString().Split('|')[1] : full_boi;
                            System.Drawing.Color c = System.Drawing.Color.FromName(color);
                            e.Appearance.ForeColor = c;
                        }
                        
                    }
                }
            }

        }

        public void SetupRowAppearances(List<string> colors,string apply_to)
        {
            GridFormatRule formatRule = new GridFormatRule();
            
            FormatConditionRuleValue dateRule = new FormatConditionRuleValue();
            dateRule.Appearance.ForeColor = Color.Lime;
            dateRule.Value1 = "Lime";
            formatRule.Rule = dateRule;
            formatRule.Column = _view.Columns["cell_color"];
            formatRule.ColumnApplyTo = _view.Columns["taskstatus_id"];
            _view.FormatRules.Add(formatRule);
            
            
        }

        private void _view_DoubleClick(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            GridView view = (GridView)sender;
            Point pt = view.GridControl.PointToClient(Control.MousePosition);
            var handled = DoRowDoubleClick(view, pt);

            DXMouseEventArgs ee = e as DXMouseEventArgs;

            
            ee.Handled = handled.handled;

            if(null != DoubleClickAction && !handled.handled)
            {
                DoubleClickAction(view,handled.ghi);
                ee.Handled = true;
            }

        }

        private class DblClickHelper
        {
            public GridHitInfo ghi;
            public bool handled;
        }

        private DblClickHelper DoRowDoubleClick(GridView view, Point pt)
        {
            bool handled = false;
            GridHitInfo info = view.CalcHitInfo(pt);
            GridHitInfo info_new = view.CalcHitInfo(view.GridControl.PointToClient(System.Windows.Forms.Cursor.Position));
            view = info_new.View;
            DblClickHelper hi = new DblClickHelper { ghi = info_new, handled = handled };
            var s = info.Column;
            
            if(null != s && (s.FieldName.Substring(0, 3) == "url" || s.FieldName.IndexOf("_link") != -1))
            {
                object url = view.GetRowCellValue(info.RowHandle, s);
                if(null != url && DBNull.Value != url)
                {
                    url = Environment.ExpandEnvironmentVariables(url.ToString());
                    string last_char = url.ToString().Substring(url.ToString().Length - 1,1);
                    if(last_char == @"\")
                    {
                        if(!Directory.Exists(url.ToString()))
                        {
                            var response = XtraMessageBox.Show(url.ToString(), "Directory doesn't exist - Create it?", MessageBoxButtons.YesNoCancel);
                            if(response == DialogResult.Yes)
                            {
                                Directory.CreateDirectory(url.ToString());
                            }
                            else
                            {
                                return hi;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    bool is_download = true;
                    string url_or_file = url.ToString();
                    foreach(string file in url_or_file.Split(','))
                    {
                        UtilsLib.ProcessHelper.SpawnAsync(file.Trim());
                    }
                            
                    
                      
                    hi.handled = true;
                }
            }
            return hi;
        }

        public bool HideColumnIfSameValue(string column)
        {
            if (null == _view.Columns[column])
                return true;
            bool all_same = AllColumnsSameValue(column);
            if (all_same)
                HideColumn(column);
            return all_same;
        }

        public bool AnyRowsFiltered()
        {
            if (_view == null)
                return false;
            if (_view.ActiveFilter == null || !_view.ActiveFilterEnabled || _view.ActiveFilter.Expression == "")
                return false;
            return true;
        }



        public List<T> GetFilteredList<T>(string column)
        {
            List<T> list = new List<T>();
            DataView view = GetFilteredRows();
            foreach (DataRowView rowView in view)
            {
                DataRow row = rowView.Row;
                object o = row[column];
                T t = (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(o, typeof(T));
                if (!list.Contains(t))
                    list.Add(t);
                
            }
            return list;
        }

        public void SelectsRowBasedOnColumn<T>(string column_to_match, List<T> matches)
        {
            var matching_handles = GetRowHanldesThatMatchAny<T>(column_to_match, matches);
            matching_handles.ForEach(n => _view.SelectRow(n));
        }
        public void HighlightRowBasedOnColumn<T>(string column_to_match, T matches)
        {
            _view.SelectRowBasedOnID(column_to_match, matches);
        }

        public void CheckOrUncheckColumnBasedOnMatch<T>(string column_to_match, List<T> matches,string col_to_check_or_uncheck, bool checked_yes_no)
        {
            var matching_handles = GetRowHanldesThatMatchAny<T>(column_to_match, matches);
            matching_handles.ForEach(n => _view.SetRowCellValue(n, col_to_check_or_uncheck, checked_yes_no));
        }
        public void CheckUncheckEntireColumn(string column_to_perform,bool checked_yes_no)
        {
            var handles = GetAllRowHandles();
            foreach(int i in handles)
            {
                _view.SetRowCellValue(i,column_to_perform, checked_yes_no);
            }
            
        }
        public List<int> GetRowHanldesThatMatchAny<T>(string column_to_match,List<T> matches)
        {
            List<int> matching_handles = new List<int>();
            var handles = GetAllRowHandles();
            foreach (int handle in handles)
            {
                object cell_value = _view.GetRowCellValue(handle, column_to_match);
                T cell = (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(cell_value, typeof(T));
                if(matches.Contains(cell))
                {
                    matching_handles.Add(handle);
                }
            }
            return matching_handles;
        }
        public List<T> GetSelectedRowList<T>(string column,bool ignore_blanks)
        {
            List<T> list = new List<T>();
            int[] handles = _view.GetSelectedRows();
            foreach (int i in handles)
            {
                DataRowView row = (DataRowView)_view.GetRow(i);
                object o = row[column];
                if(ignore_blanks && (DBNull.Value == o || null == o))
                {
                    continue;
                }
                T t = (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(o, typeof(T));
                if (!list.Contains(t))
                    list.Add(t);
                
            }
            return list;
        }

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        private List<int> GetAllRowHandles()
        {

            List<int> handles = new List<int>();
            for (int i = 0; i < _view.RowCount; i++)
            {
                DataRowView row = _view.GetRow(i) as DataRowView;
                if (row != null)
                {
                    int handle = _view.GetRowHandle(i);
                    handles.Add(handle);
                }
            }
            return handles;
        }

        public bool? IsRowVisible(string search_col, object search_val)
        {
            int rowhandle = _view.LocateByValue(search_col, search_val);
            var is_visible = _view.IsRowVisible(rowhandle);
            return (is_visible == RowVisibleState.Visible) || (is_visible == RowVisibleState.Partially);
            return null;
        }

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        

        public void DeleteFilteredRows()
        {
            int total_rows = _view.DataRowCount;
            List<int> rows_to_delete = new List<int>();
            for (int i = 0; i != total_rows; i++)
            {
                if (_view.IsRowVisible(i) == RowVisibleState.Hidden)
                {
                    rows_to_delete.Add(i);
                }
            }

            for (int i = 0; i != rows_to_delete.Count; i++)
            {
                _view.DeleteRow(rows_to_delete[i]);
            }

        }

        private void _gc_ProcessGridKey(object sender, System.Windows.Forms.KeyEventArgs e)
        {
            GridControl gc = sender as GridControl;

            if (e.KeyCode == System.Windows.Forms.Keys.V && e.Modifiers == System.Windows.Forms.Keys.Control && !gc.MainView().IsEditorFocused)
            {
                
                _view.HandleCopyPaste(false, true);
                e.Handled = true;
            }


        }

        public int GetBestWidthSafe(string column)
        {


            if (_view.GridControl.InvokeRequired)
            {
                object o = _view.GridControl.Invoke(new MethodInvoker(() => { GetBestWidthSafe(column); }));
                if (null != o)

                else
                    return -1;
            }
            else
            {
                return _view.Columns[column].GetBestWidth();
            }

        private void _view_KeyDown(object sender, System.Windows.Forms.KeyEventArgs e)
        {
            if (e.Control && e.KeyCode == System.Windows.Forms.Keys.C)
            {
                GridView View = sender as GridView;
                if (View.GetRowCellValue(View.FocusedRowHandle, View.FocusedColumn) != null && View.GetRowCellValue(View.FocusedRowHandle, View.FocusedColumn).ToString() != String.Empty)
                {

                    string to_copy = "";

                    if (View.OptionsSelection.MultiSelectMode == GridMultiSelectMode.CellSelect)
                    {
                        GridCell[] cells = View.GetSelectedCells();


                        foreach (GridCell c in cells)
                        {
                            string copy_local = View.GetRowValue<string>(c.RowHandle, c.Column.FieldName) +
                                                Environment.NewLine;
                            if (!String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(copy_local))
                                to_copy += copy_local;
                        }

                    }
                    else
                    {
                        to_copy = View.GetRowCellValue(View.FocusedRowHandle, View.FocusedColumn).ToString();
                    }

                    if (String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(to_copy))
                        Clipboard.Clear();
                    else
                        Clipboard.SetText(to_copy);
                    
                    e.Handled = true;
                }
            }
            if (e.KeyCode == System.Windows.Forms.Keys.F2)
                _AllowEdit = true;

        }

        bool _AllowEdit;
        private void _view_ShowingEditor(object sender, System.ComponentModel.CancelEventArgs e)
        {
            GridView s = sender as GridView;

            if (_editable_columns.Contains(s.FocusedColumn.FieldName))
                return;
            
            e.Cancel = !_AllowEdit;
        }

        public string GetVisibleCSVString()
        {
            List<string> cols = new List<string>();
            foreach (GridColumn gc in _view.VisibleColumns)

                }
            }
            return String.Join(",", cols.ToArray());
        }

        public void ShowCount(string csv_cols, string display_format)
        {
            ShowGridCalcs(csv_cols, display_format, DevExpress.Data.SummaryItemType.Count);
        }

        public void ShowGridCalcs(string csv_cols, string display_format, DevExpress.Data.SummaryItemType sit)
        {
            if (null == csv_cols)
                return;
            foreach (string s in csv_cols.Split(','))
            {
                
                
                
                _view.Columns[s].Summary.AddSafe(s, display_format,sit);
            }
            if (!_view.IsShowRowFooters())
                this.ShowFooter(true);
        }

        {
            SetGrid(o, csv_visible_cols, null, null, true, null, true);
        }
        


        public DataSet _DataSet;
        public DataTable _DataTable;

        public void RejectDataSourceChanges()
        {
            foreach (DataTable tbl in _DataSet.Tables)
            {
                tbl.RejectChanges();
            }
            _view.PopulateColumns();
            _view.CleanColumns(null);

        }
        public bool DataSetHasChanges()
        {

            foreach (DataTable tbl in _DataSet.Tables)
            {
                DataTable c = tbl.GetChanges();
                if (null != c && c.Rows.Count > 0)
                    return true;
            }
            return false;
        }
        public bool ActivelyEditing { get { return _editable_columns.Count > 0; } }

        List<string> _editable_columns = new List<string>();


        public void AddEditableColumn(IEnumerable<string> columns)
        {
            foreach (string s in columns)
                AddEditableColumn(s);
        }

        public void AddEditableColumn(string column)
        {
            _editable_columns.Add(column);
        }

        bool adding_color = false;
        bool auto_commit = true;

        public void RemoveColumnsFromDataSource(IEnumerable<string> columns)
        {
            DataTable raw = GetUnderlyingTable(null);
            foreach (string s in columns)
            {
                raw.Columns.Remove(s);
            }
        }

        public DataTable GetUnderlyingTable(Nullable<int> table_number)
        {
            DataTable raw = null;
            if (null == _datasource)
                return null;
            if (_datasource.GetType() == typeof(DataSet))
                raw = ((DataSet)_datasource).Tables[null == table_number ? 0 : table_number.Value];
            else
                raw = (DataTable)_datasource;
            return raw;
        }

                _view.BestFitColumns();
            }

        public LazyTable _lt;
        public void SetupGenericLazyTable(string updating_table,string lazy_update_keys_csv,bool check_if_exists, Dictionary<string,string> column_remap,Dictionary<string,string> next_ids,List<string> do_not_insert_update,List<string> columns_to_return_on_insert)
        {
            _lt = new LazyTable(this, this._server, updating_table, lazy_update_keys_csv, check_if_exists, column_remap,do_not_insert_update);
            _lt.SetNextIDPopulates(next_ids);
            _lt.SetColumnsToReturnOnInsert(columns_to_return_on_insert);
            _lt.SetDoNotInsertUpdate(do_not_insert_update);
        }



        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        


        
        
        

        

        
        


        
        
        
        
        
        


        

        
        
        
        
        

        public void ToggleColumnAutoWidth(bool enable)
        {
            if (_gc.InvokeRequired)
            {
                _gc.Invoke(new MethodInvoker(() => { ToggleColumnAutoWidth(enable); }));
            }
            else
            {
                _view.OptionsView.ColumnAutoWidth = enable;
            }
        }
        private void LinkRowColors(DataTable main, DataTable color_type)
        {
            bool changed = false;
            if (null != color_type)
            {
                if (null == main.Columns["row_color"])
                {
                    main.Columns.Add("row_color");
                    changed = true;
                }
            }

            foreach (DataRow individual in main.Rows)
            {
                string iticker = individual["ticker"].ToString();
                foreach (DataRow row in color_type.Rows)
                {
                    string ticker = row["linked_ticker"].ToString();
                    if (iticker == ticker)
                    {
                        string color = row["row_color"].ToString();
                        individual["row_color"] = color;
                    }
                }
            }
            if (changed)
            {
                main.AcceptChanges();
            }
        }

        
        
        
        

        public void ToggleGroupBy(bool enable)
        {
            _view.OptionsView.ShowGroupPanel = enable;
        }

        Dictionary<string, string> sort_cols = new Dictionary<string, string>();
        public void SetCustomSort(string display_column, string underlying_sort_column, DevExpress.Data.ColumnSortOrder sort = DevExpress.Data.ColumnSortOrder.None)
        {
            if (_view.Columns[display_column].SortMode == ColumnSortMode.Default)
            {
                _view.CustomColumnSort += ViewDetail_CustomColumnSort;
                _view.Columns[display_column].SortModeSafe(_gc,DevExpress.XtraGrid.ColumnSortMode.Custom);
                if (!sort_cols.ContainsKey(display_column))
                    sort_cols.Add(display_column, underlying_sort_column);
                
                SetColumnSortOrderSafe(display_column, sort);
            }
        }


        public void SetColumnSortOrderSafe(string display_column, DevExpress.Data.ColumnSortOrder sort)
        {
            if (_gc.InvokeRequired)
            {
                _gc.Invoke(new MethodInvoker(() => { SetColumnSortOrderSafe(display_column, sort); }));
            }
            else
            {
                _view.Columns[display_column].SortOrder = sort;
            }
        }




        public void ViewDetail_CustomColumnSort(object sender, DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Base.CustomColumnSortEventArgs e)
        {
            GridView view = sender as GridView;
            if (null == view)
                return;
            foreach (KeyValuePair<string, string> kvp in sort_cols)
            {
                if (e.Column.FieldName == kvp.Key)
                {
                    

                    string one_str = ((DataRowView)e.RowObject1)[kvp.Value].ToString();
                    Int32.TryParse(one_str, out int one);
                    
                    string two_str = ((DataRowView)e.RowObject2)[kvp.Value].ToString();
                    Int32.TryParse(two_str, out int two);

                    
                    

                    e.Handled = true;
                    e.Result = System.Collections.Comparer.Default.Compare(one, two);
                    
                }
            }
        }

        public class AsyncHelperSetAsyncColor
        {
            bool _include_holders;
            List<string> _tickers;
            List<int> _accounts;
            string _parent_format;
            bool _include_todays_bwics;
            bool _allow_no_tickers;
            bool _include_trade_history;
            bool _include_portfolios;
            bool _other_registration;
            bool _set_color_as_main_grid;
            bool _apply_account_filter_to_color;
            bool _process_row_colors;
            bool _include_naic_trades;
            bool _include_ooc_bids;
            bool _include_me_marks;

            bool _async;
            AddColorDelegate _acd;
            string _server;
            DataSet _set;
            public bool IsExecuting = false;
            public bool IsCanceled = false;
            Query.PostAction _pa = null;

            public AsyncHelperSetAsyncColor(string server, List<string> tickers, bool include_holders, bool include_trade_history, List<int> accounts, string parent_format, bool include_todays_bwics, bool allow_no_tickers, bool async, AddColorDelegate acd, bool include_portfolios, bool other_registration, bool set_color_as_main_grid, bool apply_account_filter_to_color, bool process_row_colors, bool include_naic_trades, bool include_ooc_bids, bool include_me_marks)
            {
                _tickers = tickers;
                _include_holders = include_holders;
                _accounts = accounts;
                _parent_format = parent_format;
                _include_todays_bwics = include_todays_bwics;
                _include_trade_history = include_trade_history;
                _include_portfolios = include_portfolios;
                _other_registration = other_registration;
                _set_color_as_main_grid = set_color_as_main_grid;
                _apply_account_filter_to_color = apply_account_filter_to_color;
                _process_row_colors = process_row_colors;
                _include_naic_trades = include_naic_trades;
                _include_ooc_bids = include_ooc_bids;
                _include_me_marks = include_me_marks;

                _async = async;
                _acd = acd;
                _server = server;
                _allow_no_tickers = allow_no_tickers;
                _pa = Done;
            }

            public void CancelQuery()
            {
                _pa = null;
                if (IsExecuting)
                {
                    IsCanceled = true;
                    _acd = null;
                    if (null != _colorQuery)
                        _colorQuery.CancelQuery();
                }
            }

            private Query _colorQuery = null;
            private ExtraAction _ea;
            public void AddExtraAction(ExtraAction ea)
            {
                if (null != ea)
                    _ea = ea;
            }
            public void Execute()
            {
                IsExecuting = true;
                if (_allow_no_tickers == false && (null == _tickers || _tickers.Count == 0))
                {
                    return;
                }
                
                if (_async)
                    _colorQuery.ExecuteAsync(_pa);
                else
                {
                    _set = _colorQuery.Execute();
                    if (null != _pa)
                        _pa(_set);
                    if (null != _ea)
                        _ea();
                }
            }

            public void Done(DataSet set)
            {
                IsExecuting = false;
                if (IsCanceled)
                {
                    return;
                }
                _set = set;
                if (null != _acd)
                    _acd(_set, _include_holders, _accounts, _parent_format, _include_todays_bwics, _allow_no_tickers, _set_color_as_main_grid);
                if (null != _ea)
                    _ea();
            }
        }

        public void BoldColumn(string column)
        {
            var font = new Font(_view.Columns[column].AppearanceCell.Font, FontStyle.Bold);
            _view.Columns[column].AppearanceCell.Font = font;
        }

        public delegate void AddColorDelegate(DataSet tbl, bool include_holders, List<int> accounts, string parent_format, bool include_todays_bwics, bool allow_no_tickers, bool set_color_as_main_grid);
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        



        public void CancelAnyAsyncQueries()
        {
            if (null != _adding_color)
                _adding_color.CancelQuery();
        }
        AsyncHelperSetAsyncColor _adding_color;
        public delegate void ExtraAction();
        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        


        public bool AllTickersInDataSets(IEnumerable<string> main, IEnumerable<string> color)
        {
            
            
            
            
            IEnumerable<string> diff = color.Except(main);

            return diff.Count() == 0;
        }

        public void ToggleEditing(IEnumerable<string> columnNames, Nullable<System.Drawing.Color> color)
        {

            bool editing = _view.AnyColumnEditing(columnNames);
            if (editing)
            {
                SetEditable(columnNames, CommonInterfaces.Constants.BADGER.EDIT_COLOR,true);
            }
            else
            
            {
                _DataTable.RejectChanges();
                DisableEditing();
                
            }

        }
        public void SetEditable(IEnumerable<string> columnNames, Nullable<System.Drawing.Color> color,bool enable)
        {
            if (enable)
                _editable_columns.AddRange(columnNames);
            else
                _editable_columns.RemoveRange<string>(columnNames);
            
            _view.SetEditable(columnNames, color, enable);
        }

            _view.SetReadOnly(columnNames);
        }

        public void RemoveFromEdit(IEnumerable<string> columnNames, Nullable<System.Drawing.Color> color)
        {
            foreach (string s in columnNames)
                _editable_columns.Remove(s);
            _view.SetReadOnly(columnNames, color);
        }

        private static Dictionary<string, Image> _iconCache;

        public static Image GetImageCache(string key)
        {
            
            {
                if (null == _iconCache)
                {
                    _iconCache = new Dictionary<string, Image>();
                    
                }

                if (!_iconCache.ContainsKey(key))
                {
                    string file_only = @"Images\" + key + ".ico";
                    string folder = Path.GetDirectoryName(System.Reflection.Assembly.GetExecutingAssembly().Location);
                    string file = Path.Combine(folder, file_only);
                    bool exists = File.Exists(file);
                    if (!exists)
                    {
                        XtraMessageBox.Show("Icon doesn't exist: " + file);
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        var i = Image.FromFile(file);

                        _iconCache.Add(key, i);
                    }
                    

                }

                return _iconCache[key];
            }
        }


        private static Dictionary<string, SvgImage> _iconCacheSVG;

        public static SvgImage GetSVGImageCache(string key)
        {
            
            {
                if (null == _iconCacheSVG)
                {
                    _iconCacheSVG = new Dictionary<string, SvgImage>();
 
                }

                if (!_iconCacheSVG.ContainsKey(key))
                {
                    string file = @"Images\" + key + ".png";
                    if(!File.Exists(file))
                        file = @"Images\" + key + ".svg";
                    if (File.Exists(file))
                    {
                        var i = SvgImage.FromFile(file);

                        _iconCacheSVG.Add(key, i);
                        
                    }
                }

                return _iconCacheSVG[key];
            }
        }

        public GridView _popup_grid;
        private void _view_DefaultPopups(object sender, PopupMenuShowingEventArgs e)
        {
            _popup_grid = e.HitInfo.View;
            if (e.MenuType == GridMenuType.Column)
            {
                if (null != _view.ActiveFilterCriteria)
                {
                    DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem item = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("Clear All Filters", ClearAllColumnFilters, GetImageCache("Clear"));
                    e.Menu.Items.Add(item);
                }
            }
            else if (e.MenuType == GridMenuType.Row)
            {

                DevExpress.XtraGrid.Menu.GridViewMenu menu = e.Menu as GridViewMenu;
                

                DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem item = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("Export to Excel", this.ExportGridViewToExcel, GetImageCache("Excel"));
                item.BeginGroup = true;
                menu.Items.Add(item);


                DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem show_editor = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("Show Editor", this.ShowEditor);
                menu.Items.Add(show_editor);

                if (null != _view.Columns["address_full"])
                {

                }

                if (null != _view.Columns["asset_id"])
                {

                    DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXSubMenuItem remind_sub = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXSubMenuItem("Remind Me");
                    remind_sub.ImageOptions.Image = GetImageCache("RemindMe");
                    remind_sub.BeginGroup = true;

                    UtilsLib.Dates.XDateTime xd = new Dates.XDateTime();
                    DateTime nextbday = xd.NextBusinessDay();

                    string base_msg = "Tomorrow";

                    if (!nextbday.SameDay(DateTime.Now.AddDays(1)))
                        base_msg = nextbday.ToString("ddd");
                    DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem morning = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem(base_msg + " - 8AM", this.RemindTomorrowMorning);
                    DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem tomorrow = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem(base_msg, this.RemindTomorrow);
                    DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem week = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("a Week", this.RemindNextWeek);
                    DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem month = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("a Month", this.RemindNextMonth);
                    remind_sub.Items.Add(morning);
                    remind_sub.Items.Add(tomorrow);
                    remind_sub.Items.Add(week);
                    remind_sub.Items.Add(month);
                    menu.Items.Add(remind_sub);
                }

                DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem clip = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("Copy Grid to Clipboard", this.CopyGridViewToClipboard, GetImageCache("clipboard"));
                menu.Items.Add(clip);

                DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem clip_assets = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("Copy Asset ID's to Clipboard", this.CopyAssetsToClipboard, GetImageCache("clipboard"));
                menu.Items.Add(clip_assets);


                
                
                
                
                


                
                





                
                
                

                
                

                



                
                


                
                
                
                




            }
        }

        public void SendBBGCmdLazy(string cmd)
        {
            string ticker = _view.GetActiveRowValue<string>("ticker");
            string format = String.Format("{0} <{2}> {1}<go>", ticker, cmd, "mtge");
            if (null != _view.Columns["bbg_id"])
            {
                string bbg_id = _view.GetActiveRowValue<string>("bbg_id");
                format = String.Format("{0} {1} {2}<go>", "ID", bbg_id, cmd);
                format = String.Format("{0} {1} <go>{2}<go>", "ID", bbg_id, cmd);
            }
            if (null == _dde)
            {
                _dde = new BBGDDE();
                System.Threading.Thread.Sleep(300);
            }
            _dde.Send(format);
        }
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        


        public void SetUpDropdown(DataTable table, string which_column_to_apply_on, string display_column, string value_column,string[] visible_columns = null,int? popup_width = null)
        {
            RepositoryItemLookUpEdit li = new RepositoryItemLookUpEdit();
            li.PopulateGridLookup(table, display_column, value_column, visible_columns);
            li.PopupWidthMode = PopupWidthMode.ContentWidth;
            li.SearchMode = DevExpress.XtraEditors.Controls.SearchMode.AutoSearch;
            li.ImmediatePopup = true;
            
            if (null != popup_width)
                li.PopupWidth = popup_width.Value;
            _view.SetRepositoryItemLookUpEdit(_view.Columns[which_column_to_apply_on], li);
        }

        public void SetUpRepositoryItemMemoEx(string column,int popup_width_300,int max_height_1250)
        {
            RepositoryItemMemoExEdit me = new RepositoryItemMemoExEdit();
            me.WordWrap = true;
            
            me.ValidateOnEnterKey = true;
            me.ShowIcon = false;
            me.PopupFormMinSize = new Size(popup_width_300, 0);
            me.AcceptsTab = true;
            me.ScrollBars = ScrollBars.Vertical;
            me.MaxLength = max_height_1250;
            me.AutoHeight = true;
            _view.SetRepositoryItemMemoExEdit(_view.Columns[column], me);
        }


        public string ExportToHTMLSimple()
        {
            string str;
            MemoryStream ms = new MemoryStream();
            try
            {
                _view.ExportToHtml(ms);
                ms.Seek(0, SeekOrigin.Begin);
                StreamReader sr = new StreamReader(ms);
                str = sr.ReadToEnd();
            }
            finally
            {
                ms.Close();
            }
            return str;
        }

        public T GetActiveRowValue<T>(string fieldName, bool fail_if_col_no_exist = true)

        public T? GetActiveRowValueNullable<T>(string fieldName, bool fail_if_col_no_exist = true) where T : struct
        {
            return _view.GetActiveRowValueNullable<T>(fieldName, fail_if_col_no_exist);
        }
        public int[] GetSelectedRowHandles()
        {
            return _view.GetSelectedRows();
        }

        public int[] GetAllRows()
        {
            
            
            int rowHandle = 0;
            List<int> rows = new List<int>();
            while (_view.IsValidRowHandle(rowHandle))
            {
           
         
                rows.Add(rowHandle);
                rowHandle++;
            }
            return rows.ToArray();
        }

        public T GetRowValue<T>(int row_handle, string fieldName)
        {

            object o = _view.GetRowCellValue(row_handle, fieldName);

            return (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(o, typeof(T));
        }
        public T? GetRowValueNullable<T>(int row_handle, string fieldName) where T : struct
        {

            object o = _view.GetRowCellValue(row_handle, fieldName);
            if (null == o || DBNull.Value == o)
                return null;

            return (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(o, typeof(T));
        }

        public T GetFocusedRowValue<T>(string fieldName)
        {
            return (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(_view.GetFocusedRowCellValue(fieldName), typeof(T));
        }
        public T? GetFocusedRowValueNullable<T>(string fieldName) where T : struct
        {
            object o = _view.GetFocusedRowCellValue(fieldName);
            if (o == DBNull.Value || o == null)
                return null;

            return (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(_view.GetFocusedRowCellValue(fieldName), typeof(T));
        }



        public T GetRowValue<T>( int row_handle, string fieldName, bool fail_if_column_doesnt_exist = true)
        {
            object o = _view.GetRowCellValue(row_handle, fieldName);
            

            return (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(o, typeof(T));
        }

        }

        }

            }

        {

            xd.AddBusinessDays(1);
            DateTime next = xd.Date.AddHours(8);
            RemindMeInternal(1, _view, null, true, null, next);
        }

        public static void RemindMeInternal(int days, GridView _view, string body, bool only_selected, string homeowner, DateTime? date_ovr = null)
        {

            DateTime date = DateTime.Now.AddDays(days);
            UtilsLib.Dates.XDateTime d = new Dates.XDateTime(date);
            if (!d.IsWorkDay)
            {
                date = d.NextBusinessDay();
            }

            if (null != date_ovr)
                date = date_ovr.Value;
            
            string asset_id = _view.GetActiveRowValue<string>("asset_id", false, false);
            string address_full = _view.GetActiveRowValue<string>("address_full", false, false);
            string nice_name = null;
            if(null != _view.Columns["name_simple"])
            {
                nice_name = _view.GetActiveRowValue<string>("name_simple", false, false);
            }

            string subject = $"Homeowner Reminder  ::  {nice_name} - {address_full}";

            Mail.RemindMeIn(subject, body, date);
        }

            _view.OptionsBehavior.EditingMode = DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Grid.GridEditingMode.EditFormInplace;
            _view.ShowPopupEditForm();
            _view.OptionsBehavior.EditingMode = before;

        public void AcceptChanges()
        {
            _DataTable.AcceptChanges();

        public DataTable GetChangedRows()
        {
            DataTable changes = _DataTable.GetChanges();
            return changes;
        }


        public List<DataColumn> GetChangedColumns()
        {
            DataTable changes = GetChangedRows();
            if (null == changes || changes.Rows.Count == 0)
            {
                return null;
            }
            List<DataColumn> changed = changes.GetChangedColumns();
            return changed;
        }
        public bool AnyChanges()
        {
            DataTable changes = GetChangedRows();
            if (null == changes)
                return false;
            return changes.Rows.Count > 0;
        }

        public void CollapseAllRows()
        {
            if (_gc.InvokeRequired)
            {
                _gc.Invoke(new MethodInvoker(() => { CollapseAllRows(); }));
            }
            else
            {
                _view.CollapseAllDetails();
            }
        }

        public void SetEnabled(bool enable)
        {
            if (_gc.InvokeRequired)
            {
                _gc.Invoke(new MethodInvoker(() => { SetEnabled(enable); }));
            }
            else
            {
                _gc.Enabled = enable;
            }
        }

        public void FindAndExpandUnsafe(string column, object item, bool select)
        {
            Nullable<int> find_handle_based_on_value = FindHandleBasedOnId(column, item);
            if (null != find_handle_based_on_value)
            {
                if (select)
                    _view.SelectRowBasedOnID(column, item);
                _view.SetMasterRowExpanded(find_handle_based_on_value.Value, true);
            }
        }


        public void FindAndExpand(string column, object o, bool select)
        {
            if (_gc.InvokeRequired)
            {
                _gc.Invoke(new MethodInvoker(() => { FindAndExpand(column, o, select); }));
            }
            else
            {
                FindAndExpandUnsafe(column, o, select);
            }
        }

        public Nullable<int> FindHandleBasedOnId(string column, object item)
        {
            Nullable<int> find_handle_based_on_value = null;
            int dataRowCount = _view.DataRowCount;
            for (int rHandle = 0; rHandle < dataRowCount; rHandle++)
            {
                object o = _view.GetRowValue<object>(rHandle, column);
                if (null != o && o.Equals(item))
                    return rHandle;
            }
            return null;
        }

        public bool FindAndFocusOnId(string column, object item)
        {
            int? row_id = FindHandleBasedOnId(column, item);
            if (null == row_id)
                return false;
            UnselectAllRows();
            _view.SelectRow(row_id.Value);
            
            
            
            return true;
        }

        public void UnselectAllRows()
        {
            int[] rows = _view.GetSelectedRows();
            rows.ForEach(n => _view.UnselectRow(n));
        }
        public void SetMasterRowExpandedSafe(int row_handle, bool expand)
        {
            if (_gc.InvokeRequired)
            {
                _gc.Invoke(new MethodInvoker(() => { SetMasterRowExpandedSafe(row_handle, expand); }));
            }
            else
            {
                _view.SetMasterRowExpanded(row_handle, true);
            }
        }
        public void ExpandAllRows()
        {
            _view.BeginUpdateSafe();
            try
            {
                int dataRowCount = _view.DataRowCount;
                for (int rHandle = 0; rHandle < dataRowCount; rHandle++)
                    SetMasterRowExpandedSafe(rHandle, true);
            }
            finally
            {
                _view.EndUpdateSafe();
            }
        }


        public delegate int UpdateRowAction(DataRow row,List<DataColumn> cols_modified);
        public delegate int UpdateTableHelperDelegate(UpdateRowAction action, IWriter writer, bool end_user_confirmation);
        private List<DataColumn> PruneUneditableDataColumns(List<DataColumn> cols)
        {
            List<DataColumn> final = new List<DataColumn>();
            foreach(DataColumn col in cols)
            {
                
                if(_editable_columns.Contains(col.ColumnName))
                    final.Add(col);
            }
            return final;
        }
        public int UpdateTableHelper(UpdateRowAction action,IWriter writer,bool end_user_confirmation)
        {
             bool any_changes = this.AnyChanges();
            int change_count = 0;
            if (any_changes)
            {
                DataTable changes = this.GetChangedRows();
                List<DataColumn> changedCols = changes.GetChangedColumns();
                changedCols = PruneUneditableDataColumns(changedCols);
                List<string> errors = new List<string>();
                
                DXETA eta = new DXETA(changes.Rows.Count, writer, _gc);
                foreach (DataRow row in changes.Rows)
                {
                    change_count += action(row,changedCols);
                    eta.IncrementAndReport();
                  }

                this.AcceptChanges();

                
            }
            if (end_user_confirmation)
                XtraMessageBox.Show($"Total Changes Made: {change_count}", "Confirmation...");
            return change_count;
        }


    }
}

namespace DXHelper

    public static class GridSummaryItemCollectionHelper

        public static void AddSafe(this GridSummaryItemCollection coll,string field,string display_format, DevExpress.Data.SummaryItemType sit)
        {
            if (coll.View.GridControl.InvokeRequired)
            {
                coll.View.GridControl.Invoke(new MethodInvoker(() => { AddSafe(coll,field,display_format,sit); }));
            }
            else
            {
                ((GridView) coll.View).Columns[field].Summary.Add(sit, field, display_format);
            }
        }

    }

        public static void HandleCopyPaste(this GridView view, bool cleanPaste, bool trim)
        {
            
            
            try
            {
                IDataObject dataObj = Clipboard.GetDataObject();
                List<string> data = new List<string>();
                string[] dataArray = dataObj.GetData(DataFormats.Text).ToString().Split(Environment.NewLine);
                int[] selected = view.GetSelectedRows();

                string columnName = null;
                if (null != view.FocusedColumn)
                    columnName = view.FocusedColumn.FieldName;

                if (view.OptionsBehavior.ReadOnly || !view.FocusedColumn.OptionsColumn.AllowEdit || view.FocusedColumn.OptionsColumn.ReadOnly)
                {
                    XtraMessageBox.Show("You're pasting over a ReadOnly column", "ERROR");
                    return;
                }


                
                
                
                



                int rowCounts = dataArray.Length;

                if (dataArray.Length > rowCounts)
                {
                    DataTable table = ((DataView)view.DataSource).ToTable();
                    for (int i = dataArray.Length; i != dataArray.Length + 1; i++)
                    {
                        table.Rows.Add();
                    }
                }

                data.AddRange(dataArray);
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(data[data.Count - 1]))
                    data.RemoveAt(data.Count - 1);
                
                if (cleanPaste)
                {
                    for (int i = 0; i != data.Count; i++)
                        if (null != data[i])
                            data[i] = UtilsLib.Clean.SelectOnlyNumbers(data[i]).Trim();
                }
                int number = 0;
                int startingHandle = 0;
                if (selected.Length > 0)
                    startingHandle = selected[0];
                
                for (int i = 0; i != data.Count; i++)
                {
                    try
                    {
                        int currentHandle = startingHandle + i;
                        if (view.IsValidRowHandle(currentHandle))
                        {
                            DataRow row = ((DataRowView)view.GetRow(currentHandle)).Row;

                            row[columnName] = trim ? data[number].Trim() : data[number];

                        }
                    }
                    catch (Exception n)
                    {
                        
                    }
                    number++;
                }
            }
            catch (Exception n)
            {

            }
        }

        public static void CleanColumns(this GridView gv, Fields f, string csv_fields, bool do_begin_updates, bool mark_columns_read_only = true, bool repopulate_columns = true)
        {

        public static void CleanColumnsUnsafe(this GridView gv, Fields f, string csv_visible, bool do_begin_updates, bool mark_columns_read_only = true, bool repopulate_columns = true)
        {
            
            
            
            
            

            if (do_begin_updates)
            {
                gv.BeginUpdate();
            }
            if (repopulate_columns)
                gv.PopulateColumnsSafe();
            List<GridColumn> gc = new List<GridColumn>(gv.Columns);
            
            foreach (DevExpress.XtraGrid.Columns.GridColumn c in gc)
            {
                
                
                bool matched = false;
                gv.SetHAlignmentSafe(c, HorzAlignment.Center);
                if (f.ContainsField(c.FieldName))
                {


                    if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(f[c.FieldName].display_format))
                    {
                        c.DisplayFormat.FormatType = DevExpress.Utils.FormatType.Custom;
                        c.DisplayFormat.FormatString = f[c.FieldName].display_format;
                    }
                    if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(f[c.FieldName].display_name))
                    {
                        c.Caption = f[c.FieldName].display_name;
                    }
                    if (f[c.FieldName].hide)
                    {
                        c.Visible = false;
                    }
                    matched = true;
                    if (f[c.FieldName].bold)
                        c.SetBold();
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(f[c.FieldName].alignment))
                    {
                        string align = f[c.FieldName].alignment;
                        if (align == "Center")
                        {
                            c.AppearanceCell.TextOptions.HAlignment = HorzAlignment.Center;
                        }
                        if (align == "Left")
                        {
                            c.AppearanceCell.TextOptions.HAlignment = HorzAlignment.Near;
                        }
                        if (align == "Right")
                        {
                            c.AppearanceCell.TextOptions.HAlignment = HorzAlignment.Far;
                        }
                    }
                }

                else if (c.FieldName.Contains("_id") || (c.FieldName == "id"))
                {
                    List<string> visibles = new List<string>();
                    if (null != csv_visible)
                    {
                        visibles = csv_visible.Split(',').ToList();
                    }
                    if(!visibles.Contains(c.FieldName))
                        c.SetVisibleSafe(false);
                }
                else if (c.FieldName.Contains("_time") && c.ColumnType == typeof(DateTime))
                {
                    c.DisplayFormat.FormatType = DevExpress.Utils.FormatType.Custom;
                    c.DisplayFormat.FormatString = "h:mm tt";
                }
                else if (c.ColumnType == typeof(double))
                {
                    c.DisplayFormat.FormatType = DevExpress.Utils.FormatType.Custom;
                    c.DisplayFormat.FormatString = "0.00";
                }
                string caption = c.Caption;
                if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(caption))
                    caption = c.FieldName;
                caption = caption.Replace("_", " ");
                caption = caption.TitleCase();
                caption = caption.ToUpper();
                gv.SetCaptionSafe(c, caption);
                if (mark_columns_read_only)
                    c.OptionsColumn.ReadOnly = true;
                
            }

            if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(csv_visible))
                gv.SetColumnVisible(csv_visible);

            gv.BestFitColumnsSafe();
            

            foreach (DevExpress.XtraGrid.Columns.GridColumn q in gc)
            {
                if (f.ContainsField(q.FieldName))
                {
                    if (null != f[q.FieldName].force_width)
                    {
                        q.Width = f[q.FieldName].force_width.Value;
                    }
                }
            }


            
            
            if (do_begin_updates)
                gv.EndUpdate();
        }






        public static void SetColumnVisible(this GridView v, string[] columns, bool visible)
        {
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            foreach (string col in columns)
            {
                var c = v.Columns[col];
                if (null != c)
                {
                    int index = Array.IndexOf(columns, c.FieldName);
                    c.Visible = visible;
                    c.VisibleIndex = index;
                }
            }
            foreach (DevExpress.XtraGrid.Columns.GridColumn c in v.Columns)
            {
                if (!columns.ToList<string>().Select(n => n.ToUpper()).Contains(c.FieldName.ToUpper()))
                {
                    c.Visible = !visible;
                }
            }

            
            
            
            

            
            
            
            
            
            
        }

        public static T GetActiveRowValue<T>(this GridView gv, string fieldName, bool fail_if_column_doesnt_exist = true, bool use_focused_if_no_active = true)
        {
            int[] handles = gv.GetSelectedRows();
            if (handles.Length == 0 && use_focused_if_no_active)
                handles = new int[] { gv.FocusedRowHandle };

            if (handles.Length == 0)
                return default(T);
            if (handles.Length != 1)
                throw new Exception("Too many rows selected");
            if ((fail_if_column_doesnt_exist == false && null == gv.Columns[fieldName]) || (handles.Count() == 1 && handles[0] < 0))
            {
                return default(T);
            }

            object o = gv.GetRowCellValue(handles[0], fieldName);
            if (DBNull.Value == o)
                return default(T);
            return (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(o, typeof(T));
        }


        
        
        
        
        
        public static T GetActiveRowValueNullable<T>(this GridView gv, string fieldName, bool fail_if_column_doesnt_exist = true, bool use_focused_if_no_active = true) where T : class
        {
            int[] handles = gv.GetSelectedRows();
            return GetRowValueNullableInternal<T>(gv, handles, fieldName, fail_if_column_doesnt_exist, use_focused_if_no_active);
        }


        public static T GetRowValueNullableInternal<T>(this GridView gv, int[] handles, string fieldName, bool fail_if_column_doesnt_exist = true, bool use_focused_if_no_active = true) where T : class
        {
            
            if (handles.Length == 0 && use_focused_if_no_active)
                handles = new int[] { gv.FocusedRowHandle };

            if (handles.Length == 0)
                return default(T);
            if (handles.Length != 1)
                throw new Exception("Too many rows selected");
            if ((fail_if_column_doesnt_exist == false && null == gv.Columns[fieldName]) || (handles.Count() == 1 && handles[0] < 0))
            {
                return null;
            }

            object o = gv.GetRowCellValue(handles[0], fieldName);
            if (DBNull.Value == o)
                return null;
            return (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(o, typeof(T));
        }
        public static T GetRowValue<T>(this GridView gv, string fieldName, int handle)

        public static void SetActiveRowValue(this GridView gv, string fieldName, object value)

        }

        public static T? GetActiveRowValueNullable<T>(this GridView gv, string fieldName, bool fail_if_column_doesnt_exist = true) where T : struct
        {
            int[] handles = gv.GetSelectedRows();
            if (handles.Length == 0)
                return null;
            if (handles.Length != 1)
                throw new Exception("Too many rows selected");
            if (fail_if_column_doesnt_exist == false && null == gv.Columns[fieldName])
                return null;
            object o = gv.GetRowCellValue(handles[0], fieldName);
            if (null == o || DBNull.Value == o)
                return null;
            return (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(o, typeof(T));
        }





        public static int GetFullChildRowsCount(this GridView view, int groupRowHandle)
        {
            int childRowCount = view.GetChildRowCount(groupRowHandle);
            int childGroupRowCount = 0;
            int nextChildHandle;
            for (int i = 0; i < childRowCount; i++)
            {
                nextChildHandle = view.GetChildRowHandle(groupRowHandle, i);
                if (!view.IsGroupRow(nextChildHandle))
                    return childRowCount;
                else
                    childGroupRowCount += GetFullChildRowsCount(view, nextChildHandle);
            }
            return childGroupRowCount;
        }

        public static bool HideColumnIfSameValue(this GridView _view, string column)
        {
            if (null == _view.Columns[column])
                return true;
            bool all_same = _view.AllColumnsSameValue(column);
            if (all_same)
                _view.Columns[column].Visible = false;
            return all_same;
        }

        
        
        
        

        public static bool AllColumnsSameValue(this GridView _view, string column)
        {
            object first = null;
            DataView view = GetFilteredRows(_view);
            int i = 0;
            bool any_diff = false;
            foreach (DataRowView rowView in view)
            {
                DataRow row = rowView.Row;
                object o = row[column];
                if (i == 0)
                    first = o;
                else
                {
                    if (!first.Equals(o))
                    {
                        any_diff = true;
                        break;
                    }
                }
                i++;
            }
            if (!any_diff)
            {
                return true;
            }
            return false;
        }


        public static DataView GetFilteredRows(this GridView _view)
        {
            if (_view == null)
                return null;
            if (_view.ActiveFilter == null || !_view.ActiveFilterEnabled || _view.ActiveFilter.Expression == "")
                return _view.DataSource as DataView;
            if (null == _view.DataSource)
                return null;
            DataTable table = ((DataView)_view.DataSource).Table;
            DataView filteredDataView = new DataView(table);
            filteredDataView.RowFilter = DevExpress.Data.Filtering.CriteriaToWhereClauseHelper.GetDataSetWhere(_view.ActiveFilterCriteria);
            return filteredDataView;
        }

        public static void SetEditable(this GridView gv, string columNames)
        {
            SetEditable(gv, new string[] { columNames });
        }
        public static void SetEditable(this GridView gv, string columName, Nullable<System.Drawing.Color> color)
        {
            SetColumnState(gv, new string[] { columName }, color, true);
        }


        public static void SetReadOnly(this GridView gv, string columNames)
        {
            SetReadOnly(gv, new string[] { columNames });
        }
        public static void SetEditable(this GridView gv, IEnumerable<string> columnNames, Nullable<System.Drawing.Color> color,bool enable)
        {
            SetColumnState(gv, columnNames, color, enable);
        }

        public static void SetEditable(this GridView gv, IEnumerable<string> columnNames)
        {
            SetColumnState(gv, columnNames, null, true);
        }


        public static void SetReadOnly(this GridView gv, IEnumerable<string> columnNames)
        {
            SetColumnState(gv, columnNames, null, false);
        }
        public static void SetReadOnly(this GridView gv, IEnumerable<string> columnNames, Nullable<System.Drawing.Color> color)
        {
            
            List<string> cols = new List<string>(columnNames);
            foreach (DevExpress.XtraGrid.Columns.GridColumn c in gv.Columns)
            {

                if (cols.Contains(c.FieldName))
                {
                    if (null != color)
                        gv.PaintColumn(c.FieldName, color.Value);
                    c.OptionsColumn.AllowEdit = true;
                    c.OptionsColumn.ReadOnly = true;
                }
            }
        }

        public static bool AnyColumnEditing(this GridView gv, IEnumerable<string> columnNames)
        {
            foreach(string col in columnNames)
            {
                GridColumn c = gv.Columns[col];
                if (c.OptionsColumn.AllowEdit)
                    return true;
            }
            return false;
        }
        public static void SetColumnState(this GridView gv, IEnumerable<string> columnNames, Nullable<System.Drawing.Color> color, bool editable)
        {

            
            {
                
                
            }

            if (null == color)
                color = System.Drawing.Color.OldLace;
            List<string> cols = new List<string>(columnNames);

            foreach (DevExpress.XtraGrid.Columns.GridColumn c in gv.Columns)
            {

                if (cols.Contains(c.FieldName))
                {
                    if (null != color)
                        gv.PaintColumn(c.FieldName, color.Value);
                    c.OptionsColumn.AllowEdit = editable;
                    c.OptionsColumn.ReadOnly = !editable;
                }
                else
                {
                    if (c.OptionsColumn.AllowEdit != true && c.OptionsColumn.ReadOnly != true)
                    {
                        if (null != color)
                            gv.PaintColumn(c.FieldName,"0");
                        c.OptionsColumn.AllowEdit = true;
                        c.OptionsColumn.ReadOnly = true;
                    }
                }
            }
        }



        public static List<T> GetUniqueList<T>(this GridView gv, string column)
        {
            return GetUniqueListInternal<T>(gv, column, true, false, false, false, false, null);
        }
        public static List<T> GetUniqueList<T>(this GridView gv, string column, bool only_selected)
        {
            return GetUniqueListInternal<T>(gv, column, true, only_selected, false, false, false, null);
        }
        public static bool AllValuesMatch<T>(this GridView gv, string column, bool only_selected,T value)
        {
            List<T> vals = GetActiveRowList<T>(gv,column, only_selected).Distinct().ToList();
            if(vals.Count == 1)
            {
                if (vals[0].Equals(value))
                    return true;
            }
            return false;
        }
        public static List<T> GetList<T>(this GridView gv, string column, bool only_selected)
        {
            return GetUniqueListInternal<T>(gv, column, false, only_selected, false, false, false, null);
        }

        public static bool AnyRowMatches<T>(this GridView gv, string column, T value)
        {
            int total_rows = gv.DataRowCount;
            T val_to_match = (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(value, typeof(T));
            List<T> list = new List<T>();
            for (int i = 0; i != total_rows; i++)
            {
                T o = (T)gv.GetRowCellValue(i, column);
                if (o.Equals(val_to_match))
                    return true;

            }
            return false;
        }

        
        

        

        public static List<T> GetUniqueListInternal<T>(this GridView gv, string column, bool unique_only, bool only_selected, bool formatted, bool ignore_blank, bool only_visible, int[] iteration_order)
        {
            if (null == gv)
                return new List<T>();
            int total_rows = gv.DataRowCount;
            List<int> rows = new List<int>();
            List<T> list = new List<T>();
            if (null == iteration_order || (null != iteration_order && iteration_order.Count() == 0))
            {
                for (int i = 0; i != total_rows; i++)
                    rows.Add(i);
            }
            else
            {
                rows = iteration_order.ToList();
            }
            
            foreach (int i in rows)
            {
                if (only_selected && gv.IsRowSelected(i) == false)
                    continue;
                if (only_visible && gv.IsRowVisible(i) == RowVisibleState.Hidden)
                    continue;
                
                object o = "";
                if (formatted)
                    o = gv.GetRowCellDisplayText(i, column);
                else
                    o = gv.GetRowCellValue(i, column);
                if (DBNull.Value == o && default(T) != null)
                    continue;
                T t = (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(o, typeof(T));
                if (!list.Contains(t) || !unique_only)
                {
                    if (!ignore_blank || (ignore_blank && !String.IsNullOrEmpty(t.ToString())))
                        list.Add(t);
                }
            }
            return list;
        }

        public static bool AnyColumnsNull(this GridView gv, int rowHandle, IEnumerable<string> columns)
        {
            foreach (string s in columns)
            {
                object o = gv.GetRowValue<object>(rowHandle, s);
                if (null == o || DBNull.Value == o)
                    return true;
            }
            return false;
        }
        public static int VisibleRowCount(this GridView gv)
        {
            int visible_rows = 0;
            int total_rows = gv.DataRowCount;
            for (int i = 0; i != total_rows; i++)
            {
                if (gv.IsRowVisible(i) == RowVisibleState.Visible)
                    visible_rows++;
            }
            return visible_rows;
        }

        public static List<T> GetColumnList<T>(this GridView gv, string column)
        {
            return GetUniqueListInternal<T>(gv, column, false, false, false, false, false, null);
        }

    }
}

namespace DXHelper
{
    public class GridViewCustom : GridView
    {
        public GridViewCustom() : this(null) { }
        public GridViewCustom(DevExpress.XtraGrid.GridControl grid) : base(grid)
        {
            
        }
        protected override string ViewName { get { return "MyCustomGridView"; } }

    }


    public class GridViewInfoCustom : GridViewInfo
    {

        public GridViewInfoCustom(DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Grid.GridView gridView) : base(gridView) { }

        public override int CalcRowHeight(Graphics graphics, int rowVisibleIndex, int rowHandle, int min, int level, bool useCache, GridColumnsInfo columns)
        {
            if (base.GridControl.InvokeRequired)
            {
                return System.Convert.ToInt32(base.GridControl.Invoke(new MethodInvoker(() => { CalcRowHeight(graphics, rowVisibleIndex, rowHandle, min, level, useCache, columns); })));
            }
            else
            {
                return base.CalcRowHeight(graphics, rowHandle, rowVisibleIndex, MinRowHeight, level, useCache, columns);
            }
        }


        
        
        
        
        

        double zoom = 0;
        public void SetZoom(double zoom_pct)
        {
            zoom = zoom_pct;
        }

        public override int MinRowHeight
        {
            get { return base.MinRowHeight - ((int)(3 * zoom)); }
        }
        protected override int CalcMinColumnRowHeight(int headerHeight)
        {

            return base.CalcMinColumnRowHeight(headerHeight) - ((int)(2 * zoom));
        }

        protected override int CalcGroupPanelHeight()
        {
            return base.CalcGroupPanelHeight() - ((int)(2 * zoom));
        }

        protected override int GetFooterPanelHeight()
        {
            return base.GetFooterPanelHeight() - ((int)(4 * zoom));
        }
    }
}


--- FILE: DXHelper\GridViewHelper.cs ---
namespace DXHelper
{
    public class GVH
    {
        private GridView _gv;
        private string _server;
        public GVH(GridView gv, string server)
        {
            _gv = gv;
            _server = server;
        }

        

        private void viewDetail_PopupMenuShowing(object sender, PopupMenuShowingEventArgs e)
        {
            if (e.MenuType == GridMenuType.Row)
            {
                DevExpress.XtraGrid.Menu.GridViewMenu menu = e.Menu as GridViewMenu;
                menu.Items.Clear();
                DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem item = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("Export to Excel", this.ExportGridViewToExcel);
                menu.Items.Add(item);

                DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem expand = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("Expand all Rows", this.ExpandAllRows);
                menu.Items.Add(expand);

                DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem collapse = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("Collapse all Rows", this.CollapseAllRows);
                menu.Items.Add(collapse);
                

            }
        }

        public void ExpandAllRows(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            ExpandAllRows();
        }
        public void CollapseAllRows(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            CollapseAllRows();
        }


        public void CollapseAllRows()
        {
            _gv.CollapseAllDetails();
        }
        public void ExpandAllRows()
        {
            _gv.BeginUpdate();
            try
            {
                int dataRowCount = _gv.DataRowCount;
                for (int rHandle = 0; rHandle < dataRowCount; rHandle++)
                    _gv.SetMasterRowExpanded(rHandle, true);
            }
            finally
            {
                _gv.EndUpdate();
            }
        }

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        public void ExportExcelQuick(bool show_in_folder = false)
        {
            ExportExcelQuick(_gv, show_in_folder);
        }
        public static void CopyGridToClipboard(GridView gv, bool alert)
        {
            gv.OptionsClipboard.AllowExcelFormat = DevExpress.Utils.DefaultBoolean.False;
            gv.OptionsClipboard.ClipboardMode = DevExpress.Export.ClipboardMode.Formatted;
            gv.OptionsClipboard.CopyCollapsedData = DevExpress.Utils.DefaultBoolean.True;
            gv.OptionsClipboard.CopyColumnHeaders = DevExpress.Utils.DefaultBoolean.True;
            gv.OptionsClipboard.ShowProgress = DevExpress.Export.ProgressMode.Never;
            gv.OptionsClipboard.AllowExcelFormat = DevExpress.Utils.DefaultBoolean.True;
            bool before = gv.OptionsSelection.MultiSelect;
            gv.OptionsSelection.MultiSelect = true;
            gv.SelectAll();
            gv.CopyToClipboard();
            if (alert)
                DevExpress.XtraEditors.XtraMessageBox.Show("Copied to Clipboard");
            gv.OptionsSelection.MultiSelect = before;


        }
        public static void ExportExcelQuick(GridView gv, bool show_in_folder,string basefilename = null)
        {
            string ext = ".xlsx";

            string name = "Excel Export " + DateTime.Now.ToString("m-d-yyyy HH.MM.ss") + ext;
            if (null != basefilename)
            {
                ext = Path.GetExtension(basefilename);
                name = basefilename;
            }
            string full_path = Path.Combine(Path.GetTempPath(), name);
            DevExpress.XtraPrinting.XlsxExportOptionsEx xls = new DevExpress.XtraPrinting.XlsxExportOptionsEx();
            gv.OptionsPrint.PrintDetails = true;

            GridView masterView = gv;
            masterView.OptionsDetail.DetailMode = DetailMode.Classic;

            int rowHandle = gv.FocusedRowHandle;
            masterView.ExpandMasterRow(rowHandle);
            ColumnView detailView = gv.GetDetailView(rowHandle, 0) as ColumnView;

            gv.ZoomView();
            xls.AllowSortingAndFiltering = DevExpress.Utils.DefaultBoolean.True;
            xls.ExportType = DevExpress.Export.ExportType.DataAware;
            xls.ShowGridLines = false;
            xls.AllowGrouping = DevExpress.Utils.DefaultBoolean.True;
            
            xls.BandedLayoutMode = DevExpress.Export.BandedLayoutMode.LinearColumns;
  
            
            
            
            
            

            
            
            
            
            if(ext.ToUpper().Contains(".XLSX"))
                gv.ExportToXlsx(full_path, xls);
            else if (ext.ToUpper().Contains(".CSV"))
                gv.ExportToCsv(full_path);


            if (show_in_folder)
            {
                UtilsLib.ProcessHelper.SpawnDirectoryWithFileSelect(full_path, false);

            }
            gv.NormalView();
            Process.Start(full_path);
        }



        public void ExportGridViewToExcel(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            ExportExcelQuick();
        }
    }
}
