--- FILE: DXHelper\LazyTableUpdater.cs ---
namespace DXHelper
{
    public class LazyTable
    {

        private string _lazy_update_table;
        private string _lazy_update_keys_csv;
        private string _server;
        private GridHelper _gc;
        private bool _check_if_exists;
        Dictionary<string, string> _column_remap;
        Dictionary<string, string> _next_ids_to_populate;
        List<string> _do_not_insert_update;

        public delegate void PreProcessRow(DataRow row);
        public delegate void PostProcessRow(DataRow row);

        public LazyTable(GridHelper gc, string server,string lazy_update_table, string lazy_update_keys_csv, bool check_if_exists, Dictionary<string,string> column_remap,List<string> do_not_insert_update)
        {
            _server = server;
            _gc = gc;
            _gc._view.RowUpdated += _view_RowUpdated;
            _gc._view.RowDeleted += _view_RowDeleted;
            _lazy_update_table = lazy_update_table;
            _lazy_update_keys_csv = lazy_update_keys_csv;
            _check_if_exists = check_if_exists;
            _column_remap = column_remap;
            _do_not_insert_update = do_not_insert_update;
        }

        private LazyTable.PreProcessRow _ppr;
        public void SetRowPreProcess(PreProcessRow ppr)
        {
            _ppr = ppr;
        }

        private LazyTable.PostProcessRow _ppr_post;
        public void SetRowPostProcess(PostProcessRow ppr_post)
        {
            _ppr_post = ppr_post;
        }

        public void SetNextIDPopulates(Dictionary<string,string> next_ids_to_populate)
        {
            _next_ids_to_populate = next_ids_to_populate;
        }

        public void SetDoNotInsertUpdate(List<string> do_not_insert_update)
        {
            _do_not_insert_update = do_not_insert_update;
        }

        List<string> _cols_to_return_on_insert;
        public void SetColumnsToReturnOnInsert(List<string> cols_to_return_on_insert)
        {
            _cols_to_return_on_insert = cols_to_return_on_insert;
        }
        private void _view_RowDeleted(object sender, DevExpress.Data.RowDeletedEventArgs e)
        {
            LazyTableHelper();
        }

        private void _view_RowUpdated(object sender, RowObjectEventArgs e)
        {
            LazyTableHelper();
        }
        public void ForceLazyUpdate(bool silent)
        {
            LazyTableHelper(silent);
        }
        public void LazyTableHelper(bool silent =false)
        {
            _gc.UpdateTableHelper(InsertUpdateTableGeneric, null, !silent);
        }

        private int InsertUpdateTableGeneric(DataRow row, List<DataColumn> cols_modified)
        {
            if (row.Table.Rows.Count != 1)
                throw new Exception("Should never happen");

            if (null != _column_remap)
            {
                foreach (KeyValuePair<string, string> kvp in _column_remap)
                {
                    if (row.Table.Columns.Contains(kvp.Key))
                        row.Table.Columns[kvp.Key].Rename(kvp.Value);
                }
            }


            if (null != _ppr)
                _ppr(row);

            DataTable values = row.Table.CopyAndTrimColumns(cols_modified);
            DataTable keys = row.Table.CopyAndTrimColumns(_lazy_update_keys_csv);
            
            
            

            if (null != _do_not_insert_update)
            {
                foreach (string col in _do_not_insert_update)
                {
                    if (values.Columns.Contains(col))
                        values.Columns.Remove(col);
                }
            }
            
            var results = Database.DBUtils.LazyTableUpdater(_server, _lazy_update_table, keys.Columns.ToList(), values, _check_if_exists, _next_ids_to_populate, _cols_to_return_on_insert);

            if(null != _cols_to_return_on_insert && null != results.results && _cols_to_return_on_insert.Count == values.Rows.Count)
            {
                foreach(DataRow new_row in results.results.Rows)
                {
                    foreach(string col in _cols_to_return_on_insert)
                    {
                        if (row.Table.Columns.ContainsIns(col))
                        {
                            row[col] = new_row[col]; 
                        }
                    }
                }
            }

            if (null != _ppr_post)
                _ppr_post(row);

            return 1;
        }
    }
}

        public static void SetupBiggerRepositoryEditor(this GridView gv, string columnName)
        {
            RepositoryItemMemoExEdit me = new RepositoryItemMemoExEdit();
            me.WordWrap = true;
            me.ValidateOnEnterKey = true;
            me.ShowIcon = false;
            me.PopupFormMinSize = new Size(700, 0);
            me.AcceptsTab = true;
            me.AcceptsReturn = false;
            gv.Columns[columnName].ColumnEdit = me;
        }


      
        public static void PopulateGridLookup(this DevExpress.XtraEditors.Repository.RepositoryItemLookUpEdit li, DataTable t, string display_member, string value_member)
        {
            PopulateGridLookup(li, t, display_member, value_member, null);
        }

        public static void PopulateGridLookup(this DevExpress.XtraEditors.Repository.RepositoryItemLookUpEdit li, DataTable t, string display_member, string value_member, string[] visible_columns)
        {
            li.DataSource = t;
            li.ValueMember = value_member;
            li.DisplayMember = display_member;
            li.ForceInitialize();
            li.PopulateColumns();
            li.NullText = null;
            List<string> all_visible = new List<string>(new string[] { display_member });
            if (null != visible_columns)
                all_visible.AddRange(visible_columns);
            li.Columns.HideAllExcept(all_visible);
            li.KeyDown += Li_KeyDown;

        }

        private static void Li_KeyDown(object sender, System.Windows.Forms.KeyEventArgs e)
        {
            if (e.KeyCode == Keys.Delete)
                (sender as LookUpEdit).EditValue = null;
        }

        public static void PopulateGridViewLookup(this GridLookUpEdit li, DataTable t, string display_member, string value_member, string[] visible_columns)
        {
            li.Properties.DataSource = t;
            li.Properties.ValueMember = value_member;
            li.Properties.DisplayMember = display_member;
            li.Properties.PopulateViewColumns();
            List<string> all_visible = new List<string>(new string[] { display_member });
            if (null != visible_columns)
                all_visible.AddRange(visible_columns);
            foreach (GridColumn col in li.Properties.View.Columns)
            {
                if (!all_visible.Contains(col.FieldName))
                    col.Visible = false;
            }

            li.Properties.View.BestFitColumns();


            
        }
        public static void HideAllExcept(this LookUpColumnInfoCollection lcc, string visible)
        {
            HideAllExcept(lcc, new string[] { visible });
        }
        public static void HideAllExcept(this LookUpColumnInfoCollection lcc, IEnumerable<string> csv_of_visible)
        {
            foreach (LookUpColumnInfo c in lcc)
            {
                if (!csv_of_visible.Contains(c.FieldName))
                    c.Visible = false;
                else
                    c.Caption = c.Caption.TitleCase();
                
                
                
                
                
                
            }
        }
        public static void PopulateLookup(this DevExpress.XtraEditors.LookUpEdit li, DataTable t, string display_member, string value_member, bool default_first_row = false)
        {
            PopulateLookup(li, t, new string[] { display_member }, value_member, default_first_row, null, null);
        }

        
        public static void DisableIfEditNull(this DevExpress.XtraEditors.LookUpEdit li, EventHandler eh)
        {
            li.EditValueChanged += eh;
        }




        private static void Li_EditValueChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            throw new NotImplementedException();
        }


        public static void PopulateLookup(this DevExpress.XtraEditors.LookUpEdit li, DataTable t, string[] display_member, string value_member, bool default_first_row = false, Nullable<int> width = null, bool? allow_null_input = null, string default_column_to_search = null, object default_value_to_search_for = null, bool show_header = false)
        {
            if (li.InvokeRequired)
            {
                li.Invoke(new MethodInvoker(() => { PopulateLookupInternal(li,t,display_member,value_member,default_first_row); }));
            }
            else
            {
                PopulateLookupInternal(li, t, display_member, value_member, default_first_row);
            }
        }
        public static void PopulateLookupInternal(this DevExpress.XtraEditors.LookUpEdit li, DataTable t, string[] display_member, string value_member, bool default_first_row = false, Nullable<int> width = null, bool? allow_null_input = null, string default_column_to_search = null, object default_value_to_search_for = null, bool show_header = false)
        {
            li.Properties.DataSource = t;
            li.Properties.DisplayMember = display_member[0];
            li.Properties.ValueMember = value_member;
            if (null != allow_null_input)
            {
                li.Properties.AllowNullInput = (allow_null_input.Value == true)
                    ? DevExpress.Utils.DefaultBoolean.True
                    : DevExpress.Utils.DefaultBoolean.False;
            }

            
            
            li.Properties.ForceInitialize();
            li.Properties.PopulateColumns();

            li.Properties.ShowHeader = show_header;

            
            if (display_member[0] != value_member)
                li.Properties.Columns.HideAllExcept(display_member);

            if (null != width)
                li.Properties.PopupWidth = width.Value;

            if (null != default_column_to_search && t.Columns.Contains(default_column_to_search))
            {
                DataRow[] rows = t.Select($"{default_column_to_search} = '{default_value_to_search_for}'");
                if (rows.Length == 1)
                {
                    object single = rows[0][value_member];
                    if (li.EditValue != single)
                        li.EditValue = single;
                }

            }
            else if (default_first_row && null != t && t.Rows.Count > 0)
            {
                if (li.EditValue != t.Rows[0][value_member])
                    li.EditValue = t.Rows[0][value_member];
            }
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            

            li.KeyDown += Li_KeyDown1;
        }

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        private static void Li_KeyDown1(object sender, KeyEventArgs e)
        {
            LookUpEdit le = (sender as LookUpEdit);
            if (e.KeyCode == Keys.Delete && le.Properties.AllowNullInput == DevExpress.Utils.DefaultBoolean.True)
                le.EditValue = null;
        }
    }
}

--- FILE: DXHelper\ProgressBar.cs ---
namespace DXHelper
{
    public class DXETA : UtilsLib.ETA
    {
        private ProgressBarControl _pbc = new ProgressBarControl();
        Control _c;
        public DXETA(int total, IWriter writer, System.Windows.Forms.Control c) : base(total, writer)
        {
            Init(total, writer, c);
            if(null == writer)
            {
                base.SetWriter(SetBar);
            }
        }


        private bool _lock_form = false;
        public void SetLock(bool lock_form)
        {
            _lock_form = lock_form;
        }

        private void Init(int total, IWriter writer, System.Windows.Forms.Control c)
        {
            

            if (null != c)
            {
                _c = c;
                if (c.InvokeRequired)
                {
                    c.Invoke(new MethodInvoker(() => { Init(total, writer, c); }));
                }
            }
            

            _pbc = new ProgressBarControl();
            _pbc.Parent = c;
            _pbc.CustomDisplayText += _pbc_CustomDisplayText;

            _pbc.Properties.Appearance.Font = new Font(_pbc.Properties.Appearance.Font, FontStyle.Bold);
            _pbc.Properties.Step = 1;
            _pbc.Properties.Minimum = 0;
            _pbc.Properties.Maximum = total;
            _pbc.Properties.PercentView = true;
            _pbc.ShowProgressInTaskBar = true;
            _pbc.VisibleSafe(true);
            _pbc.Properties.ShowTitle = true;
            _pbc.Dock = System.Windows.Forms.DockStyle.Bottom;
            
            _pbc.Update();
        }



        public void Hide()
        {
            _pbc.VisibleSafe(false);
            _pbc.HideSafe();
            _pbc.ShowProgressInTaskBarSafe(false);
            
            base.Complete();
            if (_lock_form)
            {
                Wait.CloseWaitingPopupIfItIsCurrentlyOpen();
            }
            _pbc.DisposeSafe();
        }

        private string last_write_string;
        public void SetBar(string txt)
        {
            last_write_string = txt;
        }

        private void _pbc_CustomDisplayText(object sender, DevExpress.XtraEditors.Controls.CustomDisplayTextEventArgs e)
        {
            e.DisplayText = last_write_string;
        }

  

        private void SetupControl()
        {
            if (null != _parent && _parent.InvokeRequired)
            {
                _parent.Invoke(new MethodInvoker(() => { SetupControl(); }));
            }
            else
            {
                if(_pbc.IsDisposed)
                {
                    _pbc = new ProgressBarControl();
                    _pbc.Parent = _c;
                }
                _pbc.VisibleSafe(true);
                _pbc.Show();
                _pbc.CreateControlSafe();
            }
        }
        public override void IncrementAndReport(Nullable<int> work_done = 1)
        {
            if (_pbc.Visible == false)
            {
                
                
                
                SetupControl();
            }
            if (null != _pbc.Parent && _lock_form && _pbc.Parent.Enabled)
            {
                Wait.ShowWaitingPopup(_pbc.Parent);
                _pbc.Enabled = false;
            }
            _pbc.IncrementSafe(work_done.Value);
            

            _pbc.UpdateSafe();
            base.IncrementAndReport(work_done);

        }



        public override void SetTotal(int total)
        {
            _pbc.Properties.Maximum = total;
            base.SetTotal(total);
        }
        public void SetParent(System.Windows.Forms.Control ctrl)
        {
            _pbc.Parent = ctrl;
            _pbc.Update();
        }
        public override void Complete()
        {
            Hide();
        }
    }
}

using static DXHelper.QuickSearch;

namespace DXHelper
{
    public class QuickSearch
    {

        CommonInterfaces.Delegates.NewAssetSelected _nas = null;
        DXHelper.Forms.QuickView f = new DXHelper.Forms.QuickView();

   

        public void SpawnQuickSearch(string server, DataTable tbl, string csv_cols, string search_text, IWin32Window owner, CommonInterfaces.Delegates.NewAssetSelected nas, bool async = false, Query refresh_query = null)
        {
            
            f.Init(server,null);
            f.Populate(tbl, csv_cols);
            f.ToggleAutoFilterRow(true);
            _nas = nas;
            f.SetRefreshQuery(refresh_query);
            f.Show(owner);
            f.Hide();
            f.Grid.ToggleSearchPanel(true);
            f.Grid.SetDoubleClickAction(DoubleClickAsset);
            f.ShowFindPanel();
            f.SetFindFilterText(search_text);

            if (async)
                f.Show();
            else
                f.ShowDialog(owner);

            if (null != _po)
                _po(f.Grid);
            
            
            
            
            
                
            
        }


        
        


        private bool _autoExecuteDelegate = false;
        public void SetExecuteDelegateOnSingleItemFilter(bool execute)
        {
            _autoExecuteDelegate = execute;
        }

        public GridHelper Grid
        {
            get { return f.Grid; }
        }

        public delegate void PostOpenEvent(GridHelper gh);
        PostOpenEvent _po;
        public void SetPostOpenEvent(PostOpenEvent po)
        {
            _po = po;
        }
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        public void ToggleColumnAutoWidth(bool enable)
        {
            f.ToggleColumnAutoWidth(enable);
        }
        public void SetTitle(string title)
        {
            f.Text = title;
        }
        public void ShowFooter(bool show)
        {
            f.ToggleFooter(show);
        }
        public void SetSumColumns(string csv)
        {
            f.AddSumsFooters(csv);
        }
        private void DoubleClickAsset(GridView view, GridHitInfo info)
        {
            if (null == info.Column)
                return;
            string clicked = info.Column.FieldName.ToLower();
            if (null != clicked && view.Columns.ContainsColumn("asset_id"))
            {
                string asset_id = f.Grid.GetActiveRowValue<string>("asset_id", false);
                f.Close();
                if (null != _nas)
                    _nas(asset_id);
                
            }
        }

    }

--- FILE: DXHelper\TabControl.cs ---
namespace DXHelper
{
    public static class TabControl
    {
        public static int GetTabIndex(this NavigationPageBaseCollection tabs, string tabName)
        {
            int i = 0;
            foreach(var v in tabs)
            {
                if (v.Name == tabName)
                    return i;
                i++;
            }
            return -1;
        }
    }
}

namespace DXHelper
{
    public class Wait
    {
        
        
        
        
        
        public static void ShowWaitingPopup(Form parentForm)
        {
            
            SplashScreenManager.ShowDefaultWaitForm(parentForm, true, true, null, null);
        }

        public static void ShowWaitingPopup(Control parentForm)
        {
            
            Form f = parentForm.FindForm();
            SplashScreenManager.ShowDefaultWaitForm(f, true, true, null, null);
        }


        public static void ShowWaitingPopup()
        {
            SplashScreenManager.ShowDefaultWaitForm(null, true, true, null, null);
        }
        public static void CloseWaitingPopupIfItIsCurrentlyOpen()
        {

            
            {
                try
                {
                   if(null != SplashScreenManager.Default)
                        SplashScreenManager.CloseDefaultWaitForm();
                }
                catch (System.InvalidOperationException e)
                {

                    

                    
                }
            }
        }
    }

namespace The_Toolbox.Controls
{
    public partial class ctrlGeneral : DevExpress.XtraEditors.XtraUserControl
    {
        public ctrlGeneral()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        private void btnGenerateDocument_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            WordLib w = new WordLib();
            string file = @"C:\temp\test.DOCX";
            string new_file_base = @"C:\temp\testMerged";
            string new_file_word = new_file_base + ".docx";
            string new_file_pdf = new_file_base + ".pdf";

            w.OpenFile(file);

            DataTable map = GetDataHack();

            Dictionary<string, string> merges = map.Rows[0].ToDictionary<string>();

            w.MergeFields(merges);
            string unused = w.ClearAllMergeFields();
            w.SaveAs(new_file_word, true);
            w.SaveAsPDF(new_file_pdf, true);
            w.Close(false);
            w.Exit(false);
            var answer = XtraMessageBox.Show("Missing Fields:\n\n" + unused, "DONE!  View?", MessageBoxButtons.YesNo);

            if (answer == DialogResult.Yes)
            {
                UtilsLib.ProcessHelper.RunAsync(new_file_pdf);
            }

        }

        public DataTable GetDataHack()
        {
            DataTable tbl = new DataTable();

            tbl.Columns.Add("SubscriberName");
            tbl.Columns.Add("CapitalContribution");
            tbl.Columns.Add("Units");
            tbl.Columns.Add("SubscriberAddress");
            tbl.Columns.Add("SubscriberPhone");
            tbl.Columns.Add("SubscriberFax");
            tbl.Columns.Add("SubscriberEMail");
            tbl.Columns.Add("SubscriberDOB");
            tbl.Columns.Add("SubscriberOccupation");
            tbl.Columns.Add("SubscriberEmployer");
            tbl.Columns.Add("SubscriberAllowDebitYN");
            tbl.Columns.Add("QuarterlyReturnsYN");
            tbl.Columns.Add("JointName");
            tbl.Columns.Add("JointAddress");
            tbl.Columns.Add("JointPhoneNumber");
            tbl.Columns.Add("JointFax");
            tbl.Columns.Add("TrustName");
            tbl.Columns.Add("TrustTitle");
            tbl.Columns.Add("TrustAddress");
            tbl.Columns.Add("TrustPhoneNumber");
            tbl.Columns.Add("TrustFaxNumber");


            DataRow row = tbl.Rows.Add();
            row["SubscriberName"] = "Dan Foster";
            row["CapitalContribution"] = 100000;
            row["Units"] = row["CapitalContribution"];

            return tbl;

        }

        private void btnConnectDatabase_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            string sql = "select * From authorizedemails a";
            Query q = new Query(sql, CommonInterfaces.Constants.Database.SALUDA_MYSQL_SERVER);
            DataTable t = q.ExecuteTable();
            _grid.SetGrid(t);
        }

        private GridHelper _grid;
        private void ctrlGeneral_Load(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

            _grid = new GridHelper(mainGrid, CommonInterfaces.Constants.Database.SALUDA_MYSQL_SERVER, false);
        }
    }
}
